Over in a little path in the meadow grass be walk old Mr. Meadow Mouse .
He be stroll along a if there be nothing in the world to fear .
Way back behind him in the same little path , walk very fast but very quietly , be big Mr. Bob Cat .
His eye be yellow , and a hungry look be in them .
He do n't see Mr. Meadow Mouse , but he would in a few minute .
Mr. Chipmunk saw that he would , and that there be no place for Mr. Meadow Mouse to hide . ''
` Humph !
I never meddle in other people 's affair , and this be none of my business , ' say little Mr. Chipmunk .
`` But old Mr. Meadow Mouse be a friend .
He think a great deal of Mr. Meadow Mouse , do little Mr. Chipmunk .
He could n't bear to think of what would happen to Mr. Meadow Mouse if big Mr. Bob Cat should catch him .
Then , almost without realize what he be do , little Mr. Chipmunk begin to shout at big Mr. Bob Cat and to call him names .
Of course big Mr. Bob Cat look up right away and saw little Mr. Chipmunk sit on the old stump .
His eye grow yellow and yellow , he draw his lip back from his long , sharp teeth in a very angry way , and his little bob tail twitch and twitch .
Then , with great leap , he come straight for the old stump on which little Mr. Chipmunk be sit .
`` Little Mr. Chipmunk do n't wait for him to get there .
Oh , my , no !
He take one good look at those fierce , hungry , yellow eye and long , cruel teeth , and then he whisk into a hole in the old stump .
You see , there be n't time to go anywhere else .
Big Mr. Bob Cat find the hole in the stump right away .
He snarl when he saw it .
You see it be too small , very much too small , for him to get into himself .
But he could get one hand and arm in , and he do , feel all around inside for little Mr. Chipmunk .
Little Mr. Chipmunk be frighten almost to death .
Yes , Sir , he be frighten almost to death .
He make himself just as flat a he could on the bottom of the hollow and hold his breath . ''
` You 'd better come out of there , Mr. Chipmunk , or I 'll pull you out ! '
snarl Mr. Bob Cat .
`` Little Mr. Chipmunk just snuggle down flatter than ever and do n't say a word .
Mr. Bob Cat felt round and round inside the hollow stump and rake his long claw on the side until little Mr. Chipmunk 's hair fairly stand up .
Yes , Sir , it stand right up on end , he be so scared .
When it do that , it tickle the claw of Mr. Bob Cat .
Mr. Bob Cat grin .
It be an ugly grin to see .
Then he reach in a little farther and make a grab for little Mr. Chipmunk .
His wide-spread , sharp claw catch in little Mr. Chipmunk 's coat near the neck and tore little strip the whole length of it .
`` Of course little Mr. Chipmunk squeal with pain , for those claws hurt dreadfully , but he be glad that his coat tore .
If it have n't , Mr. Bob Cat would surely have pull him out .
After a long time , Mr. Bob Cat give up and go off , growl and snarl .
When he think it be safe , little Mr. Chipmunk crawl out of the old stump and hurry home .
He ache and smart terribly , and his little plain brown coat be tear in long strip . ''
` This be what I get for meddling in the affair of other folk ! '
say little Mr. Chipmunk bitterly .
` If I 'd just mind my own business , it would n't have happen . '
`` Just then he happen to look over to the house of Mr. Meadow Mouse .
There be Mr. Meadow Mouse play with his child .
He do n't know a thing about what his neighbor , little Mr. Chipmunk , have do for him , for you remember he have n't see Mr. Bob Cat at all .
Little Mr. Chipmunk grin as well a he could for the pain . ''
` I 'm glad I do it , ' he mutter .
` Yes , Sir , I 'm glad I do it , and I 'm glad that Neighbor Meadow Mouse do n't know about it .
I 'm glad that nobody know about it . '
A kindly deed 's most kindly do In secret wrought , and see of none .
And so I 'm glad that no one know . '
`` Now just imagine how surprised little Mr. Chipmunk be , when in the fall it come time to put on a new coat , to have Old Mother Nature hand him out a beautiful strip coat instead of the little plain brown coat he have expect .
Old Mother Nature 's eye twinkle a she say : '' ` There 's a stripe for every tear make in your old coat by the claw of Mr. Bob Cat the day you save Mr. Meadow Mouse .
They be honor stripe , and hereafter you and your child and your child 's child shall always wear stripe . '
`` And that be how it happen that Striped Chipmunk come by his striped coat , and why he be so proud of it , and take such good care of it , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
II WHY PETER RABBIT CAN NOT FOLD HIS HANDS Happy Jack Squirrel sit with his hand fold across his white waistcoat .
He be very fond of sit with his hand fold that way .
A little way from him sit Peter Rabbit .
Peter be sit up very straight , but his hand drop right down in front .
Happy Jack notice it .
`` Why do n't you fold your hand the way I do , Peter Rabbit ? ''
shout Happy Jack .
`` I -- I -- do n't want to , '' stammer Peter .
`` You mean you ca n't ! ''
jeer Happy Jack .
Peter pretend not to hear , and a few minute later he hop away towards the dear Old Briar-patch , lipperty-lipperty-lip .
Happy Jack watch him go , and there be a puzzled look in Happy Jack 's eye .
`` I really believe he ca n't fold his hand , '' say Happy Jack to himself , but speak aloud .
`` He ca n't , and none of his family can , '' say a gruff voice .
Happy Jack turn to find Old Mr. Toad sit in the Lone Little Path .
`` Why not ? ''
ask Happy Jack .
`` Ask Grandfather Frog ; he know , '' reply Old Mr. Toad , and start on about his business .
And this be how it happen that Grandfather Frog tell this story to the little meadow and forest people gather around him on the bank of the Smiling Pool .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog .
`` Old Mr. Rabbit , the grandfather a thousand time remove of Peter Rabbit , be always get into trouble .
Yes , Sir , old Mr. Rabbit be always get into trouble .
Seemed like he would n't be happy if he could n't get into trouble .
It be all because he be so dreadfully curious about other people 's business , just a Peter Rabbit be now .
It seem that he be just bear to be curious and so , of course , to get into trouble .
`` One day word come to the Green Forest and to the Green Meadows that Old Mother Nature be come to see how all the little meadow and forest people be get along , to settle all the little trouble and fuss between them , and to find out who be and who be not obey the order she have give them when she have visit them last .
My , my , my , such a hurrying and scurrying and worrying a there be !
You see , everybody want to look his best when Old Mother Nature arrive , Yes , Sir , everybody want to look his best .
`` There be the great changing of clothes you ever do see .
Old King Bear put on his black coat .
Mr. Coon and Mr. Mink and Mr . Otter sit up half the night brush their suit and make them look a fine and handsome a they could .
Even Old Mr. Toad put on a new suit under his old one , and plan to pull the old one off and throw it away as soon a Old Mother Nature should arrive .
Then everybody begin to fix up their home and make them a neat and nice a they know how -- everybody but Mr. Rabbit .
`` Now Mr. Rabbit be lazy .
He do n't like to work any more than Peter Rabbit do now .
No , Sir , old Mr. Rabbit be afraid of work .
The very sight of work scar old Mr. Rabbit .
You see , he be so busy mind other people 's business that he do n't have time to attend to his own .
So his brown and gray coat always be rumple and tumble and dirty .
His house be a tumble-down affair in which no one but Mr. Rabbit would ever have think of living , and his garden -- oh , dear me , such a garden you never do see !
It be all weed and bramble .
They fill up the yard , and old Mr. Rabbit actually could n't have get into his own house if he have n't cut a path through the bramble .
`` Now when old Mr. Rabbit hear that Old Mother Nature be come , his heart sink way , way down , for he know just how angry she would be when she saw his house , his garden and his shabby suit . ''
` Oh , dear !
Oh , dear !
What shall I do ? '
wail Mr. Rabbit , wring his hand . ''
` Get busy and clean up , ' advise Mr. Woodchuck , hurry about his own work .
`` Now Mr. Woodchuck be a worker and very , very neat .
He mean to have his home look just as fine a he could make it .
He bring up some clean yellow sand from deep down in the ground and sprinkle it smoothly over his doorstep . ''
` I 'll help you , if I get through my own work in time , ' shout Mr. Woodchuck over his shoulder .
`` That give Mr. Rabbit an idea .
He would ask all his neighbor to help him , and perhaps then he could get his house and garden in order by the time Old Mother Nature arrive .
So Mr. Rabbit call on Mr . Skunk and Mr. Coon and Mr. Mink and Mr. Squirrel and Mr. Chipmunk , and all the rest of his neighbor , tell them of his trouble and ask them to help .
Now , in spite of the trouble Mr. Rabbit be forever make for other people by his dreadful curiosity and meddling with other people 's affair , all his neighbor have a warm place in their heart for Mr. Rabbit , and they all promise that they would help him as soon a they have their own work finish .
`` Instead of hurry home and get to work himself , Mr. Rabbit stop a while after each call and sat with his arm fold , watch the one he be call on work .
Mr. Rabbit be very fond of sit with folded arm .
It be very comfortable .
But this be no time to be do it , and Mr . Skunk tell him so . ''
` If you want the rest of u to help you , you 'd better get thing start yourself , ' say old Mr . Skunk , carefully comb out his big , plumy tail . ''
` That 's right , Mr . Skunk !
That 's right ! '
say Mr. Rabbit , start along briskly , just a if he be go to hurry right home and begin work that very instant .
`` But half an hour later , when Mr . Skunk happen to pass the home of Mr. Chipmunk , there sit Mr. Rabbit with his arm fold , watch Mr. Chipmunk hurry about a only Mr. Chipmunk can .
`` Finally Mr. Rabbit have make the round of all his friend and neighbor , and he once more reach his tumble-down house .
` Oh , dear , ' sigh Mr. Rabbit , a he look at the tangle of bramble which almost hide the little old house , ' I never , never can clear away all this !
It will be a lot easy to work when all my friend be here to help , ' So he sigh once more and fold his arm , instead of begin work a he should have do .
And then , because the sun be bright and warm , and he be very , very comfortable , old Mr. Rabbit begin to nod , and presently he be fast asleep .
`` Now Old Mother Nature like to take people by surprise , and it happen that she choose this very day to make her promised visit .
She be greatly pleased with all she saw a she go along , until she come to the home of Mr. Rabbit . ''
` Mercy me ! '
exclaim Old Mother Nature , throw up her hand a she saw the tumble-down house almost hide by the bramble and weed .
` Can it be possible that any one really live here ? '
Then , peer through the tangle of bramble , she spy old Mr. Rabbit sit on his broken-down doorstep with his arm fold and fast asleep .
`` At first she be very indignant , oh , very indignant , indeed !
She decide that Mr. Rabbit should be punish very severely .
But a she watch him sit there , dream in the warm sunshine , her anger begin to melt away .
The fact be , Old Mother Nature be like all the rest of Mr. Rabbit 's neighbor -- she just could n't help love happy-go-lucky Mr. Rabbit in spite of all his fault .
With a long stick she reach in and tickle the end of his nose .
`` Mr. Rabbit sneeze , and this make him wake up .
He yawn and blink , and then his eye suddenly fly wide open with fright .
He have discover Old Mother Nature frown at him .
She point a long forefinger at him and say : ` In every single bless day There 's time for work and time for play .
Who fold his arm with work undone Doth cheat himself and spoil his fun . ' ''
` Hereafter , Mr. Rabbit , you and your child and your child 's child will never again be able to sit with folded arm until you or they have learn to work . '
`` And that be why Peter Rabbit can not fold his arm and still live in a tumble-down house among the bramble , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
III WHY UNC ' BILLY POSSUM PLAYS DEAD One thing puzzle Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck and Striped Chipmunk a great deal after they have come to know Unc ' Billy Possum and his funny way .
They have talk it over and wonder and wonder about it , and try to understand it , and even have ask Unc ' Billy about it .
Unc ' Billy have just grin and say that they would have to ask his mammy .
Of course they could n't do that , and Unc ' Billy know they could n't , for Unc ' Billy 's mammy have die long before he even think of come up from Ol ' Virginny to the Green Forest and the Green Meadows where they live .
He say it just to tease them , and when he say it , he chuckle until they chuckle too , just a if it really be the best kind of a joke .
Now you know it always be the thing that you try and try to find out and ca n't find out that you most want to find out .
It be just so with Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck and Striped Chipmunk .
The more they talk about it , the more they want to know .
Why be it that Unc ' Billy Possum play dead instead of try to run away when he be surprise by his enemy ?
They always try to run away .
So do everybody else of their acquaintance except Unc ' Billy Possum .
`` There must be a reason '' say Peter gravely , a he pull thoughtfully at one of his long ear .
`` Of course there be a reason , '' assert Johnny Chuck , chew the end of a blade of grass .
`` There 's a reason for everything , '' add Striped Chipmunk , comb out the hair of his funny little tail .
`` Then of course Grandfather Frog know it , '' say Peter .
`` Of course !
Why do n't we think of him before ? ''
exclaim the others .
`` I 'll beat you to the Smiling Pool ! ''
shout Peter .
Of course he do , for his leg be long and make for run , but Striped Chipmunk be not far behind .
Johnny Chuck take his time , for he know that he could not keep up with the others .
Besides he be so fat that to run make him puff and blow .
Grandfather Frog sit just as usual on his big green lily-pad , and he grin when he saw who his visitor be , for he guess right away what they have come for .
`` Chug-a-rum !
What be it you want to know now ? ''
he demand , before Peter could fairly get his breath .
`` If you please , Grandfather Frog , we want to know why it be that Unc ' Billy Possum play dead , '' reply Peter as politely a he know how .
Grandfather Frog chuckle .
`` Just to fool people , stupid ! ''
say he .
`` Of course we know that , '' reply Striped Chipmunk , `` but what we want to know be how he ever find out that he could fool people that way , and how he know that he will fool them . ''
`` I suspect that his mammy teach him , '' say Grandfather Frog , with another chuckle way down deep in his throat .
`` But who teach his mammy ? ''
persist Striped Chipmunk .
Grandfather Frog snap at a foolish green fly , and when it be safely tuck away inside his white and yellow waistcoat , he turn once more to his three little visitor , and there be a twinkle in his big , goggly eye .
`` I see , '' say he , `` that you will have a story , and I suppose that the sooner I tell it to you , the sooner you will leave me in peace .
Unc ' Billy Possum 's grandfather a thousand time remove be -- '' `` Was this way back in the day when the world be young ? ''
interrupt Peter .
Grandfather Frog scowl at Peter .
`` If I have any more interruption , there will be no story to-day '' say he severely .
Peter look ashamed and promise that he would hold his tongue right between his teeth until Grandfather Frog be through .
Grandfather Frog clear his throat and begin again .
`` Unc ' Billy Possum 's grandfather a thousand time remove be very much a Unc ' Billy be now , only he be a little more spry and know good than to stuff himself so full that he could n't run .
He be always very sly , and he play a great many trick on his neighbor , and sometimes he get them into trouble .
But when he do , he always manage to keep out of their way until they have forget all about their anger .
`` One morning the very imp of mischief seem to get into old Mr. Possum 's head .
Yes , Sir , it certainly do seem that way .
And when you see Mischief trot along the Lone Little Path , if you look sharp enough , you 'll see Trouble follow at his heel like a shadow .
I never know it to fail .
It 's just as sure a a stomach-ache be to follow overeating . ''
Just here Grandfather Frog pause and look very hard at Peter Rabbit .
But Peter pretend not to notice , and after slowly wink one of his big , goggly eye at Johnny Chuck , Grandfather Frog continue : `` Anyway , a I say before , the imp of mischief seem to be in old Mr. Possum 's head that morning , for he begin to play trick on his neighbor as soon a they be out of bed .
He hide Old King Bear 's breakfast , while the latter have his head turn , and then pretend that he have just come along .
He be very polite and offer to help Old King Bear hunt for his lose breakfast .
Then , whenever Old King Bear come near the place where it be hide , old Mr. Possum would hide it somewhere else .
Old King Bear be hungry , and he work himself up into a terrible rage , for he be in a hurry for his breakfast .
Old Mr. Possum be very sympathetic and seem to be do his very best to find the lost meal .
At last Old King Bear turn his head suddenly and catch sight of old Mr. Possum hide that breakfast in a new place .
My , my , but his temper do boil over !
It certainly do .
And if he could have lay hand on old Mr. Possum that minute , it surely would have be the end of him .
`` But old Mr. Possum be mighty spry , and he go off through the Green Forest laugh fit to kill himself .
Pretty soon he meet Mr. Panther .
He be very polite to Mr. Panther .
He tell him that he have just come from a call on Old King Bear , and hint that Old King Bear be then enjoy a feast and that there might be enough for Mr. Panther , if he hurry up there at once .
`` Now , Mr. Panther be hungry , for he have find nothing for his breakfast that morning .
So he thank old Mr. Possum and hurry away to find Old King Bear and share in the good thing old Mr. Possum have tell about .
`` Old Mr. Possum himself hurry on , chuckle a he think of the way Mr. Panther be likely to be receive , with Old King Bear in such a temper .
Pretty soon along come Mr. Lynx .
Old Mr. Possum tell him the same story he have tell Mr. Panther , and Mr. Lynx go bound off in a terrible hurry , for fear that he would not be in time to share in that good breakfast .
It be such a good joke that old Mr. Possum try it on Mr. Wolf and Mr. Fisher and Mr. Fox .
In fact , he hunt up every one he could think of and send them to call on Old King Bear , and without really tell them so , he make each one think that he would get a share in that breakfast . ''
`` Now , there be n't any more breakfast than Old King Bear want himself , and by the time Mr. Panther arrive , there be n't so much a a crumb left .
Then , one after another , the others come drop in , each lick his chop , and all very polite to Old King Bear .
At first he do n't know what to make of it , but pretty soon Mr. Fox delicately hint that they have come in response to the invitation send by Mr. Possum , and that a they be all very hungry , they would like to know when the feast would be ready .
Right away Old King Bear know that old Mr. Possum have be up to some of his trick , and he tell his visitor that they be the victim of a practical joke .
-LSB- Illustration : `` As they be all very hungry , they would like to know when the feast would be ready . '' -RSB-
`` My , my , my , how angry everybody grow !
With Old King Bear at their head , they start out to hunt for old Mr. Possum .
When he saw them come , he realize that what he have think be a joke have become no longer a laughing matter for him .
He be too frighten to run , so he scramble up a tree .
He quite forget that Mr. Panther and Mr. Lynx could climb just as fast a he .
Up the tree after him they scramble , and he creep a far out a he could get on one of the branch .
Mr. Panther do n't dare go out there , so he just shake the branch .
He shake and shook and shook and shook , and the first thing old Mr. Possum know , he be fly through the air down to where the others be all ready to pounce on him .
`` Old Mr. Possum be frighten almost to death .
He shut his eye , and then he land with a thump that knock all the wind from his body .
When he get his breath again , he still keep his eye close , for he could n't bear the thought of look at the cruel teeth and claw of Old King Bear and the others .
Presently , while he be wonder why they do n't jump on him and tear him to piece , Old King Bear speak : '' ' I guess Mr. Possum wo n't play any more joke , Mr. Panther , ' say he .
` You just knock the life out of him when you shake him off that branch . '
`` Mr. Panther come over and sniff at Mr. Possum and turn him over with one paw .
All the time Mr. Possum lay just a if he be dead , because he be too frighten to move . '
I do n't mean to kill him , ' say Mr. Panther .
` We certainly will miss him .
What will we do with him ? ' ''
` Leave him here a a warning to others , ' growl Old King Bear .
`` Each in turn come up and sniffed of Mr. Possum , and then they all go about their business .
He wait long enough to make sure that they be out of sight , and then take the short way home .
When he get there and think it all over , he think that the best joke of all be the way he have make everybody think that he be dead .
And then a bright idea strike him : he would try the same trick whenever he be catch .
So the next time he get in trouble , instead of run away , he try play dead .
It be such a success that he teach his child how to do it , and they teach their child , and so on down to Unc ' Billy , whom you know .
Unc ' Billy say it be a lot easy than run away , and safer , too .
Besides , it be always such a joke .
Now , do n't bother me any more , for I want to take a nap , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
`` Thank you ! ''
cry Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck and Striped Chipmunk , and start off to hunt up Unc ' Billy Possum .
IV WHY REDDY FOX WEARS RED Peter Rabbit sit in the middle of the dear Old Briar-patch making face and laugh at Reddy Fox .
Of course that be n't a nice thing to do , not a bit nice .
But Peter have just have a narrow escape , a very narrow escape , for Reddy Fox have spring out from behind a bush a Peter come down the Lone Little Path , and have so nearly caught Peter that he have actually pull some fur out of Peter 's coat .
Now Peter be safe in the dear Old Briar-patch .
He be a little out of breath , because he have have to use his long leg as fast a he know how , but he be safe .
You see , Reddy Fox would n't run the risk of tear his handsome red coat on the bramble .
Besides , they scratch terribly .
`` Never mind , Peter Rabbit , I 'll get you yet ! ''
snarl Reddy , a he give up and start back for the Green Forest .
`` Reddy Fox be very sly !
Reddy Fox be very spry !
But sly and spry , 't be vain to try To be a sly and spry a I. '' When Peter Rabbit shout this , Reddy look back and show all his teeth , but Peter only laugh , and Reddy trot on .
Peter watch him out of sight .
`` My !
I wish I have such a handsome coat , '' he say , with a long sigh , for you know Peter 's coat be very plain , very plain , indeed .
`` You would n't , if you have to wear it for the same reason that Reddy Fox have to wear his .
A good heart and honest way be good than fine clothes , Peter Rabbit . ''
Peter look up .
There be saucy , pert , little Jenny Wren fuss around in one of the old bramble bush .
`` Hello , Jenny ! ''
say Peter .
`` Why do Reddy wear a red coat ? ''
`` Do you mean to say that you do n't know ? ''
Jenny Wren look very hard at Peter with her sharp eye .
`` I think everybody know that !
You certainly be slow , Peter Rabbit .
I have n't time to tell you about it now .
Go ask Grandfather Frog ; he know all about it . ''
Jenny Wren bustle off before Peter could find his tongue .
Now , you all know how full of curiosity Peter Rabbit be .
Jenny Wren 's busy tongue have set that curiosity fairly boil over .
He just could n't sit still for wonder and wonder why Reddy Fox wear a red coat .
He have never think anything about it before , but now he could n't get it out of his head .
He just have to know .
So , make sure that Reddy Fox have disappear in the Green Forest , Peter start for the Smiling Pool , lipperty-lipperty-lip , a fast a he could go .
There he find Grandfather Frog set on his big green lily-pad , just a usual .
`` If you please , Grandfather Frog , why do Reddy Fox wear a red coat ? ''
pant Peter , quite out of breath .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
grunt Grandfather Frog crossly .
`` Do n't you know that it be very impolite to disturb people when they be have a nap ? ''
`` I -- I 'm very sorry .
Indeed I be , Grandfather Frog , '' say Peter very humbly .
`` Will you tell me if I come again some time when you be not so sleepy ? ''
Now , like everybody else , Grandfather Frog be rather fond of Peter Rabbit , and now Peter look so truly sorry , and at the same time there be such a look of disappointment in Peter 's eye , that Grandfather Frog forget all about his crossness .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say he .
`` You and your question be a nuisance , Peter Rabbit , and I may as well get rid of you now a to have you keep come down here and pester me to death .
Besides , any one who have to keep such a sharp watch for Reddy Fox a you do ought to know why he wear a red coat .
If you 'll promise to sit perfectly still and ask no foolish question , I 'll tell you the story . ''
Of course Peter promise , and settle himself comfortably to listen .
And this be the story that Grandfather Frog tell : `` A long time ago , when the world be young , old Mr. Fox , the grandfather a thousand time remove of Reddy Fox , be one of the smart of all the forest and meadow people , just a Reddy be now .
He be so smart that he know enough not to appear smart , and the fact be his neighbor think him rather dull .
He wear just a common , everyday suit of dull brown , like most of the others , and there be n't anything about him to attract attention .
He be always very polite , very polite indeed , to every one .
Yes , Sir , Mr. Fox be very polite .
He always seem to be mind his own business , and he never go around ask foolish question or poke his nose into other people 's affair . ''
Grandfather Frog stop a minute and look very hard at Peter after he say this , and Peter look uncomfortable .
`` Now , although Mr. Fox do n't appear to take any interest in other people 's affair and never ask question , he have two of the sharp ear among all the little meadow and forest people , and while he be go about seem to be just mind his own business , he be listen and listen to all that be say .
Everything he hear he remember , so that it be n't long before he know more about what be go on than all his neighbor together .
But he keep his mouth tight close , do Mr. Fox , and be very humble and polite to everybody .
Every night he come home early and go to bed by sundown , and everybody say what good habit Mr. Fox have .
`` But when everybody else be asleep , Mr. Fox use to steal out and be go half the night .
Yes , Sir , sometimes he 'd be go until almost morning .
But he always take care to get home before any of his neighbor be awake , and then he 'd wait until everybody be up before he show himself .
When he come out and start to hunt for his breakfast , some one be sure to tell him of mischief do during the darkness of the night .
Sometimes it be a storehouse break into , and the best thing take .
Sometimes it be of terrible fright that some of the little people have receive by be waken in the night and see a fierce face with long , sharp teeth grinning at them .
Sometimes it be of bad thing that be tell in whisper .
Mr. Fox use to listen a if very much shock , and say that something ought to be do about it , and wonder who it could be who would do such dreadful thing .
`` By and by thing get so bad that they reach the ear of Old Mother Nature , and she come to find out what it all meant .
Now , the very night before she arrive , Mrs. Quack , who live on the river bank , have a terrible fright .
Somebody spring upon her a she be sleep , and in the struggle she lose all her tail feather .
She hurry to tell Old Mother Nature all about it , and big tear roll down her cheek a she tell how she have lose all her beautiful tail feather .
Mother Nature call all the people of the forest and the meadow together .
She make them all pas before her , and she look sharply at each one a they go by .
Mr. Fox look meeker than ever , and he be very humble and polite .
`` Now when Mr. Fox have pay his respect and turn his back , Old Mother Nature saw something red on the tail of his coat .
It be nothing but a little smear of red clay , but that be enough for Old Mother Nature .
You see , she know that Mrs. Quack 's home be right at the foot of a red claybank .
She do n't say a word until everybody have pay their respect and pass before her .
Then she tell them how grieved she be to hear of all the trouble there have be , but that she could n't watch over each one all the time ; they must learn to watch out for themselves .
`` And so that you may know who to watch out for , from now on never trust the one who wear a bright red coat , '' conclude Old Mother Nature .
`` All of a sudden Mr. Fox become aware that everybody be look at him , and in every face be hate .
He glance at his coat .
It be bright red !
Then Mr. Fox know that he have be find out , and he sneak away with his tail between his leg .
The first chance he get , he go to Old Mother Nature and beg her to give him back his old coat .
She promise that she would when his heart change , and he change his way .
But his heart never do change , and his child and his child 's child be just like him .
They have always be the smart and the sliest and the most feared and dislike of all the little people on the meadow or in the forest .
And now you know why Reddy Fox wear a red coat , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
Peter Rabbit draw a long breath .
`` Thank you , thank you , Grandfather Frog ! ''
say he .
`` I -- I think hereafter I 'll be quite content with my own suit , even if it be n't handsome .
Jenny Wren be right .
A good heart and honest way be good than fine clothes . ''
V WHY JIMMY SKUNK NEVER HURRIES The Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind have just be release from the big bag in which she carry them every night to their home behind the Purple Hills and every morning bring them back to the Green Meadows to romp and play all day .
They romp and race and dance away , some one way , some another , to see whom they could find to play with .
Presently some of them spy Jimmy Skunk slowly amble down the Crooked Little Path , stop every few step to pull over a loose stone or stick .
They know what he be do that for .
They know that he be look for fat beetle for his breakfast .
They dance over to him and form a ring around him while they sing : `` Who be it never , never hurry ?
Who be it never , never worry ?
Who be it do just what he please , Just like u Merry Little Breezes ?
Jimmy Skunk !
Jimmy Skunk ! ''
Now not so far away but that he could hear them very plainly sat Peter Rabbit , just finish his breakfast in a sweet-clover patch .
He sit up very straight , so a to hear well .
Of course some of the Merry Little Breezes saw him right away .
They leave Jimmy to come over and dance in a circle around Peter , for Peter be a great favorite with them .
And a they dance they sing : `` Who be it hop and skip and jump ?
Who be it sometimes loudly thump ?
Who be it dearly love to play , But when there 's danger run away ?
Peter Rabbit !
Peter Rabbit ! ''
Peter grin good-naturedly .
He be quite use to be laugh at for always run away , and he do n't mind it in the least .
`` When danger 's near , who run away will live to run another day , '' retort Peter promptly .
Then he begin the mad kind of a frolic with the Merry Little Breezes until they and he be quite tire out and ready for a good rest .
`` I wish , '' say Peter , a he stretch himself out in the middle of the patch of sweet clover , `` that you would tell me why it be that Jimmy Skunk never hurry . ''
`` And we wish that you would tell u the same thing , '' cry one of the Merry Little Breezes .
`` But I ca n't , '' protest Peter .
`` Everybody else seem to hurry , at time anyway , but Jimmy never do .
He say it be a waste of energy , whatever that mean . ''
`` I tell you what -- let 's go over to the Smiling Pool and ask Grandfather Frog about it now .
He 'll be sure to know , '' speak up one of the Merry Little Breezes .
`` All right , '' reply Peter , hop to his foot .
`` But you 'll have to ask him .
I 've ask him for so many story that I do n't dare ask for another right away , for fear that he will say that I be a nuisance . ''
So it be agree that the Merry Little Breezes should ask Grandfather Frog why it be that Jimmy Skunk never hurry , and that Peter should keep out of sight until Grandfather Frog have begin the story , for they be sure that there would be a story .
Away they all hurry to the Smiling Pool .
The Merry Little Breezes race so hard that they be quite out of breath when they burst through the bulrush and surround Grandfather Frog , a he sit on his big green lily-pad .
`` Oh , Grandfather Frog , why be it that Jimmy Skunk never hurry ? ''
they pant .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
reply Grandfather Frog in his deepest , gruff voice .
`` Chug-a-rum !
Probably because he have learn well . ''
`` Oh ! ''
say one of the Merry Little Breezes , in a rather faint , disappointed sort of voice .
Just then he spy a fat , foolish , green fly and blow it right over to Grandfather Frog , who snap it up in a flash .
Right away all the Merry Little Breezes begin to hunt for foolish green fly and blow them over to Grandfather Frog , until he do n't have room for another one inside his white and yellow waistcoat .
Indeed the leg of the last one he try to swallow stick out of one corner of his big mouth .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog , try very hard to get those leg out of sight .
`` Chug-a-rum !
I always like to do something for those who do something for me , and I suppose now that I ought to tell you why it be that Jimmy Skunk never hurry .
I would , if Peter Rabbit be here .
If I tell you the story , Peter will be sure to hear of it , and then he will give me no peace until I tell it to him , and I do n't like to tell story twice . ''
`` But he be here ! ''
cried one of the Little Breezes .
`` He 's right over behind that little clump of tall grass . ''
`` Humph !
I think he be n't very far away , '' grunt Grandfather Frog , with a twinkle in his great , goggly eye .
Peter creep out of his hiding-place , look rather shamefaced and very foolish .
Then the Merry Little Breezes settle themselves on the lily-pads in a big circle around Grandfather Frog , and Peter sit down as close to the edge of the bank of the Smiling Pool a he dare to get .
After what seem to them a very long time , Grandfather Frog swallow the leg of the last foolish green fly , open his big mouth , and begin : `` Of course you all know that long , long ago , when the world be young , thing be very different from what they be now , very different indeed .
The great-great-ever-so-great grandfather of Jimmy Skunk be slim and trim than Jimmy be .
He be more like his cousin , Mr. Weasel and Mr. Mink .
He be just a quick move a they be .
Yes , Sir , Mr . Skunk be very lively on his foot .
He have to be to keep out of the way of his big neighbor , for in those day he do n't have any mean of protect himself , a Jimmy have now .
He be dress all in black .
You know it be n't until Old Mother Nature find out that he be take advantage of that black suit to get into mischief on dark night that she give him white stripe , so that the darker the night , the harder it would be for him to keep from be see .
`` Now Mr . Skunk be very smart and shrewd , oh , very !
When the hard time come , which make so many change in the life of the people who live in the Green Forest and on the Green Meadows , Mr . Skunk be very quick to see that unless he could think of some way to protect himself , it be only a matter of time when he would furnish a dinner for one of his fierce big neighbor , and of course Mr . Skunk have no desire to do that .
It be then that he ask Old Mother Nature to give him a bag of perfume so strong that it would make everybody ill but himself .
Mother Nature think it all over , and then she do , but she make him promise that he would never use it unless he be in great danger .
`` Mr . Skunk have to try his new defence only once or twice before his enemy take the great care to let him alone .
He find that he no longer have to run for a safe hiding-place when he meet Mr. Wolf or Mr. Lynx or Mr. Panther .
They just snarl at him and pass without offer to touch him .
So Mr . Skunk grow very independent and go where he please when he please .
And , because he no longer have to run from his enemy , he get out of the habit of run .
Then he make a discovery .
He watch those of his neighbor who be forever hurry about look for food , hurrying because all the time there be great fear upon them that an enemy might be near , hurry because each be fearful that his neighbor would get more than he .
It be n't long before Mr . Skunk saw that in their hurry they overlook a great deal .
In fact , by just follow after them slowly , he find all he want to eat .
`` So Mr . Skunk begin to grow fat .
His neighbor , who be have hard work to make a living , grow envious , and say unkind thing about him , and hint that he must be steal , or he never could have so much to eat .
But Mr . Skunk do n't mind .
He go right on about his business .
He never worry , because , you know , he fear nobody .
And he never hurry , because he find that it pay best to go slowly .
In that way he never miss any of the good thing that his hurrying , worry neighbor do .
So he grow fatter and fatter , while others grow thinner .
After a while he almost forget how to run .
Being fat and never hurrying or worry make him good-natured .
He keep right on mind his own affair and never meddling in the affair of others , so that by and by his neighbor begin to respect him .
`` Of course he teach his child to do a he do , and they teach their child .
And so , ever since that long-ago day , when the world be young , that little bag of perfume have be hand down in the Skunk family , and none of them have ever be afraid .
Now you know why Jimmy Skunk , whom you all know , be so independent and never hurry . ''
`` Thank you !
Thank you , Grandfather Frog ! ''
cry the Merry Little Breezes .
`` When you want some more foolish green fly , just let u know , and we 'll get them for you . ''
`` Chug-a-rum !
What be you look so wistful for , Peter Rabbit ? ''
demand Grandfather Frog .
`` I -- I be just wish that I have a -- '' begin Peter .
Then suddenly he make a face .
`` No , I do n't either ! ''
he declare .
`` I guess I 'd well be get home to the dear Old Briar-patch now .
Mrs. Peter probably think something have happen to me . ''
And away he go , lipperty-lipperty-lip .
VI WHY SAMMY JAY HAS A FINE COAT Sammy Jay have a very fine coat , a very beautiful coat .
Everybody know that .
In fact , Sammy 's coat have long be the envy of a great many of his neighbor in the Green Forest .
Some of them , you know , have very modest coat .
They be not beautiful at all .
And yet the owner of some of these plain coat be among the most honest and hard-working of all the little people who live in the Green Forest .
They find it hard , very hard indeed , to understand why such a scamp and mischiefmaker a Sammy Jay should be give such a wonderful blue coat with white trimming .
Peter Rabbit often have think about it .
He have a number of feathered friend whom he like ever so much good than he do Sammy Jay .
In fact , he and Sammy be forever fall out , because Sammy delight to tease Peter .
He sometimes make up for it by warn Peter when Granny or Reddy Fox happen to be about , and Peter be honest enough to recognize this and put it to Sammy 's credit .
But in spite of this , it never seem to him quite right that Sammy Jay should be so handsomely dress .
`` Of course , '' say Peter to Grandfather Frog , `` Old Mother Nature know a great deal more than I do -- '' `` Really !
You do n't mean to say so !
Chug-a-rum !
You do n't mean to say so , Peter ! ''
interrupt Grandfather Frog , pretend to be very much surprise at what Peter say .
-LSB- Illustration : `` You do n't mean to say so , Peter , '' interrupt Grandfather Frog . -RSB-
Peter grin and wrinkle his nose at Grandfather Frog .
`` Yes , '' say he , `` Old Mother Nature know a great deal more than I do , but it seem to me a if she have make a mistake in give Sammy Jay such a handsome coat .
There must be a reason , I suppose , but for the life of me I can not understand it .
I should think that she would give such a thief a Sammy Jay the very homely suit she could find .
You may depend I would , if I be in her place . ''
Grandfather Frog chuckle until he shake all over .
`` It 's lucky for some of u that you be not in her place ! ''
say he .
`` Chug-a-rum !
It certainly be lucky ! ''
`` If I be , I would give you a handsome coat , too , Grandfather Frog , '' reply Peter .
Grandfather Frog suddenly swell out with indignation .
`` Chug-a-rum !
Chug-a-rum !
What 's the matter with the coat I have get , Peter Rabbit ?
Tell me that !
Who 's get a handsomer one ? ''
Grandfather Frog glare with his great , goggly eye at Peter .
`` I do n't mean to say that you have n't get a handsome coat .
Your coat be handsome , very handsome indeed , Grandfather Frog , '' Peter hasten to say .
`` I always do like green .
I just love it !
And I should think you would be ever so proud of your white and yellow waistcoat .
I would if it be mine .
What I mean to say be , that if I be in Old Mother Nature 's place , I would give some plain folk handsome suit .
Certainly , I would n't give such a rascal a Sammy Jay one of the handsome coat in all the Green Forest .
Knowing Sammy as well a I do , it be hard work to believe that he come by it honestly . ''
Grandfather Frog chuckle way down deep in his throat .
`` Sammy come by it honestly enough , Peter .
Yes , Sir , he come by it honestly enough , because it be hand down to him by his father , who get it from his father , who get it from his father , and so on , way back to the day when the world be young , but -- '' Grandfather Frog pause , and that dreamy , far-away look which Peter have see so often come into his great , goggly eye .
`` But what , Grandfather Frog ? ''
ask Peter eagerly , when he could keep still no longer .
Grandfather Frog settle himself comfortably on his big green lily-pad and look very hard at Peter .
`` I 'm go to tell you a story , Peter Rabbit , '' say he , `` so that never again will you be lead to doubt that Old Mother Nature know exactly what she be about .
In the first place , Sammy Jay be not wholly to blame for all his bad habit .
Some of them be hand down to him with his fine coat , just the same a your troublesome curiosity be hand down to you with the white patch on the seat of your trouser . ''
Peter nod .
He have felt a great many time that he just could n't help this habit of poke that wobbly little nose of his in where it have no business to be , any more than he could change that funny little bunch of white cotton , which he call a tail , for a really , truly tail .
`` Of course , you have hear all about what a very fine gentleman Sammy Jay 's great-great-ever-so-great grandfather be think to be until it be discover that he be all the time steal from his neighbor and put the blame on others , and how Old Mother Nature punish him by take away the beautiful voice of which he be so proud , and give him instead the harsh voice which Sammy have now , and make him tell just what he be by scream ` thief , thief , thief ! '
every time he open his mouth to speak .
`` At first Old Mother Nature have intend to take away the fine coat of which Mr. Jay be so proud , but when he discover that he have lose his fine voice , he be so ashamed that he hurry away to hide himself from the eye of his neighbor , so that Old Mother Nature do n't have time to change his coat just then .
` I 'll wait a bit , ' say she to herself , ` and see how he behave .
Perhaps he be truly sorry for what he have do , and I will not have to punish him more . '
`` But if Mr. Jay be truly sorry , he give no sign of it .
You see , he have cheat his neighbor , and have steal from them for so long , that he find this the easy way to get a living .
His bad habit have become fix , a bad habit have a way of do .
Besides , right down in his heart , he be n't sorry for what he have do , only angry at have be find out .
Now that he have be find out , of course every one be on the watch for him , and it be n't so easy to steal a it have be before .
So now , instead of go about openly , with his head hold high , he grow very crafty , and sneak quietly about through the Green Forest , try to keep out of sight , that he might the easy steal from his neighbor and make trouble for them .
`` When Old Mother Nature saw this , she change her mind about take away his handsome suit .
` If I do that , ' think she , ` it will make it all the easy for him to keep out of sight , and all the harder for his neighbor to know when he be about . '
`` So instead of give him the plain , homely suit that she have think of give him , she make his coat of blue brighter than before and trim it with the white of white trimming , so that Mr. Jay have one of the very handsome coat in all the Green Forest .
At first he be very proud of it , but it be n't long before he find that it be very hard work to keep out of sight when he want to .
That bright blue coat be forever give him away when he be out on mischief .
Everybody be all the time on the watch for it , and so where in the past Mr. Jay have be able , without any trouble , to steal all he want to eat , now he sometimes actually have to work for his food , and get it honestly or else go hungry .
`` You would suppose that he would have mend him way , would n't you ? ''
Peter nod .
`` But he do n't .
He grow more sly and crafty than ever .
But in spite of this , he do n't begin to make a much trouble a before .
He could n't , you know , because of his bright coat .
When Old Mother Nature find that Mr. Jay have pass along his bad habit to his child , she pass along his handsome blue coat , too , and so it have be from that long-ago day right down to this .
Sammy Jay 's fine coat be n't a reward for goodness , a be Winsome Bluebird 's , but be to help the other little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows to protect themselves , and keep track of Sammy when he be sneak and snoop around look for mischief .
Now what do you think , Peter Rabbit ? ''
Peter scratch one long ear and then the other long ear thoughtfully , and he look a wee bit ashamed a he reply : `` I guess Old Mother Nature make no mistake and always know just what she be do . ''
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog in his deep voice .
`` You may be sure she do .
And another thing , Peter Rabbit : Never judge any one by his clothes .
It be a great mistake , a very great mistake .
Plain clothes sometimes cover the kind heart , and fine clothes often be a warning to beware of mischief . ''
`` I -- I do n't know but you be right , '' admit Peter .
`` I know I be , '' say Grandfather Frog .
VII WHY JERRY MUSKRAT BUILDS HIS HOUSE IN THE WATER Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck have go down to the Smiling Pool for a call on their old friend , Jerry Muskrat .
But Jerry be nowhere to be see .
They wait and wait , but no Jerry Muskrat .
`` Probably he be take a nap in that big house of his , '' say Johnny Chuck , `` and if he be we 'll have to sit here until he wake up , or else go back home and visit him some other time . ''
`` That 's so , '' reply Peter .
`` I do n't see what he have his house in the water for , anyway .
If he have build it on land , like sensible people , we might be able to waken him .
Funny place to build a house , be n't it ? ''
Johnny Chuck scratch his head thoughtfully .
`` It do seem a funny place , '' he admit .
`` It certainly do seem a funny place .
But then , Jerry Muskrat be a funny fellow .
You know how much of the time he stay in the water .
That seem funny to me .
I suppose there be a reason for it , and probably there be a reason for build his house where it be .
I 've find that there be a reason for most thing .
Probably Jerry 's great-great-grandfather build his house that way , and so Jerry do the same thing . ''
Peter Rabbit suddenly brighten up .
`` I do believe you be right , Johnny Chuck , and if you be , there must be a story about it , and if there be a story , Grandfather Frog will be sure to know it .
There he be , over on his big green lily-pad , and he look a if he might be feel very good-natured this morning .
Let 's go ask him why Jerry Muskrat build his house in the water . ''
Grandfather Frog saw them come , and he guess right away that they be come for a story .
He grin to himself and pretend to go to sleep .
`` Good morning , Grandfather Frog , '' say Johnny Chuck .
Grandfather Frog do n't answer .
Johnny try again , and still no reply .
`` He 's asleep , '' say Johnny , look dreadfully disappoint , `` and I guess we 'd well not disturb him , for he might wake up cross , and of course we would n't get a story if he do . ''
Peter look at Grandfather Frog sharply .
He be n't so sure that that be a real nap .
It seem to him that there be just the least little hint of a smile in the corner of Grandfather Frog 's big mouth .
`` You sit here a minute , '' he whisper in Johnny Chuck 's ear .
So Johnny Chuck sit down where he be , which be right where Grandfather Frog could see him by lift one eyelid just the teeny bit , and Peter hop along the bank until he be right behind Grandfather Frog .
Now just at that place on the bank be grow a toadstool .
Peter look over at Johnny Chuck and wink .
Then he turn around , and with one of his long hind-feet , he kick the toadstool with all his might .
Now toadstools , a you all know , be not very well fasten at the root , and this one be no different from the rest .
When Peter kick it it fly out into the air and land with a great splash in the Smiling Pool , close beside the big green lily-pad on which Grandfather Frog be sit .
Of course he do n't see it come , and of course it give him a great start .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
exclaim Grandfather Frog and dive head first into the water .
A minute later Peter 's sharp eye saw him peep out from under a lily-pad to see what have frighten him so .
`` Ha , ha , ha ! ''
shout Peter , dance about on the bank .
`` Ha , ha , ha !
Grandfather Frog , afraid of a toadstool !
Ha , ha , ha ! ''
At first Grandfather Frog be angry , very angry indeed .
But he be too old and too wise to lose his temper for long over a joke , especially when he have be fairly catch try to play a joke himself .
So presently he climb back on to his big green lily-pad , blink his great , goggly eye and look just a wee bit foolish .
`` Chug-a-rum !
I might have know that that be some of your work , Peter Rabbit , '' say he , `` but I think it surely be a stone throw by Farmer Brown 's boy .
What do you mean by frighten an old fellow like me this way ? ''
`` Just try to get even with you for try to fool u into think that you be asleep when you be wide awake , '' reply Peter .
`` Oh , Grandfather Frog , do tell u why it be that Jerry Muskrat build his house in the water .
Please do ! ''
`` I have a mind not to , just to get even with you , '' say Grandfather Frog , settle himself comfortably , `` but I believe I will , to show you that there be some folk who can take a joke without lose their temper . ''
`` Goody ! ''
cry Peter and Johnny Chuck together , sit down side by side on the very edge of the bank .
Grandfather Frog fold his hand across his white and yellow waistcoat and half close his eye , a if look way , way back into the past .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
he begin .
`` A long , long time ago , when the world be young , there be very little dry land , and most of the animal live in the water .
Yes , Sir , most of the animal live in the water , a sensible animal do to-day . ''
Peter nudge Johnny Chuck .
`` He mean himself and his family , '' he whisper with a chuckle .
`` After a time , '' continue Grandfather Frog , `` there begin to be more land and still more .
Then some of the animal begin to spend most of their time on the land .
As there get to be more and more land , more and more of the animal leave the water , until finally most of them be spend nearly all of the time on land .
Now Old Mother Nature have be keep a sharp watch , a she always do , and when she find that they be foolish enough to like the land best , she do all that she could to make thing comfortable for them .
She teach them how to run and jump and climb and dig , accord to which thing they like best to do , so that it be n't very long before a lot of them forget that they ever have live in the water , and they begin to look down on those who still live in the water , and to put on air and hold their head very high .
`` Now , of course , Old Mother Nature do n't like this , and to punish them she say that they should no longer be able to live in the water , even if they want to .
At first they only laugh , but after a while they find that quite often there be time when it would be very nice to be at home in the water a they once have be .
But it be of no use .
Some could swim as long a they could keep their head above water , but as soon a they put their head under water they be likely to drown .
You know that be the way with you to-day , Peter Rabbit . ''
Peter nod .
He know that he could swim if he have to , but only for a very little way , and he hat the thought of it .
`` Now there be a few animal , of whom old Mr. Muskrat , the grandfather a thousand time remove of Jerry Muskrat , be one , who learn to walk and run on dry land , but who still love the water , '' continue Grandfather Frog .
`` One day Old Mother Nature find Mr. Muskrat sit on a rock , look very mournful . ''
` What 's the matter , Mr. Muskrat ? '
she ask .
`` Mr. Muskrat look very much ashamed a he finally own up that he be envious of his cousin and some of the other animal , because they have such fine house on the land . ''
` Then why do n't you build you a fine house on the land ? '
ask Old Mother Nature .
`` Mr. Muskrat hesitate .
` I -- I -- love the water too well to want to stay on land all the time , ' say he , ` and -- and -- well , I be put in the water in the first place , and I ought to be content with what I have get and make the best of it . '
`` Old Mother Nature be so pleased with Mr. Muskrat 's reply that right away she make up her mind that he should have a finer house than any of the others , so she take him over to a quiet little pool , where the water be not too deep and she show him how to build a wonderful house of mud and rush and twig , with a nice warm bedroom line with grass above the water , and an entrance down under the water , so that no one except those who still live most of the time in the water could possibly get into it .
None of his friend on land have such a big , fine house , and Mr. Muskrat be very proud of it .
But with all his pride he never forget that it be a reward for try to be content with his surroundings and make the best of them .
`` So from that day to this , the Muskrats have build their house in the water , and have be among the most industrious , content , and happy of all the animal .
And that be why Jerry Muskrat have build that fine house in the Smiling Pool and have so few enemy , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
Peter Rabbit draw a long breath , which be almost a sigh .
`` I almost wish my grandfather a thousand time remove have be content to stay in the water , too , '' he say .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
retort Grandfather Frog .
`` If he have , you would n't have the dear Old Briar-patch .
Be content with what you 've get , '' `` I think I will , '' say Peter .
VIII WHY OLD MAN COYOTE HAS MANY VOICES Of course Old Man Coyote have only one voice , but that one be such a wonderful voice that he can make it sound like a great many voice , all yelping and howling and shouting and laughing at the same time .
So those who hear him always say that he have many voice , and that certainly be the way it seem .
The first time Peter Rabbit hear Old Man Coyote , he be sure , absolutely sure , that there be a whole crowd of stranger on the Green Meadows , and you may be sure that he keep very close to his dear Old Briar-patch .
If you have be there and try to tell Peter that all that noise be make by just one voice , he would n't have believe you .
No , Sir , he would n't have believe you .
And you could n't have blame him .
It be the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind who first tell Peter who the stranger be and warn him to watch out , because Old Man Coyote be just a fond of Rabbit a Granny or Reddy Fox , and be even more crafty and sly than they .
Peter thank the Merry Little Breezes for the warning , and then he ask them how many of his family Old Man Coyote have bring with him .
Of course the Merry Little Breezes tell Peter that Old Man Coyote be all alone , and they become very indignant when Peter laugh at them .
He just could n't help it .
`` Why , '' say he , `` every night I hear a whole crowd yelping and howl together . ''
`` But you do n't ! ''
insist the Merry Little Breezes .
`` It be Old Man Coyote alone who make all that noise . ''
`` Do n't you suppose I know what I hear ? ''
demand Peter .
`` No ! ''
retort the Merry Little Breezes .
`` You may have big ear and be able to hear a great deal , sometimes a great deal more than you have any business to hear , but you be old enough by this time to have learn that you can not believe all you hear . ''
And with that the Merry Little Breezes indignantly race away to spread the news all over the Green Meadows .
Now Peter be quite a indignant because they think he could n't or should n't believe his own ear , a they be because he would n't believe what they tell him , and all the rest of that day he could n't put the matter out of his mind .
He be still think of it a the Black Shadows come creep down from the Purple Hills across the Green Meadows .
Suddenly Peter saw a dark form skulking among the Black Shadows .
At first he think it be Reddy Fox , only somehow it look big .
Peter , safe in the dear Old Briar-patch , watch .
Presently the dark form come out from among the Black Shadows where Peter could see it clearly , sit down , point a sharp nose up at the first twinkling little star , open a big mouth , and out of it pour such a yelping and howling a make Peter shiver with fright .
And now Peter have to believe his eye rather than his ear .
His ear tell him that there be many voice , but his eye tell him that all that dreadful sound be come out of one mouth .
It be hard , very hard , to believe , but it be so .
`` The Merry Little Breezes be right , '' mutter Peter to himself , a Old Man Coyote trot away in the direction of the Green Forest , and he felt a wee bit ashamed to think that he have refuse to believe them .
After that , Peter could think of nothing but Old Man Coyote 's wonderful voice that sound like many voice , and at the very first opportunity he hurry over to the Smiling Pool to ask Grandfather Frog what it mean .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog .
`` It mean simply that Old Man Coyote come of a very smart family , and that he know how to make the most of the gift of Old Mother Nature to his grandfather a thousand time remove . ''
This sound so much like a story that Peter straightway tease Grandfather Frog to tell him all about it .
At last , to get rid of him and enjoy a little quiet and peace , Grandfather Frog do so .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
he begin , a he always do .
`` The great-great-ever-so-great grandfather of Old Man Coyote , who live long , long ago when the world be young , be very much a Old Man Coyote be to-day .
He be just a smart and just a clever .
Indeed , he be smart enough and clever enough not to let his neighbor know that he be smart and clever at all .
Those be very peaceful time at first , and everybody be on the best of term with everybody else , a you know .
There be plenty to eat without the trouble to steal , and everybody be honest simply because it be easy to be honest than it be to be dishonest .
So Old King Bear rule in the Green Forest , and everybody be happy and content .
`` But there come a time when food be scarce , and it be no long easy to get plenty to eat .
It be then that the strong begin to steal from the weaker , and by and by even to prey upon those small than themselves .
The time grow hard and hard , and because hunger be a hard and cruel master , it make the large and strong people hard and cruel , too .
Some of them it make very sly and cunning , like old Mr. Fox .
Mr. Coyote be another whom it make sly and cunning .
He be smart in the first place , even smarter than Mr. Fox , and he very early make up his mind that if he would live , it must be by his wit , for he be n't big enough or strong enough to fight with his neighbor such a his big cousin , Mr . Timber Wolf , or Mr. Lynx , or Mr. Panther or Old King Bear , who be king no longer .
And yet he like the same thing to eat .
`` So he use to study and plan how he could outwit them without danger to himself . '
A whole skin be good than a full stomach , but both a whole skin and a full stomach be good still , ' say he to himself ; a he think and scheme .
For a while he be content to catch what he could without danger to himself , and to eat what his big and strong neighbor leave when they happen to get more than they want for themselves .
Little by little he get the habit of slyly follow them when they be hunt , always keep out of sight .
In this way , he manage to get many meal of scrap .
But these scrap never wholly satisfy him , and his mouth use to water a he watch the others feast on the very best when they have have a successful hunt .
He know it would n't be of the least use to go out and boldly ask for some , for in those hard time everybody be very , very selfish .
`` The time grow hard and hard , until it seem a if Old Mother Nature have wholly forget her little people of the Green Meadows and the Green Forest .
Mr. Coyote still manage to pick up a living , but he be hungry most of the time , and the le he have to put in his stomach , the sharp his wit grow .
At last one day , a he steal soft-footed through the Green Forest , he discover Mr. Lynx have a great feast .
To keep still and watch him be almost more than Mr. Coyote could stand , for he be so hungry that it seem a if the side of his stomach almost meet , it be so empty . ''
` If I could make myself into three , we could take that dinner away from Mr. Lynx ! ''
thought he , and right on top of that thought come a great idea .
Why not make Mr. Lynx think he have a lot of friend with him ?
It would do no harm to try .
So Mr. Coyote put his nose up in the air and howl .
Mr. Lynx look up and grin .
He have no fear of Mr. Coyote .
Then Mr. Coyote hurry around to the other side of Mr. Lynx , all the time keep out of sight , and howl again , and this time he try to make his voice sound different .
Mr. Lynx stop eat and look up a little surprised . '
I wonder if Mr. Coyote have get a brother with him , ' think he .
A minute later Mr. Coyote howl again from the place where he have howl in the first place .
` He certainly have , ' think Mr. Lynx , ` but I 'm a match for two of them , ' and once more he go on eating .
`` Then Mr. Coyote begin to run in a circle around Mr. Lynx , always keep out of sight in the thick brush , and every few step he yelp or howl , and each yelp or howl he try to make sound different .
Now Mr. Coyote could run very fast , and he run now as hard a ever he could in a big circle , yelp and howl and make his voice sound as different a possible each time .
Mr. Lynx grow anxious and lose his appetite .
` Mr. Coyote must have a whole crowd of brother , ' think he . '
I guess this be no place for me ! '
With that he start to sneak away .
`` Mr. Coyote follow him , still try to make his voice sound like the voice of many .
Mr. Lynx give a hurried look over his shoulder and begin to run .
Mr. Coyote keep after him , yelp and howl , until he be sure that Mr. Lynx be so frightened that he would n't dare come back .
Then Mr. Coyote return to the dinner Mr. Lynx have leave , and ate and ate until he could n't hold another mouthful .
His throat be very raw and sore because he have strain it try to make his voice change so often , but he do n't mind this , because , you know , it felt so good to have all he could eat at one time once more .
`` Now it just happen that Old Mother Nature have come along just in time to see and hear Mr. Coyote , and it tickle her so to think that Mr. Coyote have be so smart that what do you think she do ?
Why , while he sleep that night , she heal his sore throat , and she give him a new voice ; and this voice be very wonderful , for it sound for all the world like many voice , all yelping and howling at the same time .
After that , all Mr. Coyote have to do when he want to frighten some one big and strong than himself be to open his mouth and send forth his new voice , which sound like many voice .
`` So he have plenty to eat from that time on .
And all his child and his child 's child have that same wonderful voice , just a Old Man Coyote have now .
Chug-a-rum !
Now scamper home , Peter Rabbit , and see that you do n't let Old Man Coyote 's sharp wit get you into trouble . ''
`` Thank you , Grandfather Frog ! ''
cry Peter and scamper as fast a he could go for the dear , safe Old Briar-patch .
IX WHY MINER THE MOLE LIVES UNDER GROUND Striped Chipmunk sit star at a little ridge where the grass be raise up .
He have often see little ridge like that without think much about them .
He know that they be make by Miner the Mole .
He have know that ever since he be big enough to begin to ask question .
But now a he look at this one , it suddenly strike him that he have not see Miner the Mole more than once or twice in all his life .
`` What a queer way of living ! ''
thought Striped Chipmunk .
`` It 's all very well to have a snug house under the ground , where one can sleep the long cold winter away and be perfectly safe , but what any one want to live under the ground all the time for , in the beautiful springtime and summertime and autumntime , I ca n't understand .
Just think of all that Miner miss -- the sunshine , the flower , the song of the bird , and the Merry Little Breezes to play with !
I wonder -- '' `` What do you wonder ? ''
The voice be so close to Striped Chipmunk that it make him jump .
He whirl about .
There be Johnny Chuck , who have tiptoe up as softly a he know how , to give Striped Chipmunk a scare .
Johnny grin .
`` What do you wonder ? ''
he repeat .
Striped Chipmunk make a face at Johnny .
`` I wonder something that I bet you do n't know , '' he reply .
`` That 's easy , '' reply Johnny .
`` There be more thing I do n't know than I do know , but I 'm always ready to learn .
What be it this time ? ''
`` Why do Miner the Mole live under ground all the time ? ''
Striped Chipmunk point to the ridge make by Miner .
Johnny Chuck scratch his head thoughtfully .
`` I do n't know , '' he confess finally .
`` I never think of it before .
Of course there must be a reason .
He never come out to play with the rest of u -- just spend all his time by himself down in the dark , dig and digging .
I wonder -- '' `` Well , what do you wonder ? ''
`` The same thing you wonder , '' laugh Johnny Chuck .
`` If you have n't get anything else to do , let 's go down to the Smiling Pool and ask Grandfather Frog ; he 'll be sure to know . ''
Striped Chipmunk have n't anything else to do , so off they start .
On the way they meet Jimmy Skunk and Danny Meadow Mouse .
Neither of them know why Miner the Mole live under ground , and because they have n't anything well to do , they also start for the Smiling Pool .
Grandfather Frog be sit on his big green lily-pad in the warm sunshine , and for once he do n't have to be tease for a story .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say he in his deep voice .
`` It 's very strange to me how little some folk know about their near neighbor . ''
He look up and wink at jolly , round , bright Mr. Sun .
Striped Chipmunk , Johnny Chuck , Jimmy Skunk , and Danny Meadow Mouse look a though they felt very foolish , a indeed they do .
You see , all their life Miner the Mole have be one of their near neighbor , and yet they do n't know the first thing about him .
`` It happen a long time ago , '' continue Grandfather Frog .
`` When the world be young ? ''
interrupt Danny Meadow Mouse .
`` Of course , '' reply Grandfather Frog , pretend to be very much put out at such a foolish question .
Danny hang his head and resolve that he would bite his tongue before he ask another question .
`` In those day Miner 's great-great-grandfather a thousand time remove do n't live under ground , '' continue Grandfather Frog .
`` Nobody do .
He be n't so very different from a lot of other animal .
Food be plenty , and everybody be on the best of term with everybody else .
Mr. Mole live just a the rest do .
He go and come a he please , and enjoy the sunshine and take part in all the good time of his neighbor .
Everybody like him , and whenever he make a call , he be sure of a welcome .
But one thing Mr. Mole never do ; he never meddle in other people 's affair .
No , Sir , Mr. Mole never poke his nose in where he have no business .
`` For a long time everything go smoothly with all the people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows .
Then come hard time .
They grow hard and hard .
Food be scarce and keep grow more scarce .
Everybody be hungry , and you know how it be with hungry people -- they grow ugly and quarrelsome .
Matters grow bad and bad , and then it be that fear be bear .
The big people , like Old King Bear and Mr. Wolf and Mr. Panther and Mr. Lynx , begin to look with hungry eye on the little people , and the little people begin to grow afraid and hide from the big people , and all the time they be continually quarrel among themselves and steal from each other to get enough to eat .
`` Now , a I say before , Mr. Mole never have meddle with other people 's business , and he do n't now .
He go off by himself to think thing over .
` It be n't safe to run around any more , ' say he . '
I meet Mr. Wolf this morning , and he look at me with such a hungry look in his eye that it give me the cold shiver .
I believe he would have eat me , if I have n't crawl into an old hollow stump .
Now I ca n't run fast , because my leg be too short .
I ca n't climb tree like Mr. Squirrel , and I ca n't swim like Mr. Muskrat .
The only thing I can do be to dig . '
`` You see , Mr. Mole always have be very fond of digging , and he have do so much of it that his front leg and claw have grow very stout . ''
` Now if I dig a hole and keep out of sight , I wo n't have to worry about Mr. Wolf or anybody else , ' continue Mr. Mole to himself .
So he go to work at once and dig a hole on the Green Meadows , and , because he want to be comfortable , he make a big hole .
When it be finish , he be tire , so he curl up at the bottom for a nap .
He be awaken by hear voice outside .
He know those voice right away .
They be the voice of Mr. Fox and Mr. Badger . ''
` These be terrible time , ' say Mr. Fox .
` I 'm so hungry that I 'm waste away to a shadow .
I wonder who have dug this hole . ' ''
` Mr. Mole , ' reply Mr. Badger . '
I saw him at work here this morning .
Have you notice how very plump he look ? ' ''
` Yes , ' reply Mr. Fox .
` He make my mouth water the very last time I saw him .
Seems to me I can smell him now .
If he have make this hole just a little bit big I would go down and pull him out , but I be too tired to do any digging now . ' '' '
I tell you what , ' reply Mr. Badger .
` We 'll hunt together a little long , and then if we ca n't find anything to eat , we 'll come back , and I 'll help you dig , I hate to hurt Mr. Mole , because he always mind his own business , but these be hard time , and each one must look out for himself . '
`` With that they go away , leave Mr. Mole shake with fright at the bottom of his hole .
` It 's of no use , ' think Mr. Mole .
` If I go outside , they will soon find me , and if I stay here , they will dig me out .
Oh , dear , oh , dear !
What ever can I do ? '
`` He lay there feel very helpless and miserable , when all of a sudden a thought come to him .
If he have make his hole small , just big enough for him to crawl into , Mr. Badger and Mr. Fox would have have to do a great deal of dig to make it big enough for either of them to get in !
He would make a little tunnel off one side and hide in that .
So he go to work and make a little tunnel off one side just big enough for him to squeeze into .
He work very hard and very fast , and by the time Mr. Badger and Mr. Fox return , Mr. Mole be at the end of a long tunnel , so far from the hole he have first dug that he know it would take them a long time to dig him out , even if they notice his tunnel .
`` But they do n't .
They dig down to the bottom of his hole and then , because they do n't find him there , they straightway fell to quarrel , each blame the other for suggest such a lot of hard work for nothing .
Finally they go away , still call each other name , and from that day to this , Foxes and Badgers have never be friend .
`` Mr. Mole be very thankful for his narrow escape , and it set him to think .
If he have a lot of these underground tunnel , no one would be able to catch him .
It be a splendid idea !
He go to work on it at once .
And then he make a discovery -- such a splendid discovery !
There be plenty of food to eat right down under ground -- worm and grub -- all he need .
After that , Mr. Mole spend all his time in his tunnel and seldom put his nose outside .
He be safe , and he be comfortable , and he could always find something to eat by dig for it .
`` Little by little his old neighbor forget all about him .
Because he have little use for them , his eye grow small and small , and when he do come up into the light , they hurt him so that he be glad to go back into the dark again .
He be perfectly happy and satisfied there , and what be there in life well than to be happy and satisfy ? ''
`` Nothing , '' reply Striped Chipmunk , at whom Grandfather Frog happen to be look when he ask the question .
`` Right ! ''
reply Grandfather Frog .
`` And now you know why Miner the Mole live under ground -- because he be perfectly happy and satisfied there . ''
Just then up come Peter Rabbit , all out of breath .
`` Has Grandfather Frog be tell a story ? ''
he pant .
`` Yes , '' reply Striped Chipmunk , wink at Grandfather Frog , `` and now we be go back home perfectly happy and satisfied . ''
And to this day Peter Rabbit wonder what the story be that he miss .
X WHY MR. SNAKE CAN NOT WINK Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck be play tag on the Green Meadows .
Of course Peter can run so much fast than Johnny Chuck that he would never have be `` it '' if he have try his best to keep out of the way .
But he do n't .
No , Sir , Peter Rabbit do n't do anything of the kind .
He pretend that one of his long hind-legs be lame so that he have to run on three leg , while Johnny Chuck could use all four .
It be great fun .
They race and dodge and twisted and turn .
Sometimes Peter be so excited that he would forget and use all four leg .
Then Johnny Chuck would shout `` No fair ! ''
Peter would say that he do n't mean to , and to make up for it would be `` it '' and try to catch Johnny .
Now it happen that curl up on a little grassy tussock , take an early morning sun-bath , lay little Mr. Greensnake .
Of course Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck be not afraid of him .
If it have be Mr. Rattlesnake or Mr. Gophersnake , it would have be different .
But from little Mr. Greensnake there be nothing to fear , and sometimes , just for fun , Peter would jump right over him .
When he do that , Peter always wink good-naturedly .
But Mr. Greensnake never wink back .
Instead he would raise his head , run his tongue out at Peter , and hiss in what he try to make a very fierce and angry manner .
Then Peter would laugh and wink at him again .
But never once do Mr. Greensnake wink back .
-LSB- Illustration : He would make no reply , save to run out his tongue at them . -RSB-
Peter be think of this a he and Johnny Chuck stretch out in a sunny spot to get their breath and rest .
He have never think of it before , but now that he have notice it , he could n't remember that he ever have see little Mr. Greensnake wink , nor any of Mr. Greensnake 's relative .
He mention the matter to Johnny Chuck .
`` That 's so , '' reply Johnny thoughtfully .
`` I never have see any of them wink , either .
Do you suppose they can wink ? ''
`` Let 's go ask Mr. Greensnake , '' say Peter .
Up they hop and race over to the grassy tussock where Mr. Greensnake lay , but to all their question he would make no reply save to run out his tongue at them .
Finally they give up ask him .
`` I tell you what , let 's go over to the Smiling Pool and ask Grandfather Frog .
He 'll be sure to know , and perhaps , if he be feel good , he 'll tell u a story , '' say Peter .
So off they scamper to the Smiling Pool .
There they find Grandfather Frog sit on his big green lily-pad just a usual , and Peter knew by the look in his great , goggly eye that Grandfather Frog have a good breakfast of foolish green fly tuck away inside his white and yellow waistcoat .
His eye twinkle a Peter and Johnny very politely wish him good morning .
`` Good morning , '' say he gruffly .
But Peter have see that twinkle in his eye and know that Grandfather Frog be feel good-natured in spite of his gruff greeting .
`` If you please , Grandfather Frog , why do n't Mr. Greensnake wink at u when we wink at him ? ''
he ask .
`` Chug-a-rum !
Because he ca n't , '' reply Grandfather Frog .
`` Ca n't ! ''
cry Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck together .
`` That 's what I say -- ca n't , '' reply Grandfather Frog .
`` And no more can Mr. Blacksnake , or Mr. Rattlesnake , or Mr. Gophersnake , or any other member of the Snake family . ''
`` Why not ? ''
cry Peter and Johnny , all in the same breath .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog , fold his hand across his white and yellow waistcoat , `` if you will sit still until I finish , I 'll tell you ; but if you move or ask any foolish question , I 'll stop right where I be , and you 'll never hear the end of the story , for no one else know it . ''
Of course Peter and Johnny promise to sit perfectly still and not say a word .
After they have make themselves comfortable , Grandfather Frog clear his throat a if to begin , but for a long time he do n't say a word .
Once Peter open his mouth to ask why , but remember in time and close it again without make a sound .
