At last Grandfather Frog clear his throat once more , and with a far-away look in his great , goggly eye begin : `` Once upon a time , long , long ago , when the world be young , live old Mr. Snake , the grandfather a thousand time remove of little Mr. Greensnake and all the other Snakes whom you know .
Of course he be n't old then .
He be young and spry and smart , be Mr. Snake .
Now there be such a thing a be too smart .
That be the trouble with Mr. Snake .
Yes , Sir , that be the trouble with Mr. Snake .
He be so smart that he soon find out that he be the smart of all the meadow and forest people , and that be a bad thing .
It certainly be a very bad thing . ''
Grandfather Frog shake his head gravely .
`` You see , '' he continue , `` as soon a he find that out , he begin to take advantage of his neighbor and cheat them , but he would do it so smoothly that they never once suspect that they be be cheat .
Mr. Snake would go about all day cheat everybody he meet .
At night he would go home and chuckle over his smartness .
It be n't long before he begin to look down on his neighbor for be so honest that they do n't suspect other people of be dishonest , and for be so easily cheat .
`` Now one bad habit almost always lead to another .
From cheat , Mr. Snake just naturally slip to steal .
Yes , Sir , he become a thief .
Of course that make trouble right away , but still no one suspect Mr. Snake .
He be always very polite to every one and always offer to do favor for his neighbor .
In fact , Mr. Snake be very well like and much respect .
When any one have be rob , he be always the first to offer sympathy and join in the hunt for the thief .
He be so spry and slim , and could slip through the tall grass so fast , that he could go almost where he please without be see , and this make him very bold .
If he do happen to be find near the scene of trouble , he always have a story ready to account for his presence , and it sound so true , and he tell it in such an honest manner , that no one thought of doubt it .
`` So Mr. Snake find that lie help him to cheat and steal , and all the time he keep think how smart he be .
But even Mr. Snake have a little bit of conscience , and once in a while it would trouble him .
So what do you think he do ?
Why , cheating have become such a habit with him that he actually try to cheat himself -- to cheat his conscience !
When he be tell a lie , he would wink one eye .
` That , ' say he to himself , ` mean that it be n't true , and if these folk be not smart enough to see me wink and know what it mean , it be their own fault if they believe what I be tell them . '
But always he take care to wink the eye that be turn away from the one he be talk to .
`` Dear me , dear me , such terrible time a there be on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest !
They grow bad and bad , and when at last Old Mother Nature come to see how all the little people be get along , she hear so many complaint that she hardly know where to begin to straighten matter out .
She have all the little people come before her in turn and tell their trouble .
When it come Mr. Snake 's turn , he have no complaint to make .
He seem to be the only one who have no trouble .
She ask him a great many question , and for each one he have a ready reply .
Of course a great many of these reply be lie , and every time he tell one of these , he wink without know it .
You see , it have become a habit .
`` Now , with all his smartness , Mr. Snake have forget one thing , one very important thing .
It be this : You ca n't fool Old Mother Nature , and it be of no use to try .
He have n't be talk three minute before she know who be at the bottom of all the trouble .
She let him finish , then call all the others about her and tell them who have make all the trouble .
Mr. Snake be very bold .
He hold his head very high in the air and pretend not to care .
When Old Mother Nature turn her head , he even run out his tongue at her , just a all the Snake family do at you and me to-day .
When she have finish tell them how cheating and stealing and lying be n't smart at all , but very , very dreadful , she turn to Mr. Snake and say : '' ` From this time on , no one will believe anything you say , and you shall have no friend .
You will never wink again , for you and your child and your child 's child forever will have no eyelid , that all the world may know that those who make a wrong use of the thing give them shall have them take away . '
`` And now you know why little Mr. Greensnake can not wink at you ; he have n't any eyelid to wink with '' finish Grandfather Frog .
Peter Rabbit draw a long breath .
`` Thank you , oh , thank you ever so much , Grandfather Frog , '' he say .
`` Will you tell u next time why Bobby Coon wear ring on his tail ? ''
`` Perhaps , '' reply Grandfather Frog .
XI WHY BOBBY COON HAS RINGS ON HIS TAIL Peter Rabbit would give Grandfather Frog no peace .
Every day Peter visit the Smiling Pool to tease Grandfather Frog for a story -- for one particular story .
He want to know why it be that Bobby Coon wear ring on his tail .
You see , Peter have admire Bobby Coon 's tail for a long time .
Peter have such a funny little tail himself , just a little white bunch of cotton , that such a handsome tail a Bobby Coon 's sometimes stir just a wee bit of envy in Peter 's heart .
But it be n't envy so much a curiosity that prompt Peter to tease for that story .
Bobby Coon 's tail be very handsome , you know .
It have beautiful ring of black and gray , and Peter do n't know of any other tail at all like it .
Somehow , he felt right down deep in his heart that there must be a reason for those ring , just a there be a reason for his own long ear and long leg .
The more he think about it , the more he felt that he simply must know , and the only way he could find out be from Grandfather Frog , who be very old and very wise .
So he tease and he tease until finally Grandfather Frog promise him that on the next afternoon he would tell Peter why Bobby Coon have ring on his tail .
Peter hurry away to tell all the little meadow and forest people , and the next afternoon they be all on hand on the bank of the Smiling Pool to hear the story about Bobby Coon 's tail .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
begin Grandfather Frog , smooth down his white and yellow waistcoat .
`` Chug-a-rum !
Some folk seem to think that what they do do n't matter to anybody but themselves .
That be the way with old Mr. Rabbit , who live a long time ago when the world be young .
He think he could make all the trouble he please by his dreadful curiosity , and if he be find out , no one would suffer but himself .
But it be n't so .
Here be Peter Rabbit , his grandchild a thousand time remove , with long leg and long ear , and the bad habit of curiosity , all because old Mr. Rabbit have a bad habit and do n't try to overcome it .
`` It be the same way with old Mr. Coon .
He be dishonest and steal from Old King Bear .
Old Mother Nature punish him by put mustard in his food , and Mr. Coon think he be so smart that he could get ahead of Old Mother Nature by wash all his food before he eat it .
Old Mother Nature do n't say anything , but watch him and smile to herself .
You see , she know that Mr. Coon be begin a good habit , a very good habit indeed -- the habit of neatness .
So , though she know perfectly well that he be do it just to get ahead of her , she be glad , for she be fond of Mr. Coon in spite of the bad way he have grow into , and she know that good habit be like bad habit -- once start they grow and grow , and be very likely to lead to more good habit .
`` It be so with Mr. Coon .
He find that his food taste good for be so clean , and he grow very fussy about what he eat .
No matter where he find it or how tempting it look , he would n't eat it until he have carry it to the near water and wash it .
He still remember the mustard and try to fool himself into think that he be simply spit Old Mother Nature , but right down in his heart he know that even if he should be tell that never again would there be mustard in his food , he would wash it just the same .
`` One day , a he sit beside the Laughing Brook eat his supper , he notice that while his food have be wash clean , his hand be dirty .
They spoil his supper .
Yes , Sir , they spoil his supper . ''
` What good do it do to wash my food , if I eat it out of dirty hand ? '
say Mr. Coon to himself , and he hurry to a quiet little pool to give them a good scrubbing .
Then he wash his face and brush his coat .
` Now I feel well , and I know my supper will taste well , ' say he .
`` From that time he begin to be particular , very particular , about keep himself clean , until finally there be no one on the Green Meadows or in the Green Forest quite so neat a Mr. Coon .
`` Now at this time Mr. Coon have a very plain tail .
It be all of one color , a grayish white , not at all pretty .
Mr. Coon use to think a great deal about that tail and wish and wish that it be handsome .
Sometimes he use to envy Mr. Fox his beautiful red tail with it black and white tip .
One day , a he sit on an old log with his chin in his hand , think about his tail , who should come along but Old Mother Nature . ''
` Good morning , Mr. Coon , ' say she in her pleasant voice .
`` Mr. Coon get up and make a very low bow .
` Good morning , Mother Nature , ' he reply in his politest manner , which be very polite indeed . ''
` What be you think about so hard ? '
ask Old Mother Nature .
`` Mr. Coon look a little bit ashamed .
Then he sigh . '
I be wish that my tail be handsome , ' say he .
` But it be a very good tail a it be , ' he add hastily .
`` Old Mother Nature 's eye twinkle .
She sit down beside Mr. Coon and ask him all about his affair , just a if she do n't know all about them already .
She tell him how pleased she be to find him so neat and clean , and Mr. Coon just tingle all over with pleasure .
At last she get up to go , and her eye twinkle more than ever , a she say : '' ` By the way , Mr. Coon , I be so pleased with your neatness that I be leave you a reward .
I hope you will like it . '
`` Mr. Coon do n't see any reward , but he thank her just the same , and Old Mother Nature go on her way .
Mr. Coon watch her out of sight .
Then he sit down on the old log again and scratch his head thoughtfully a he look this way and that . '' '
I wonder what she mean by reward .
I do n't see any anywhere , ' he say to himself .
`` By and by he just happen to glance at his tail .
` Oh ! '
cried Mr. Coon , and then for a long time he could n't say another word , but just look and look with shin eye and such a queer feeling of happiness in his heart .
You see , Old Mother Nature have leave a beautiful , broad , black ring around his tail .
Mr. Coon could n't do anything the rest of that day but look at and admire that ring , until his neck ache from twist it around so long .
`` After that he be neater than ever , you may be sure , and the next time Old Mother Nature come around , she leave another handsome black ring on his tail , because he have n't grow careless , but have keep up his good habit .
`` Now about this time , hard time come to all the little people of the Green Forest and the Green Meadows .
Every one begin to grumble .
Mr. Bear grumble .
Mr. Fox grumble .
Mr. Rabbit grumble .
Mr. Jay grumble .
Mr. Squirrel grumble .
Even Mr. Chuck grumble .
And one and all they begin to blame Old Mother Nature .
Then they begin to quarrel among themselves and to steal from each other .
Some even leave their home and go out into the Great World to try to find a good place to live , only to find that the Great World be a hard place to live in than the Green Forest and the Green Meadows .
`` But Mr. Coon do n't grumble , and he do n't go away .
No , Sir , Mr. Coon just stick to his home and do the best he could to find enough to eat .
He keep himself as neat a ever and be always cheerful .
Whenever he meet one of his grumbling neighbor , he would say : '' ` Better time come !
Better time come !
Old Mother Nature be do the best she can .
Better time come ! '
`` The others would laugh at him for his faith in Old Mother Nature , and say ugly thing about her , and urge Mr. Coon to go with them out into the Great World .
But he keep right on mind his own business and keep neat and cheerful , until at last Old Mother Nature , all worried and troubled , come to see what she could do to straighten matter out .
It do n't take her long to find out how all the little meadow and forest people , except Mr. Coon , have grumble and be discontent and say ugly thing about her , for you ca n't fool Old Mother Nature , and it 's of no use to try .
Some she punish one way , and some she punish another way , for of course she have n't be to blame for the hard time , but have be work night and day to put an end to them .
`` Mr. Coon be the last to be call before her , and instead of be frown and cross , a she have be to the others , she be all smile .
She say a lot of nice thing to him , and when at last she send him away , what do you think she have give him ? ''
`` More ring , '' cry Peter Rabbit .
`` Yes , '' reply Grandfather Frog , `` Mr. Coon 's tail be ring way to the tip .
There be one for cheerfulness , and one for faith , and one for persistence in make the best of a bad matter and stay at home .
And ever since that long-ago day when the world be young , the Coons have be very proud of their beautiful tail and have keep up the good habit of old Mr. Coon .
Now you know , Peter Rabbit , why Bobby Coon wear ring on his tail , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
Peter give a long sigh .
`` I think it 's perfectly beautiful , '' he say .
`` I wish I have ring on my tail . ''
And then he wonder why everybody laugh .
XII WHY THERE IS A BLACK HEAD IN THE BUZZARD FAMILY Ol ' Mistah Buzzard have just tell the story of why he have a bald head and be proud of it .
You know he have n't a feather on it , and it be very , very red .
It be a very interesting story , and it have be listen to with the close attention by a lot of the little meadow and forest people .
Unc ' Billy Possum , who be Ol ' Mistah Buzzard 's particular friend , both have come from `` way down souf , '' happen along just in time to hear the end of it .
`` May Ah ask yo ' a question , Brer Buzzard ? ''
say he .
`` Cert ` nly , Brer Possum .
Cert ` nly , '' reply Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
`` Is Buzzard really your fam ` ly name ? ''
ask Unc ' Billy .
`` No , Brer Possum , it be n't , '' reply Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
Everybody look surprised .
You see , no one ever have hear him call anything but Buzzard .
But no one say anything , and after a minute or two Ol ' Mistah Buzzard explain .
`` Mah fam ` ly name be Vulture , '' say he .
`` Yes , Sah , mah fam ` ly name be Vulture , but we-uns do be call Buzzards so long , that Ah don ' know a Ah would know Ah be be speak to , if Ah be call Mistah Vulture . ''
`` An ' do Ah understand that all of your fam ` ly have red haids ? ''
inquired Unc ' Billy .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard look down at Unc ' Billy , and he saw a twinkle in Unc ' Billy 's shrewd little eye .
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard grin .
`` Ah know jes ' what yo ' do get in your mind , Brer Possum , '' say he .
`` It 's that trifle , no ` count cousin of mine .
He 's a Buzzard , or a Vulture , if yo ' like that good , jes ' like Ah be , but he belong to another branch of the fam ` ly .
He have a bald haid , jes ' like Ah have , but his haid be black instead of red .
That 's because his grandpap be trifle an ' po ' trash , jes ' like he be . ''
Peter Rabbit prick up his ear .
This sound like another story .
He be curious about that black-headed cousin of Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , very curious indeed .
He wonder if Ol ' Mistah Buzzard would have to be tease for a story , like Grandfather Frog .
Anyway , he would find out .
There would be no harm in try .
`` If you please , how do your cousin happen to have a black head ? ''
ask Peter as politely a he know how .
`` Because his grandpap ask too many question , '' reply Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , slyly wink at the others .
Everybody laugh , for everybody know that no one ask more question than Peter Rabbit .
Peter laugh with the rest , although he look a wee bit foolish .
But he do n't mean to give up just because he be laugh at .
Oh , my , no !
`` Please , Mr. Buzzard , please tell u the story , '' he beg .
Now Ol ' Mistah Buzzard be naturally good-natured and accommodating , and when Peter beg so hard , he just could n't find it in his heart to refuse .
Besides , he rather enjoy tell story .
So he shake his feather out , half spread his wing to let the air blow under them , look down at all the little meadow and forest people gather about the foot of the tall , dead tree where he delight to roost , grin at them in the funny way , and then begin this story : `` Way back in the day when Grandpap Buzzard have his lil fall out with ol ' King Eagle and do fly so high he sco ` tch the feather offen his haid , he have a cousin , do Grandpap Buzzard , and this cousin be jes ' naturally lazy and no ` count .
Like most no ` count people , he use to make a regular nuisance of hisself , poke his nose into ev ` ybody 's business and never ` tend to his own .
Was n't anything go on that this trifle member of the Buzzard fam ` ly do n't find out about and meddle in .
He could ask mo ' question than Peter Rabbit can , an ' anybody that can do that have get to ask a lot . ''
Everybody look at Peter and laugh .
Peter make a funny face and laugh too .
`` Seemed like he jes ' go ` round from mo ` ning to night ask question , '' continue Ol ' Mistah Buzzard , `` Got so that eve ` ybody dread to see that no ` count Buzzard coming , because he bind to pester with question about thing what do n't concern him no way .
`` Now yo ' know that way down in Ol ' Virginny where Ah do come from , mah fam ` ly do get the habit of sit on the top of chimney in the wintertime to warm their toe . ''
`` Why , I think it be warm down south ! ''
interrupt Peter Rabbit .
`` So it be , Brer Rabbit !
So it be ! ''
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard hasten to say .
`` But yo ' see , ol ' Jack Frost try to come down there sometimes , an ' he cool the air off a right smart lot before he turn tail an ' run back where he belong .
So we-uns sit on the chimney-tops whenever ol ' Jack Frost get to stray down where he have no business .
Yo ' see , if we-uns keep our toe warm , we-uns be warm all over .
`` One day this no ` count , trifle cousin of Grandpap Buzzard get cold in his foot .
He look ` round right smart fo ' a chimney fo ' to warm his toe , an ' pretty soon he see one where he never be before .
It be on a lil ol ' house , a lil ol ' tumble-down house .
Mistah Buzzard fly right over an ' sit on that chimney-top fo ' to warm his toe .
Of course he right smart curious about that lil ol ' tumble-down house and who live there .
He hear somebody inside talk to theirself , but he ca n't hear what they say , jes ' a mumbling sound that come up the chimney to him .
`` He listen an ' listen .
Then he shift ` round to the other side of the chimney an ' listen .
No matter where he sit , he ca n't hear what be say down inside that lil ol ' tumble-down house .
Then what do yo ' think Mistah Buzzard do ?
Why , he jes ' stretch his fool haid a far down that chimney a he can an ' listen an ' listen .
Yes , Sah , that be jes ' what that no ` count Buzzard do .
But all he hear be jes ' a mumbling and a mumbling , an ' that make him more curious than ever .
It seem to him that he must go clean outen his haid ` le he hear what go on down inside that lil ol ' house .
`` Now when he stretch his haid an ' neck down the chimney that way , he get 'em all black with soot .
But he do n't mind that .
No , Sah , he don ' mind that a bit .
Fact be , he don ' notice it .
He so curious he don ' notice anything , an ' pretty soon he plumb fo ` get where he be an ' that he be listen where he have no business .
He plumb fo ` get all about this , an ' he holler down that chimney .
Yes , Sah , he holler right down that chimney ! ''
` Will yo ' - alls please speak a lil louder , ' he holler down the chimney , jes ' like that .
`` Now the lil ol ' woman what live by herself in that lil ol ' tumble-down house have n't see that no ` count Buzzard light on the chimney fo ' to warm his toe , an ' when she hear that voice come right outen the fireplace , she be some flustrated and scar , be that lil ol ' woman .
Yes , Sah , she sho ` ly be plumb scared .
She so scar she tip over a whole kettleful of soup right in the fire .
Of course that make a terrible mess an ' a powerful lot of smoke an ' hot ash fly up the chimney .
They like to choke that no ` count Buzzard to death .
They burn the feather offen his haid an ' neck , an ' the soot make him black , all but his foot an ' laigs an ' the inside of his wing , which he keep close .
`` Mistah Buzzard he give a mighty squawk an ' fly away .
When he get home , he try an ' try to brush that soot off , but it do get into the skin an ' it stay there .
An ' from that day his haid an ' neck stay black , an ' he never speak lessen he speak to , an ' then he only grunt .
His chillen jes ' like him , an ' his chillen 's chillen the same way .
An ' that be the reason that mah cousin who live down souf do have a black haid , '' conclude Ol ' Mistah Buzzard .
A little sigh of satisfaction go around the circle of listener .
As usual , Peter Rabbit be the first to speak .
`` That be a splendid story , Mr. Buzzard , '' say he , `` and I 'm ever and ever so much oblige to you .
It be just as good a one of Grandfather Frog 's . ''
Ol ' Mistah Buzzard grin and slowly wink one eye at Unc ' Billy Possum a he reply : `` Thank yo ' , Brer Rabbit .
That 's quite the nice thing yo ' could say . ''
`` But it 's true ! ''
shout all together , and then everybody give three cheer for Ol ' Mistah Buzzard before start off to attend to their own private affair .
XIII WHY BUSTER BEAR APPEARS TO HAVE NO TAIL Peter Rabbit have something new to bother his bump of curiosity .
And it do bother it a lot .
He have just see Buster Bear for the first time , and what do you think have impress him most ?
Well , it be n't Buster 's great size , or wonderful strength , or big claw , or deep , grumbly-rumbly voice .
No , Sir , it be n't one of these .
It be the fact that Buster Bear seem to have no tail !
Peter could n't get over that .
He almost pity Buster Bear .
You see , Peter have a great admiration for fine tail .
He have always be rather ashamed of the funny little one he have himself .
Still , it be a real tail , and he have often comfort himself with that thought .
So the first thing Peter do when he saw Buster Bear be to look to see what kind of a tail he have .
Just imagine how surprised he be when he could n't make sure that Buster have any tail at all .
There be something that might , just might , be mean for a tail , and Peter be n't even sure of that .
If it be , it be so ridiculously small that Peter felt that he have no reason to be ashamed of his own tail .
He be still think about this when he start for home .
Half way there , he pause , saw that the way to the Smiling Pool be clear , and suddenly make up his mind to ask Grandfather Frog about Buster Bear 's tail .
Off he start , lipperty-lipperty-lip .
`` Oh , Grandfather Frog , '' he pant , as soon a he reach the edge of the Smiling Pool , `` have Buster Bear get a tail ? ''
Grandfather Frog regard Peter in silence for a minute or two .
Then very slowly he ask : `` What be your eye for , Peter Rabbit ?
Could n't you see whether or not he have a tail ? ''
`` No , Grandfather Frog .
I really could n't tell whether he have a tail or not , '' reply Peter quite truthfully .
`` At first I think he have n't , and then I think he might have .
If he have , it do n't seem to me that it be enough to call a really truly tail . ''
`` Well , it be a really truly tail , even if you do n't think so , '' retort Grandfather Frog , `` and he have it for a reminder . ''
`` A reminder ! ''
exclaim Peter , look very much puzzle .
`` A reminder of what ? ''
Grandfather Frog clear his throat two or three time .
`` Sit down , Peter , and learn a lesson from the tale of the tail of Old King Bear , '' say he very seriously .
`` You remember that once upon a time , long ago , when the world be young , Old King Bear rule in the Green Forest , and everybody bring tribute to him . ''
Peter nod and Grandfather Frog go on .
`` Now Old King Bear be the great-great-ever-so-great grandfather of Buster Bear , and he look very much a Buster do , except that he do n't have any tail at all , not the least sign of a tail .
At first , before he be make king of the Green Forest , he do n't mind this at all .
In fact , he be rather pleased that he do n't have a tail .
You see , he could n't think of any earthly use he would have for a tail , and so he be glad that he have n't get one to bother with .
`` This be just Old Mother Nature 's view of the matter .
She have do her very best to give everybody everything that they really need , and not to give them thing which they do n't need .
She could n't see that Mr. Bear have the least need of a tail , and so she have n't give him one .
Mr. Bear be perfectly happy without one , and be so busy get enough to eat that he do n't have time for silly thought or vain wish .
`` Then he be make king over all the people of the Green Forest , and his word be law .
It be a very great honor , and for a while he felt it so and do his best to rule wisely .
He go about just a before , hunt for his living , and have no more time than before for foolish thought or vain wish .
But after a little , the little people over whom he rule begin to bring him tribute , so that he no longer have to hunt for enough to eat .
Indeed , he have so much brought to him , that he could n't begin to eat all of it , and he grow very dainty and fussy about what he do eat .
Having nothing to do but eat and sleep , he grow very fat and lazy , a be the case with most people who have nothing to do .
He grow so fat that when he walk , he puff and wheeze .
He grow so lazy that he want to be wait on all the time .
`` It happen about this time that he overhear Mr. Fox talk to Mr. Wolf when they both think him asleep . '
A pretty kind of a king , he be ! '
sneer Mr. Fox .
` The idea of a king without a tail ! ' ''
` That 's so , ' assent Mr. Wolf .
` Why , even that little upstart , Mr. Rabbit , have get a make-believe tail . ' ''
Grandfather Frog 's eye twinkle a he say this , and Peter look very much embarrass .
But he do n't say anything , so Grandfather Frog go on .
`` Old King Bear pretend to wake up just then , and right away Mr. Fox and Mr. Wolf be a polite and smile a you please and begin to flatter him .
They tell him how proud they be of their king , and how handsome he be , and a lot of other nice thing , all of which he have hear often before and have believe .
He pretend to believe them now , but after they be through pay their respect and have go away , he keep turn over and over in his mind what he have overhear them say when they think he be asleep .
`` After that he could n't think of anything but the fact that he have n't any tail .
He take particular notice of all who come to pay him tribute , and he saw that every one of them have a tail .
Some have long tail ; some have short tail ; some have handsome tail and some have homely tails ; but everybody have a tail of some kind .
The more he try not to think of these tail , the more he do think of them .
The more he think of them , the more discontented he grow because he have none .
He do n't stop to think that probably all of them have use for their tail .
No , Sir , he do n't think of that .
Everybody else have a tail , and he have n't .
He felt that it be a disgrace that he , the king , should have no tail .
He brood over it so much that he lose his appetite and grow cross and peevish .
`` Then along come Old Mother Nature to see how thing be go in the Green Forest .
Of course she saw right away that something be wrong with Old King Bear .
When she ask him what the matter be , he be ashamed to tell her at first .
But after a little he tell her that he want a tail ; that he could never again be happy unless he have a tail .
She tell him that he have n't the least use in the world for a tail , and that he would n't be any happy if he have one .
Nothing that she could say make any difference -- he want a tail .
Finally she give him one .
`` For a few day Old King Bear be perfectly happy .
He spend all his spare time admire his new tail .
He call the attention of all his subject to it , and they all tell him that it be a very wonderful tail and be very become to him .
But it be n't long before he find that his new tail be very much in the way .
It bother him when he walk .
It be in the way when he sit down .
It be a nuisance when he climb a tree .
He do n't have a single use for it , and yet he have to carry it with him wherever he go .
Worse still , he overheard little Mr. Squirrel and Mr. Possum make fun of it .
And then he discover that the very one who admire his tail so to his face be laugh at him and poke fun at him behind his back .
`` And then Old King Bear wish that he have n't a tail more than ever he wish that he do have a tail .
Again he lose his appetite and grow cross and peevish , so that no one dare come near him .
So matter go from bad to worse , until once more Old Mother Nature visit the Green Forest to see how thing be .
Very humbly Old King Bear go down on his knee and beg her to take away his tail .
At first Old Mother Nature refuse , but he beg so hard and promise so faithfully never again to be discontent , that finally she relent and take away his tail , all but just a wee little bit .
That she leave a a reminder lest he should forget the lesson he have learn and should again grow envious .
-LSB- Illustration : `` Then Old King Bear wish that he have n't a tail . '' -RSB-
`` And every bear since that long-ago day have carry about with him a reminder -- you can hardly call it a real tail -- of the silly , foolish discontent of Old King Bear , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
Peter Rabbit scratch one long ear thoughtfully a he reply : `` Thank you , Grandfather Frog .
I think that hereafter I will be quite content with what I 've get and never want thing it be not meant that I should have . ''
XIV WHY FLITTER THE BAT FLIES AT NIGHT -LSB- Illustration : `` It must be fine to fly , '' think Peter .
`` I wish I could fly . '' -RSB-
Flitter the Bat make Peter Rabbit 's head dizzy .
Peter could n't help watch him .
He just have to .
It seem so wonderful that Flitter could really fly , that whenever he saw him , Peter have to stop and watch .
And then , a he saw Flitter twist and turn , fly high , fly low , and go round and round , Peter 's head would begin to swim and grow dizzy , and he wonder and wonder how it be that Flitter himself do n't grow dizzy .
`` It must be fine to fly , '' think Peter .
`` I wish I could fly .
If I could , I would n't spend all my time fly around the way Flitter do .
I 'd go on long journey and see the Great World .
I 'd fly way , way up in the blue , blue sky , the way Ol ' Mistah Buzzard do , where I could look down and see all that be go on in the Green Forest and on the Green Meadows .
And I 'd fly in the daytime , because there be more go on then .
I wonder , now , why it be that Flitter never come out until after jolly , round , red Mr. Sun have go to bed behind the Purple Hills .
I never see him in the daytime , and I do n't even know where he keep himself .
I never think of it before , but I wonder why it be that he fly only at night .
I believe I 'll ask Grandfather Frog the very next time I see him . ''
Now you know that once Peter Rabbit 's curiosity be arouse , it just have to be satisfy .
No sooner do he begin to wonder about Flitter the Bat than he could think of nothing else .
So he watch until the way be clear , and then he start for the Smiling Pool as fast a he could go , lipperty-lipperty-lip .
He hop he would find Grandfather Frog sit as usual on his big green lily-pad , and that he would be good-natured .
If he be n't feel good-natured , it would be of no use to ask him for a story .
When Peter reach the Smiling Pool he be disappoint , terribly disappointed .
The big green lily-pad be there , but there be no one sit on it .
Somehow the Smiling Pool do n't seem quite like itself without Grandfather Frog sit there watch for foolish green fly .
Peter 's face show just how disappointed he felt .
He be just go to turn away when a great , deep voice say : `` Chug-a-rum !
Where be your manner , Peter Rabbit , that you forget to speak to your elder ? ''
Peter star eagerly into the Smiling Pool , and presently he saw two great , goggly eye and the top of a green head , way out almost in the middle of the Smiling Pool .
It be Grandfather Frog himself , have his morning swim .
`` Oh , Grandfather Frog , I do n't see you at all ! ''
cry Peter , `` If I have , of course I would have speak .
The fact be , I -- I -- '' `` You want a story , '' finish Grandfather Frog for him .
`` You ca n't fool me , Peter Rabbit .
You come over here just to ask me for a story .
I know you , Peter !
I know you !
Well , what be it this time ? ''
`` If you please , '' reply Peter politely and happily , for he saw that Grandfather Frog be feel good-natured , `` why be it that Flitter the Bat fly only at night ? ''
Grandfather Frog climb out on his big green lily-pad and make himself comfortable .
Peter sit still and try not to show how impatient he felt .
Grandfather Frog take his time .
It tickle him to see how hard impatient Peter be try to be patient , and his big , goggly eye twinkle .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say he at last , with a suddenness that make Peter jump .
`` That 's very good , Peter , very good indeed !
Now I 'll tell you the story . ''
Of course he mean that Peter 's effort to keep still be very good , but Peter do n't know this , and he could n't imagine what Grandfather Frog meant .
However , what he care most about be the story , so he settle himself to listen , his long ear stand straight up , and his eye stretch wide open a he watch Grandfather Frog .
The latter clear his throat two or three time , each time a if he intend to begin right then .
It be one of Grandfather Frog 's little joke .
He do it just to tease Peter .
At last he really do begin , and the very first thing he do be to ask Peter a question .
`` What be the reason that you stay in the dear Old Briar-patch when Reddy Fox be around ? ''
`` So that he wo n't catch me , of course , '' reply Peter .
`` Very good , '' say Grandfather Frog .
`` Now , why do you go over to the sweet-clover patch every day ? ''
`` Why , because there be plenty to eat there , '' reply Peter , look very , very much puzzle .
`` Well , now you 've answer your own question , '' grunt Grandfather Frog .
`` Flitter fly at night because he be safe then , and because he can find plenty to eat . ''
`` Oh , '' say Peter , and his voice sound dreadfully disappointed .
He have find out what he have want to know , but he have n't have a story .
He fidget about and look very hard at Grandfather Frog , but the latter seem to think that he have tell Peter what he want to know , and that be all there be to it .
Finally Peter sigh , and it be such a heavy sigh !
Then very slowly he turn his back on the Smiling Pool and start to hop away .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog in his deepest , story-telling voice .
`` A long time ago when the world be young , the great-great-ever-so-great grandfather of Flitter the Bat first learn to fly . ''
`` I know ! ''
cry Peter eagerly .
`` You tell me about that , and it be a splendid story . ''
`` But when he learn to fly , he find that Old Mother Nature never give all her blessing to any single one of her little people , '' continue Grandfather Frog , without pay the least attention to Peter 's interruption .
`` Old Mr . Bat have wing ; something no other animal have , but he find that he could no longer run and jump .
He could just flop about on the ground , and be almost helpless .
Of course that mean that he could very easily be catch , and so the ground be no long a safe place for him .
But he soon find that he be not safe in the air in daytime .
Old Mr. Hawk could fly even faster than he , and Mr. Hawk be always watch for him .
At first , Mr . Bat do n't know what to do .
He do n't like to go to Old Mother Nature and complain that his new wing be not all that he have think they would be .
That would look a if he be ungrateful for her kindness in give him the wing . ''
` I 've get to think of some way out of my trouble myself , ' think old Mr . Bat .
` When I 'm sure that I ca n't , it will be time enough to go to Old Mother Nature . '
`` Now of course it be very hard to think when you be twist and dodge and turn in the air . ''
`` Of course ! ''
say Peter Rabbit , just a if he know all about it .
`` So Mr . Bat go look for a place where he could be quiet all by himself and think without danger of be gobble up for some one 's dinner , '' continue Grandfather Frog .
`` He fly and he fly and have almost give up hope of find any such place when he saw a cave .
It look very black inside , but it be big enough for Mr . Bat to fly into , and in he go .
He know that Mr. Hawk would never come in there , and when he find a little shelf up near the roof , he know that he be safe from any four-footed enemy who might follow him there .
It be just the place to rest and think .
So he rest , and while he rest , he think and think .
`` By and by he notice that it be grow dark outside .
` My goodness !
If I be go to get anything to eat to-day , I shall have to hurry , ' think he .
When he get outside , he find that Mr. Sun have go to bed .
So have all the bird , except Mr. Owl and Mr. Nighthawk .
Now Mr. Nighthawk do n't belong to the Hawk family at all , so there be nothing to fear from him .
Then Mr . Bat have a very pleasant surprise .
He find the air full of insect , ever so many more than in the daytime .
By be very smart and quick he catch a few before it be too dark for him to see .
They do n't fill his stomach , but they keep him from starve .
As he fly back to the cave , a great idea come to him , the idea for which he have be think so hard .
He would sleep day in the cave , where he be perfectly safe , and come out to hunt bug and insect just as soon a Mr. Hawk have go to bed !
Then he would be safe and would not have to complain to Old Mother Nature .
`` At first old Mr . Bat , who be n't old then , you know , have hard work to catch enough insect before it grow too dark , but he find that every night he could see a little long and a little good than the night before , until by and by he could see as well in the dusk a he use to see in the daytime .
Then he realize that Old Mother Nature have once more be very good to him , and that she have help him just a she always help those who help themselves .
She have give him night-seeing eye , and he no more have to go hungry .
`` Mr . Bat be very grateful , and from that day to this , Bats have be content to live in cave and fly in the evening .
You ask Flitter if it be n't so . ''
Peter grin .
`` He never stay in one place long enough for me to ask him anything , '' say he .
`` I 'm ever so much oblige for the story , Grandfather Frog .
It pay to make the best of what we have , do n't it ? ''
`` It certainly do .
Chug-a-rum !
It certainly do ! ''
reply Grandfather Frog .
XV WHY SPOTTY THE TURTLE CARRIES HIS HOUSE WITH HIM Spotty the Turtle sit on an old log on the bank of the Smiling Pool , take a sun-bath .
He have sit that way for the long time without once move .
Peter Rabbit have see him when he go by on his way to the Laughing Brook and the Green Forest to look for some one to pass the time of day with .
Spotty be still there when Peter return a long time after , and he do n't look a if he have move .

XVI WHY PADDY THE BEAVER HAS A BROAD TAIL Usually the thing that interest u most be something that we have n't get ourselves .
It be that way with Peter Rabbit .
Peter be not naturally envious .
Oh , my , no !
Peter be pretty well satisfied with what he have , which be quite a it should be .
There be only one thing with which Peter be really dissatisfied , and it be only once in a while , when he have n't much of anything else to think about , that he be dissatisfy with this .
Can you guess what it be ?
Well , it be his tail .
Yes , Sir , that be the one thing that ever really trouble Peter .
You see , Peter 's tail be , nothing but a funny little bunch of cotton , which do n't look like a tail at all .
The only time he ever see it be when he be back to the Smiling Pool and look over his shoulder at his reflection in the water , and then , of course , he really do n't see his tail itself .
So sometimes when Peter see the fine tail of his neighbor , a little bit of envy creep into his heart for just a little while .
Why , even little Danny Meadow Mouse have a real tail , short a it be .
And a for Happy Jack Squirrel and Reddy Fox and Bobby Coon and Jimmy Skunk , everybody know what beautiful tail they have .
Once Peter think about it so much that Grandfather Frog notice how sober he be and ask Peter what the trouble be .
When Peter tell him that it seem to him that Old Mother Nature have not be fair in give him such a foolish little tail when she have give others such beautiful one , Grandfather Frog just open his big mouth and laugh until he have to hold his side .
`` Why , Peter , '' say he , `` you look so sober , that I think you really have something to worry about .
What would you do with a big tail , if you have one ?
It would always be in your way .
Just think how many time Reddy Fox or old Granny Fox have almost catch you .
They certainly would have before this , if you have have a long tail stick out behind for them to get hold of .
I have a long tail when I be young , and I be mighty glad to get rid of it . ''
After he hear that , Peter felt well .
But he do n't lose interest in tail , and he spend a great deal of time in wonder why some of his neighbor have big , bushy tail and some have long , slim tail and why he himself have almost no tail at all .
So when Paddy the Beaver come to live in the Green Forest , and make a pond there by build a wonderful dam across the Laughing Brook , the first thing Peter look to see be what kind of a tail Paddy have , and the first time he get a good look at it , his eye pop almost out of his head .
He just star and star .

All he could think of be that great , broad , flat , thick tail , which be so unlike any tail he have ever see or hear of .

Grandfather Frog 's big , goggly eye twinkle .

And he believe in help himself , do Mr. Beaver , and not in leave everything to Old Mother Nature , a do most of his neighbor .

You see , Old Mother Nature always help those who help themselves .

I THE MERRY LITTLE BREEZES SAVE THE GREEN MEADOWS Old Mother West Wind 's family be very big , very big indeed .
There be dozen and dozen of Merry Little Breezes , all child of Old Mother West Wind .
Every morning she come down from the Purple Hills and tumble them out of a great bag on to the Green Meadows .
Every night she gather them into the great bag and , put it over her shoulder , take them to their home behind the Purple Hills .
One morning , just a usual , Old Mother West Wind turn the Merry Little Breezes out to play on the Green Meadows .
Then she hurry away to fill the sail of the ship and blow them across the great ocean .
The Merry Little Breezes hop and skip over the Green Meadows look for some one to play with .
It be then that one of them discover something -- something very dreadful .
It be a fire !
Yes , Sir , it be a fire in the meadow grass !
Some one have drop a lighted match , and now little red flame be run through the grass in all direction .
The Merry Little Breeze hasten to tell all the other Little Breezes and all rush over as fast a they could to see for themselves .
They saw how the little red flame be turn to smoke and ash everything they touch , and how black and ugly , with nothing alive there , become that part of the Green Meadows where the little flame run .
It be dreadful !
Then one of them notice that the little red flame be run in the direction of Johnny Chuck 's new house .
Would the little red flame burn up Johnny Chuck , a they burn up the grass and the flower ?
`` Hi ! ''
cry the Merry Little Breeze , `` We must warn Johnny Chuck and all the other little meadow people ! ''
So he catch up a capful of smoke and race off as fast a he could go to Johnny Chuck 's house .
Then each of the Merry Little Breezes catch up a capful of smoke and start to warn one of the little meadow people or forest folk .
So pretty soon jolly , round , red Mr. Sun , look down from the blue sky , saw Johnny Chuck , Jimmy Skunk , Peter Rabbit , Striped Chipmunk , Danny Meadow Mouse , Reddy Fox , Bobby Coon , Happy Jack Squirrel , Chatterer the Red Squirrel , Jumper the Hare and old Mr. Toad all hurry as fast a they could to the Smiling Pool where live Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat and Spotty the Turtle and Grandfather Frog .
There they would be quite safe from the little red flame .
`` Oh , '' gasp Johnny Chuck , puff very hard , for you know he be round and fat and roly-poly and it be hard work for him to run , `` what will become of my nice new house and what will there be leave to eat ? ''
The Merry Little Breeze who have bring him the warning in a capful of smoke think for a minute .
Then he call all the other Little Breezes to him .
`` We must get Farmer Brown 's help or we will have no beautiful Green Meadows to play on , '' say the Merry Little Breeze .
So together they rush back to where the little red flame have grow into great , angry , red flame that be lick up everything in their way .
The Merry Little Breezes gather a great cloud of smoke and , lift all together , they carry it over and drop it in Farmer Brown 's dooryard .
Then one of them blow a little of the smoke in at an open window , near which Farmer Brown be eat breakfast .
Farmer Brown cough and strangle and sprang from his chair .
`` Phew ! ''
cry Farmer Brown , `` I smell smoke !
There must be a fire on the meadow . ''
Then he shout for his boy and for his hired man and the three , with shovel in their hand , start for the Green Meadows to try to put the fire out .
The Merry Little Breezes sigh with relief and follow to the fire .
But when they saw how fierce and angry the red flame have become they know that Farmer Brown and his boy and his hired man would not be able to put the fire out .
Choking with smoke , they hurry over to tell the dreadful news to the little meadow people and forest folk gather at the Smiling Pool .
`` Chug-a-rum !
Why do n't you help put the fire out ? ''
ask Grandfather Frog .
`` We warn Farmer Brown and his boy and his hired man ; what more can we do ? ''
ask one of the Merry Little Breezes .
`` Go find and drive up a rain cloud , '' reply Grandfather Frog .
`` Splendid ! ''
cry all the little meadow people and forest folk .
`` Hurry !
hurry !
Oh , do hurry ! ''
So the Merry Little Breezes scatter in all direction to hunt for a rain cloud .
`` It be a good thing that Old Mother West Wind have such a big family , '' say Grandfather Frog , `` for one of them be sure to find a wandering rain cloud somewhere . ''
Then all the little meadow people and forest folk sit down around the Smiling Pool to wait .
They watch the smoke roll up until it hide the face of jolly , round , red Mr. Sun .
Their heart almost stand still with fear a they saw the fierce , angry , red flame leap into the air and climb tall tree on the edge of the Green Forest .
Splash !
Something strike in the Smiling Pool right beside Grandfather Frog 's big , green , lily-pad .
Spat !
Something hit Johnny Chuck right on the end of his funny little , black nose .
They be drop of water .
`` Hurrah ! ''
cry Johnny Chuck , whirl about .
Sure enough , they be drop of water -- rain drop .
And there , come just as fast a the Merry Little Breezes could push it , and they be push very hard , very hard indeed , be a great , black , rain cloud , spill down rain a it come .
When it be just over the fire , the great , black , rain cloud split wide open , and the water pour down so that the fierce , angry , red flame be drown in a few minute .
`` Phew ! ''
say Farmer Brown , mop his face with his handkerchief , `` that be warm work !
That shower come up just in time and it be lucky it do . ''
But you know and I know and all the little meadow people and forest folk know that it be n't luck at all , but the quick work and hard work of Old Mother West Wind 's big family of Merry Little Breezes , which save the Green Meadows .
And this , too , be one reason why Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck and Bobby Coon and all the other little meadow and forest people love the Merry Little Breezes who play every day on the Green Meadows .
II THE STRANGER IN THE GREEN FOREST Old Mother West Wind , hurry down from the Purple Hills with her Merry Little Breezes , discover the newcomer in the Green Forest on the edge of the Green Meadows .
Of course the Merry Little Breezes saw him , too , and as soon a Old Mother West Wind have turn them loose on the Green Meadows they start out to spread the news .
As they hurry along the Crooked Little Path up the hill , they meet Reddy Fox .
`` Oh , Reddy Fox , '' cry the Merry Little Breezes , so excited that all talk together , `` there 's a stranger in the Green Forest ! ''
Reddy Fox sit down and grin at the Merry Little Breezes .
The grin of Reddy Fox be not pleasant .
It irritate and exasperate .
It make the Merry Little Breezes feel very uncomfortable .
`` You do n't say so , '' drawl Reddy Fox .

He be big , much big than Reddy .
Could he be a relative of Happy Jack Squirrel ?
He do n't look a bit , not the least little bit like Happy Jack .
And he move slowly , very slowly , indeed , while Happy Jack and his cousin move quickly .
Reddy decide that the stranger could not be relate to Happy Jack .
The long Reddy look the more he be puzzle .
Also , Reddy begin to feel just a little bit jealous .
You see all the little meadow people and forest folk be afraid of Reddy Fox , but this stranger be so big that Reddy begin to feel something very like fear in his own heart .
The Merry Little Breezes have tell the news to Jimmy Skunk and then hurry over the Green Meadows telling every one they meet of the stranger in the Green Forest -- Billy Mink , Little Joe Otter , Johnny Chuck , Peter Rabbit , Happy Jack Squirrel , Danny Meadow Mouse , Striped Chipmunk , old Mr. Toad , Grandfather Frog , Sammy Jay , Blacky the Crow , and each as soon a he hear the news start for the Green Forest to welcome the newcomer .
Even Grandfather Frog leave his beloved big , green lily-pad and start for the Green Forest .
So it be that when finally the stranger decide that he have eat enough bark for his breakfast , and climb slowly down the tall maple , he find all the little meadow people and forest folk sit in a big circle wait for him .
The stranger be anything but handsome , but his size fill them with respect .
The nearer he get to the ground the big he look .
Down he come , and Reddy Fox , note how slow and clumsy in his movement be the stranger , decide that there be nothing to fear .
If the stranger be slow and clumsy in the tree , he be clumsy still on the ground .
His eye be small and dull .
His coat be rough , long and almost black .
His leg be short and stout .
His tail be rather short and broad .
Altogether he be anything but handsome .
But when the little meadow people and forest folk saw his huge front teeth they regard him with great respect than ever , all but Reddy Fox .
Reddy strut out in front of him .
`` Who be you ? ''
he demand .

The stranger pay no attention to Reddy Fox .
