demand Reddy , show all his teeth .
The stranger just grunt and appear not to see Reddy Fox .
Reddy swell himself out until every hair stand on end and he look twice as big a he really be .
He strut back and forth in front of the stranger .
`` Do n't you know that I 'm afraid of nothing and nobody ? ''
snarl Reddy Fox .
The stranger refuse to give him so much a a glance .
He just grunt and keep right on about his business .
All the little meadow people and forest folk begin to giggle and then to laugh .
Reddy know that they be laugh at him and he grow very angry , for no one like to be laugh at , least of all Reddy Fox .
`` You 're a pig ! ''
taunt Reddy .
`` You 're afraid to fight .
I bet you 're afraid of Danny Meadow Mouse ! ''
Still the stranger just grunt and pay no further attention to Reddy Fox .
Now , with all his boast Reddy Fox have keep at a safe distance from the stranger .
Happy Jack Squirrel have notice this .
`` If you 're so brave , why do n't you drive him out , Reddy Fox ? ''
ask Happy Jack , skip behind a tree .
`` You do n't dare to ! ''
Reddy turn and glare at Happy Jack .
`` I 'm not afraid ! ''
he shout .
`` I 'm not afraid of anything nor anybody ! ''
But though he speak so bravely it be notice that he go no nearer the stranger .
Now it happen that that morning Bowser the Hound take it into his head to take a walk in the Green Forest .
Blacky the Crow , sit on the tip-top of a big pine , be the first to see him come .
From pure love of mischief Blacky wait until Bowser be close to the circle around the stranger .
Then he give the alarm .
`` Here 's Bowser the Hound !
Run ! ''
scream Blacky the Crow .
Then he laugh so that he have to hold his side to see the fright down below .
Reddy Fox forget that he be afraid of nothing and nobody .
He be the first one out of sight , run so fast that his foot seem hardly to touch the ground .
Peter Rabbit turn a back somersault and suddenly remember that he have important business down on the Green Meadows .
Johnny Chuck dodge into a convenient hole .
Billy Mink run into a hollow tree .
Striped Chipmunk hid in an old stump .
Happy Jack Squirrel climb the near tree .
In a twinkle the stranger be alone , face Bowser the Hound .
Bowser stop and look at the stranger in sheer surprise .
Then the hair on the back of his neck stand on end and he growl a deep , ugly growl .
Still the stranger do not run .
Bowser do n't know just what to make of it .
Never before have he have such an experience .
Could it be that the stranger be not afraid of him ?
Bowser walk around the stranger , growl fiercely .
As he walk the stranger turn , so a always to face him .
It be perplex and very provoking .
It really seem a if the stranger have no fear of him .
`` Bow , wow , wow ! ''
cry Bowser the Hound in his deepest voice , and sprang at the stranger .
Then something happen , so surprising that Blacky the Crow lose his balance on the top of the pine where he be watch .
The instant that Bowser sprang , the stranger roll himself into a tight round ball and out of the long hair of his coat sprang hundred of sharp little yellowish white barbed spear .
The stranger look for all the world like a huge black and yellow chestnut burr .
Bowser the Hound be as surprised a Blacky the Crow .
He stop short and his eye look a if they would pop out of his head .
He look so puzzled and so funny that Happy Jack Squirrel laugh aloud .
The stranger do not move .
Bowser back away and begin to circle around again , sniff and snuff .
Once in a while he bark .
Still the stranger do not move .
For all the sign of life he make he might in truth have be a giant chestnut burr .
Bowser sit down and look at him .
Then he walk around to the other side and sit down .
`` What a queer thing , '' think Bowser .
`` What a very queer thing . ''
Bowser take a step nearer .
Then he take another step .
Nothing happen .
Finally Bowser reach out , and with his nose gingerly touch the prickly ball .
Slap !
The stranger 's tail have strike Bowser full in the face .
Bowser yell with pain and roll over and over on the ground .
Sticking in his tender lip be a dozen sharp little spear , and claw and rub at them a he would , Bowser could not get them out .
Every time he touch them he yelp with pain .
Finally he give it up and start for home with his tail between his leg like a whipped puppy , and with every step he yelp .
When he have disappear and his yelp have die away in the distance , the stranger unroll , the sharp little spear disappear in the long hair of his coat and , just a if nothing at all have happen , the stranger walk slowly over to a tall maple and begin to climb it .
And this be how Prickly Porky the Porcupine come to the Green Forest , and win the respect and admiration of all the little meadow people and forest folk , include Reddy Fox .
Since that day no one have try to meddle with Prickly Porky or his business .
III HOW PRICKLY PORKY GOT HIS QUILLS The newcomer in the Green Forest be a source of great interest to the Merry Little Breezes .
Ever since they have see him turn himself into a huge prickly ball , like a giant chestnut burr , and with a slap of his tail send Bowser the Hound yelping home with his lip stick full of little barbed spear , they have visit the Green Forest every day to watch Prickly Porky .
He be not very social .
Indeed , he be not social at all , but attend strictly to his own business , which consist chiefly of strip bark from the tree and eat it .
Never have the Merry Little Breezes see such an appetite !
Already that part of the Green Forest where he have choose to live have many bare stark tree , kill that Prickly Porky the Porcupine might live .
You see a tree can not live without bark , and Prickly Porky have strip them clean to fill his stomach .
But if Prickly Porky be not social he be not unfriendly .
He seem to enjoy have the Merry Little Breezes about , and do not in the least mind have them rumple up the long hair of his coat to feel the sharp little barbed spear underneath .
Some of these be so loose that they drop out .
Peter Rabbit 's curiosity lead him to examine some of these among bit of bark at the foot of a tree .
Peter wish that he have leave them alone .
One of the sharp little barb pierce his tender skin and Peter could not get it out .
He have to ask Johnny Chuck to do it for him , and it have hurt dreadfully .
After that the little meadow people and forest folk hold Prickly Porky in great respect than ever and leave him severely alone , which be just what he seem to want .
One morning the Merry Little Breezes fail to find Prickly Porky in the Green Forest .
Could he have leave as mysteriously a he have come ?
They hurry down to the Smiling Pool to tell Grandfather Frog .
Bursting through the bulrush on the edge of the Smiling Pool , they nearly upset Jerry Muskrat , who be sit on an old log intently watch something out in the middle of the Smiling Pool .
It be Prickly Porky .
Some of the sharp little barbed spear be stand on end ; altogether he be the queer sight the Smiling Pool have see for a long time .
He be swim easily and you may be sure no one try to bother him .
Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink sit on the Big Rock and for once they have forget to play trick .
When Prickly Porky head towards the Big Rock , Little Joe Otter suddenly remember that he have business down the Laughing Brook , and Billy Mink recall that Mother Mink have forbid him to play at the Smiling Pool .
Prickly Porky have the Smiling Pool quite to himself .
When he have swim to his heart 's content he climb out , shake himself and slowly amble up the Lone Little Path to the Green Forest .
The Merry Little Breezes watch him out of sight .
Then they dance over to the big green lily-pad on which sit Grandfather Frog .
The Merry Little Breezes be great favorite with Grandfather Frog .
As usual they bring him some foolish green fly .
Grandfather Frog 's eye twinkle a he snap up the last foolish green fly .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog , `` and now I suppose you want a story . ''
And he fold his hand across his white and yellow waistcoat .
`` If you please ! ''
shout the Merry Little Breezes .
`` If you please , do tell u how it be that Prickly Porky have spear on his back ! ''
Grandfather settle himself comfortably .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say he .
`` Once upon a time when the world be young , Mr. Porcupine , the grandfather a thousand time remove of Prickly Porky , whom you all know , live in the Green Forest where old King Bear rule .
Mr. Porcupine be a slow clumsy fellow , just a his grandson a thousand time remove be to-day .
He be so slow moving , and when he try to hurry tumble over himself so much , that he have hard work to get enough to eat .
Always some one reach the berry patch before he do .
The beetle and the bug be so spry that seldom could he catch them .
Hunger be in his stomach , and little else most of the time .
Mr. Porcupine grow thin and thinner and still more thin .
His long , shaggy coat look twice too big for him .
Because he be so hungry he could sleep little , and night as well a day he roam the forest , think of nothing but his empty stomach , and look for something to put in it .
So he learn to see by night as well a by day .
`` One day he could not find a single berry and not a beetle or a bug could he catch .
He be so hungry that he sit down with his back against a big black birch , and clasp both hand over his lean stomach , he weep .
There Sister South Wind find him , and her heart be move to pity , for she know that his wit be as slow a his body .
Softly she steal up behind him . ''
` Try the bark of the black birch ; it 's sweet and good , ' whisper Sister South Wind .
Then she hurry on her way .
`` Mr. Porcupine still sit with his hand clasp over his lean stomach , for it take a long time for his slow wit to understand what Sister South Wind meant .
` Bark , bark , try bark , ' say Mr. Porcupine over and over to himself .
He roll his dull little eye up at the big black birch . '
I believe I will try it , ' say Mr. Porcupine at last .
`` Slowly he turn and begin to gnaw the bark of the big black birch .
It be tough , but it taste good .
Clumsily he begin to climb , tear off a mouthful of bark here and there a he climb .
The high he get the tenderer and sweeter the bark become .
Finally he reach the top of the tree , and there on the small branch the bark be so tender and so sweet that he eat and eat and eat until for the first time in many day Mr. Porcupine have a full stomach .
That night he curl up in a hollow log and sleep all the night through , dreaming of great forest of black birch and all he want to eat .
`` The next day he hunt for and find another black birch , and climb to the top , he eat and eat until his stomach be full .
From that time on Mr. Porcupine cease to hunt for berry or beetle or bug .
He grow stout and stouter .
He fill his shaggy coat until it be so tight it threaten to burst .
`` Now while Mr. Porcupine be so thin and lean he have no enemy , but when he grow stout and then fat , Mr. Panther and Mr. Fisher and Mr. Bobcat and even old King Bear begin to cast longing eye upon him , for time be hard and they be hungry .
Mr. Porcupine begin to grow afraid .
By night he hide in hollow tree and by day he go abroad to eat only when he be sure that no one big than himself be about .
And because he no longer dare to move about a before , he no longer depend upon the black birch alone , but learn to eat and to like all kind of bark .
`` One day he have make his breakfast on the bark of a honey-locust .
When he come down the tree he bring with him a strip of bark , and attach to it be some of the long thorn with which the honey-locust seek to protect itself .
When he reach the ground whom should he find wait for him but Mr. Panther .
Mr. Panther be very lean and very hungry , for hunt have be poor and the time be hard . ''
` Good morning , Mr. Porcupine , ' say Mr. Panther , with a wicked grin .
` How fat you be ! ' ''
` Good morning , Mr. Panther , ' say Mr. Porcupine politely , but his long hair stand on end with fright , a he look into Mr. Panther 's cruel yellow eye . '' '
I say , how fat you be , ' say Mr. Panther , lick his chop and show all his long teeth .
` What do you find to eat these hard time ? ' ''
` Bark , Mr. Panther , just bark , ' say Mr. Porcupine , while his teeth chatter with fear .
` It really be very nice and sweet .
Wo n't you try a piece , Mr. Panther ? '
Mr. Porcupine hold out the strip of locust bark which he have bring down the tree for his lunch .
`` Now Mr. Panther have never try bark , but he think to himself that if it make Mr. Porcupine so fat it must be good .
He would try the piece of bark first and eat Mr. Porcupine afterward .
So he reach out and snap up the strip of bark .
`` Now the locust thorn be long and they be sharp .
They pierce Mr. Panther 's tender lip and his tongue .
They stick in the roof of his mouth .
Mr. Panther spat and yell with pain and rage and claw frantically at his mouth .
He roll over and over try to get rid of the thorn .
Mr. Porcupine do n't stay to watch him .
For once in his life he hurry .
By the time Mr. Panther be rid of the last thorn , Mr. Porcupine be nowhere to be see .
He be safely hidden inside a hollow log .
`` Mr. Porcupine do n't sleep that night .
He just lay and think and think and think .
The next morning , very early , before any one else be astir , he start out to call on old Mother Nature . ''
` Good morning , Mr. Porcupine , what bring you out so early ? '
ask old Mother Nature .
`` Mr. Porcupine bow very low .
` If you please , Mother Nature , I want you to help me , ' say he .
`` Then he tell her all about his meeting with Mr. Panther and how helpless he be when he meet his enemy , and he beg her to give him stout claw and a big mouth full of long teeth that he might protect himself .
`` Old Mother Nature think a few minute .
` Mr. Porcupine , ' say she , ` you have always mind your own business .
You do not know how to fight .
If I should give you a big mouth full of long teeth you would not know how to use them .
You move too slowly .
Instead , I will give you a thousand little spur .
They shall be hide in the long hair of your coat and only when you be in danger shall you use them .
Go back to the Green Forest , and the next time you meet Mr. Panther or Mr. Fisher or Mr. Bobcat or old King Bear roll yourself into a ball and the thousand little spear will protect you .
Now go ! '
`` Mr. Porcupine thank old Mother Nature and start back for the Green Forest .
Once he stop to smooth down his long , rough coat .
Sure enough , there , under the long hair , he felt a thousand little spear .
He go along happily until suddenly he meet Mr. Panther .
Yes , Sir , he meet Mr. Panther .
`` Mr. Panther be feel very ugly , for his mouth be sore .
He grin wickedly when he saw Mr. Porcupine and step right out in front of him , all the time lick his lip .
Mr. Porcupine tremble all over , but he remember what old Mother Nature have tell him .
In a flash he have roll up into a tight ball .
Sure enough , the thousand little spear spring out of his long coat , and he look like a huge chestnut burr .
`` Mr. Panther be so surprised he do n't know just what to do .
He reach out a paw and touch Mr. Porcupine .
Mr. Porcupine be nervous .
He switch his tail around and it strike Mr. Panther 's paw .
Mr. Panther yell , for there be spear on Mr. Porcupine 's tail and they be bad than the locust thorn .
He back away hurriedly and limp off up the Lone Little Path , growl horribly .
Mr. Porcupine wait until Mr. Panther be out of sight , then he unroll , and slowly and happily he walk back to his home in the Green Forest .
`` And since that long-ago day when the world be young , the Porcupines have fear nothing and have attend strictly to their own business .
And that be how they happen to have a thousand little barbed spear , which be call quill , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
The Merry Little Breezes draw a long breath .
`` Thank you , Grandfather Frog , thank you ever so much ! ''
they cry all together .
`` We be go back now to tell Prickly Porky that we know all about his little spear and how he happen to have them . ''
But first they blow a dozen fat , foolish , green fly over to Grandfather Frog .
IV PETER RABBIT 'S EGG ROLLING It be spring .
Drummer the Woodpecker be beat the long roll on the hollow limb of the old hickory , that all the world might know .
Old Mother West Wind , hurry down from the Purple Hills across the Green Meadows , stop long enough to kiss the smile little bluets that crowd along the Lone Little Path .
All up and down the Laughing Brook be shy violet turn joyful face up to jolly , round , red Mr. Sun .
Johnny Chuck be sit on his doorstep , stretch one short leg and then another , to get the kink out , after his long , long winter sleep .
Very beautiful , very beautiful indeed , be the Green Meadows , and very happy be all the little meadow people -- all but Peter Rabbit , who sit at the top of the Crooked Little Path that wind down the hill .
No , Sir , Peter Rabbit , happy-go-lucky Peter , who usually carry the light heart on the Green Meadows , be not happy .
Indeed , he be very unhappy .
As he sit there at the top of the Crooked Little Path and look down on the Green Meadows , he saw nothing beautiful at all because , why , because his big soft eye be full of tear .
Splash !
A big tear fell at his foot in the Crooked Little Path .
Splash !
That be another tear .
Splash !
splash !
`` My gracious !
My gracious !
What be the matter , Peter Rabbit ? ''
ask a gruff voice close to one of Peter 's long ear .
Peter jump .
Then he wink the tear back and look around .
There sit old Mr. Toad .
He look very solemn , very solemn indeed .
He be wear a shabby old suit , the very one he have sleep in all winter .
Peter forget his trouble long enough to wonder if old Mr. Toad would swallow his old clothes when he get a new suit .
`` What 's the matter , Peter Rabbit , what 's the matter ? ''
repeat old Mr. Toad .
Peter look a little foolish .
He hesitate , cough , look this way and look that way , hitch his trouser up , and then , why then he find his tongue and tell old Mr. Toad all his trouble .
`` You see , '' say Peter Rabbit , `` it 's almost Easter and I have n't find a single egg . ''
`` An egg ! ''
exclaim old Mr. Toad .
`` Bless my star !
What do you want of an egg , Peter Rabbit ?
You do n't eat egg . ''
`` I do n't want just one egg , oh , no , no indeed !
I want a lot of egg , '' say Peter .
`` You see , Mr. Toad , I be go to have an Easter egg rolling , and here it be almost Easter and not an egg to be find ! ''
Peter 's eye fill with tear again .
Old Mr. Toad roll one eye up at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun and wink .
`` Have you see Mrs. Grouse and Mrs. Pheasant ? ''
ask old Mr. Toad .
`` Yes , '' say Peter Rabbit , `` and they wo n't have any egg until after Easter . ''
`` Have you be to see Mrs. Quack ? ''
ask old Mr. Toad .
`` Yes , '' say Peter Rabbit , `` and she say she ca n't spare a single one . ''
Old Mr. Toad look very thoughtful .
He scratch the tip of his nose with his left hind foot .
Then he wink once more at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun .
`` Have you be to see Jimmy Skunk ? ''
he inquire .
Peter Rabbit 's big eye open very wide .
`` Jimmy Skunk ! ''
he exclaim .
`` Jimmy Skunk !
What do Jimmy Skunk have to do with egg ? ''
Old Mr. Toad chuckle deep down in his throat .
He chuckle and chuckle until he shake all over .
`` Jimmy Skunk know more about eggs than all the other little meadow people put together , '' say old Mr. Toad .
`` You take my advice , Peter Rabbit , and ask Jimmy Skunk to help you get the egg for your Easter egg roll . ''
Then old Mr. Toad pick up his cane and start down the Crooked Little Path to the Green Meadows .
There he find the Merry Little Breezes steal kiss from the bashful little wind flower .
Old Mr. Toad puff out his throat and pretend that he disapprove , disapprove very much indeed , but at the same time he roll one eye up at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun and wink .
`` Have n't you anything good to do than make bashful little flower hang their head ? ''
ask old Mr. Toad gruffly .
The Merry Little Breezes stop their dancing and gather about old Mr. Toad .
`` What 's the matter with you this morning , Mr. Toad ? ''
ask one of them .
`` Do you want u to go find a breakfast for you ? ''
`` No , '' reply old Mr. Toad sourly .
`` I be quite able to get breakfast for myself .
But Peter Rabbit be up on the hill cry because he can not find any egg . ''
`` Crying because he can not find any egg !
Now what do Peter Rabbit want of egg ? ''
cry the Merry Little Breezes all together .
`` Supposing you go ask him , '' reply old Mr. Toad tartly , once more pick up his cane and start for the Smiling Pool to call on his cousin , Grandfather Frog .
The Merry Little Breezes star after him for a few minute , then they start in a mad race up the Crooked Little Path to find Peter Rabbit .
He be n't at the top of the Crooked Little Path .
They look everywhere , but not so much a the tip of one of his long ear could they see .
Finally they meet him just come away from Jimmy Skunk 's house .
Peter be hop , skip , jump up in the air and kick his long heel a only Peter can .
There be no trace of tear in his big , soft eye .
Plainly Peter Rabbit be in good spirit , in the very best of spirit .
When he saw the Merry Little Breezes he jump twice as high a he have jump before , then sit up very straight .
`` Hello ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` Hello yourself , '' reply the Merry Little Breezes .
`` Tell u what under the sun you want of egg , Peter Rabbit , and we 'll try to find some for you . ''
Peter 's eye sparkle .
`` I 'm go to have an Easter egg rolling , '' say he , `` but you need n't look for any egg , for I be go to have all I want ; Jimmy Skunk have promise to get them for me . ''
`` What be an Easter egg roll ? ''
ask the Merry Little Breezes .
Peter look very mysterious .
`` Wait and see , '' he reply .
Then a sudden thought pop into his head .
`` Will you do something for me ? ''
he ask .
Of course the Merry Little Breezes be delight to do anything they could for Peter Rabbit , and tell him so .
So in a few minute Peter have them scatter in every direction with invitation to all the little people of the Green Meadows and all the little folk of the Green Forest to attend his egg roll on Easter morning .
Very , very early on Easter morning Old Mother West Wind hurry down from the Purple Hills and sweep all the rain cloud out of the sky .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun climb up in the sky , smile his broad .
All the little song bird sing their sweetest , and some who really can not sing at all try to just because they be so happy .
Across the beautiful Green Meadows come all the little meadow people and forest folk to the smooth , grassy bank where the big hickory grows .
Peter Rabbit be there wait for them .
He have brush his clothes until you would hardly have know him .
He felt very much excite and very important and very , very happy , for this be to be the very first egg roll the Green Meadows have ever know , and it be all his very own .
Hidden behind the old hickory , tuck under piece of bark , scatter among the bluets and wind flower be big egg , little eggs and middle-sized egg , for Jimmy Skunk have be true to his promise .
Where they come from Jimmy would n't tell .
Perhaps if old Gray Goose and Mrs. Quack could have be there , they would have understand why it take so long to fill their nest .
Perhaps if Farmer Brown 's boy have happen along , he would have guess why he have to hunt so long in the barn and under the henhouse to get enough egg for breakfast .
But Jimmy Skunk hold his tongue and just smile to see how happy Peter Rabbit be .
First come Peter 's cousin , Jumper the Hare .
Then up from the Smiling Pool come Jerry Muskrat , Little Joe Otter , Billy Mink , Grandfather Frog and Spotty the Turtle .
Johnny Chuck , Danny Meadow Mouse , and old Mr. Toad come together .
Of course Reddy Fox be on hand promptly .
Striped Chipmunk come dance out from the home no one have be able to find .
Out from the Green Forest trot Bobby Coon , Happy Jack Squirrel and Chatterer the Red Squirrel .
Behind them shuffle Prickly Porky .
Last of all come Jimmy Skunk , who never hurry , and Jimmy wear his very best suit of black and white .
Up in the old hickory sit Blacky the Crow , Sammy Jay and Drummer the Woodpecker , to watch the fun .
When all have arrive , Peter Rabbit start them to hunt for the egg .
Everybody get in the way of everybody else .
Even old Mr. Toad catch the excitement and hop this way and hop that way hunt for egg .
Danny Meadow Mouse find a goose egg big than himself and have to get help to bring it in .
Bobby Coon stub his toe and fell down with an egg under each arm .
Such a look sight a he be !
He have to go down to the Smiling Pool to wash .
By and by , when all the egg have be find , Peter Rabbit send a big goose egg roll down the grassy bank and then race after it to bring it back and roll it down again .
In a few minute the green grassy bank be cover with egg -- big egg , little egg , all kind of egg .
Some be nearly round and roll swiftly to the bottom .
Some be sharp point at one end and roll crookedly and sometimes turned end over end .
A big egg knock Johnny Chuck 's leg from under him and , because Johnny Chuck be round and roly-poly , he just roll over and over after the egg clear to the bottom of the green grassy bank .
And it be such fun that he scramble up and do it all over again .
Then Bobby Coon try it .
Pretty soon every one be try it , even Reddy Fox , who seldom forgets his dignity .
For once Blacky the Crow and Sammy Jay almost wish that they have n't get wing , so that they might join in the fun .
But the great fun of all be when Prickly Porky decide that he , too , would join in the rolling .
He tuck his head down in his vest and make himself into a perfectly round ball .
Now when he do this , all his hidden spear stand out straight , until he look like a great , giant , chestnut burr , and every one hurry to get out of his way .
Over and over , fast and faster , he roll down the green , grassy bank until he land -- where do you think ?
Why right in the midst of a lot of egg that have be leave when the other little people have scamper out of his way .
Now , have his head tuck into his vest , Prickly Porky could n't see where he be go , so when he reach the bottom and hop to his foot he do n't know what to make of the shout that go up from all the little meadow people .
So foolish Prickly Porky lose his temper because he be be laugh at , and start off up the Lone Little Path to his home in the Green Forest .
And what do you think ?
Why , stick fast in a row on the spear on his back , Prickly Porky carry off six of Peter Rabbit 's Easter egg , and do n't know it .
V HOW JOHNNY CHUCK RAN AWAY Johnny Chuck stand on the doorstep of his house and watch old Mrs. Chuck start down the Lone Little Path across the Green Meadows towards Farmer Brown 's garden .
She have her market basket on her arm , and Johnny know that when she return it would be full of the thing he like best .
But not even the thought of these could chase away the frown that darken Johnny Chuck 's face .
He have never be to Farmer Brown 's garden and he have beg very hard to go that morning with old Mrs. Chuck .
But she have say `` No .
It be n't safe for such a little chap a you . ''
And when Mrs. Chuck say `` No , '' Johnny know that she mean it , and that it be of no use at all to beg .
So he stand with his hand in his pocket and scowl and scowl a he think of old Mrs. Chuck 's very last word : `` Now , Johnny , do n't you dare put a foot outside of the yard until I get back . ''
Pretty soon along come Peter Rabbit .
Peter be try to jump over his own shadow .
When he saw Johnny Chuck he stop abruptly .
Then he look up at the blue sky and wink at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun .
`` Looks mighty showery ` round here , '' he remark to no one in particular .
Johnny Chuck smile in spite of himself .
Then he tell Peter Rabbit how he have get to stay at home and mind the house and could n't put his foot outside the yard .
Now Peter have n't have the best bring up in the world , for his mother have such a big family that she be kept busy just get them something to eat .
So Peter have be allow to bring himself up and do just about a he please .
`` How long will your mother be go ? ''
ask Peter .
`` Most all the morning , '' say Johnny Chuck mournfully .
Peter hop a couple of step nearer .
`` Say , Johnny , '' he whisper , `` how be she go to know whether you stay in the yard all the time or not , so long a you be here when she get home ?
I know where there 's the dandy sweet-clover patch .
We can go over there and back easy before old Mrs. Chuck get home , and she wo n't know anything about it .
Come on ! ''
Johnny Chuck 's mouth water at the thought of the sweet-clover , but still he hesitate , for Johnny Chuck have be teach to mind . ''
` Fraid cat !
` Fraid cat !
Tied to your mother 's apron string ! ''
jeered Peter Rabbit .
`` I ai n't either ! ''
cry Johnny Chuck .
And then , just to prove it , he thrust his hand into his pocket and swagger out into the Lone Little Path .
`` Where 's your old clover patch ? ''
ask he .
`` I 'll show you , '' say Peter Rabbit , and off he start , lipperty-lipperty-lip , so fast that Johnny Chuck lose his breath try to make his short leg keep up .
And all the time Johnny 's conscience be prick him .
Peter Rabbit leave the Lone Little Path across the Green Meadows for some secret little path of his own .
His long leg take him over the ground very fast .
Johnny Chuck , run behind him , grow tired and hot , for Johnny 's leg be short and he be fat and roly-poly .
At time all he could see be the white patch on the seat of Peter Rabbit 's pant .
He begin to wish that he have mind old Mrs. Chuck and stay at home .
It be too late to go back now , for he do n't know the way .
`` Wait up , Peter Rabbit ! ''
he call .
Peter Rabbit just flirt his tail and run faster .
`` Please , please wait for me , Peter Rabbit , '' pant Johnny Chuck , and begin to cry .
Yes , Sir , he begin to cry .
You see he be so hot and tired , and then he be so afraid that he would lose sight of Peter Rabbit .
If he do he would surely be lose , and then what should he do ?
The very thought make him run just a little faster .

Now Peter Rabbit be really one of the best-hearted little fellow in the world , just happy-go-lucky and careless .

he pant , wipe his eye with the back of his hand .

We 'll rest here a few minute and then I wo n't run so fast . ''
So Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck lay down in the grass to rest while Johnny Chuck recover his breath .

It make Johnny Chuck nervous .

Peter Rabbit lead the way , and if he have run fast before it be nothing to the way he run now .

say Peter Rabbit , `` do n't mind a little thing like that . ''

`` I do n't unless I feel like it .
You stay away a long time and then your mother will be so glad to see you that she wo n't ever think of the pant . ''
Johnny Chuck look doubtful , but before he could say anything Peter Rabbit stick his head out to see if the way be clear .
It be , and Peter 's long leg follow his head .

But Johnny Chuck be afraid .
He be almost sure that Old Whitetail be wait just outside to gobble him up .

But without Peter Rabbit it grow lonesome and lonesomer in under the old stone wall .
Besides , he be afraid that he would lose Peter Rabbit , and then he would be lose indeed , for he do n't know the way home .
Finally Johnny Chuck venture to peep out .

My , how good that sweet-clover do taste !

VI PETER RABBIT 'S RUN FOR LIFE `` I wish I have n't run away , '' say Johnny Chuck dolefully , a he and Peter Rabbit peep out from the sweet-clover patch and watch old Mrs. Chuck start for home with her market basket on her arm .

If it have n't be for me she would have , '' say Peter Rabbit .

Yes , Sir , Johnny Chuck 's conscience be prick him hard , very hard indeed , because he have run away from home with Peter Rabbit after old Mrs. Chuck have tell him not to leave the yard while she be away .
Now he do n't know the way home .

Let 's go up and see it .
It 's a dandy place . ''
Now right down in his heart Johnny Chuck know that he ought to go home , but he could n't go unless Peter Rabbit would show him the way , and then he do want to see that old house .

So Johnny Chuck follow Peter Rabbit up the hill to the old house of Jimmy Skunk .

So they hunt and hunt , and by and by Johnny Chuck find the back door way off at one side and cunningly hide under a tangle of grass .
Inside be a long dark hall and at the end of that a nice big room .
It be very dirty , and Johnny Chuck , who be very neat , at once begin to clean house and soon have it spick and span .
Suddenly they hear a voice outside the front door .
`` Does n't look a if anybody live here , but seem a if I smell young rabbit and -- yes , I 'm sure I smell young chuck , too .

Peter Rabbit be run for his life .

Peter Rabbit do not like to think what would happen to him if she should catch him .
Peter Rabbit be use to run for his life .

This time , however , the only place of safety he could think of be the friendly old brier patch , and that be a long way off .
Back at the old house on the hill , where Granny Fox have discover Peter Rabbit , be little Johnny Chuck , tremble with fright .

While he have seem to be run his very hard , really he be not .

VII A JOKER FOOLED Peter Rabbit and Johnny Chuck sit in the doorway of Jimmy Skunk 's deserted old house on the hill and look down across the Green Meadows .

VIII THE FUSS IN THE BIG PINE Peter Rabbit hop down the Crooked Little Path to the Lone Little Path and down the Lone Little Path to the home of Johnny Chuck .

They be very pleasant dream , very pleasant dream indeed .
They be such pleasant dream that for once Johnny Chuck forget to put his funny little ear on guard .
So Johnny Chuck sit on his doorstep dreaming and heard nothing .
Lipperty-lipperty-lip down the Lone Little Path come Peter Rabbit .
He saw Johnny Chuck and he stop long enough to pluck a long stem of grass .
Then very , very softly he steal up behind Johnny Chuck .
Reaching out with the long stem of grass , he tickle one of Johnny Chuck 's ear .
Johnny Chuck slap at his ear with a little black hand , for he think a fly be bother him , just a Peter Rabbit mean that he should .
Peter tickle the other ear .
Johnny Chuck shake his head and slap at this with the other little black hand .
Peter almost giggle .
He sit still a few minute , then tickle Johnny Chuck again .

Peter laugh before he could clap his hand over his mouth .

Such a dreadful racket !

Peter Rabbit begin to get interested , for you know Peter have a very great deal of curiosity .

You know Hooty the Owl can not see in the daytime very well , and they can do almost anything to him that they want to .

`` I do n't see any sport in make other people uncomfortable , '' say Johnny Chuck .
