I wonder why !
Because to hear what others say He 's bound to try !
he 's bound to try . ''
It be Peter Rabbit 's turn to look discomfit .
`` Anyway , I do n't try to bully and torment others and I do n't steal , '' he retort .
`` Sammy Jay 's a handsome chap And wear a coat of blue .
I wonder if it 's really his Or if he steal that , too . ''
Just then Johnny Chuck 's sharp eye catch sight of something steal along the edge of the Green Meadows toward the Green Forest and the big pine .
`` There 's Farmer Brown 's boy with a gun , '' cry Johnny Chuck .
`` There 's go to be trouble at the big pine if Blacky the Crow do n't watch out .
That 's what come of be so noisy . ''
Peter Rabbit and Sammy Jay stop quarrel to look .
Sure enough , there be Farmer Brown 's boy with his gun .
He have hear Blacky the Crow and his aunt and his uncle and his cousin and he have hurry to get his gun , hop to take them by surprise .
But Blacky the Crow have sharp eye , too .
Indeed , there be none sharper .
Then , too , he be a mischief-maker .
Mischief-makers be always on the watch l they get catch in their mischief .
So Blacky the Crow , sit on the tip-top of the big pine , keep one eye out for trouble while he enjoy the tormenting of Hooty the Owl by his aunt and his uncle and his cousin .
He have see Farmer Brown 's boy even before Johnny Chuck have .
But he could n't bear to spoil the fun of torment Hooty the Owl , so he wait just as long a he dare .
Then he give the signal .
`` Caw , caw , caw , caw ! ''
shout Blacky at the top of his lung .
`` Caw , caw , caw , caw ! ''
reply all his aunt and uncle and cousin , rise into the air in a black cloud .
Then , with Blacky in the lead , they fly over on to the Green Meadows , laugh and talk noisily a they go .
Farmer Brown 's boy do not try to follow them , for he know that it be of not the least bit of use .
But he be curious to learn what the crow have be make such a fuss about , so he keep on towards the big pine .
Johnny Chuck watch him go .
Suddenly he remember Hooty the Owl , and that Hooty can not see well in the daytime .
Very likely Hooty would think that the crow have become tired of torment him and have go off of their own accord .
Farmer Brown 's boy would find him there and then -- Johnny Chuck shudder a he think of what might happen to Hooty the Owl .
`` Run , Peter Rabbit , run as fast a you can down on the Green Meadows where the Merry Little Breezes be at play and send one of them to tell Hooty the Owl that Farmer Brown 's boy be come with a gun to the big pine !
Hurry , Peter , hurry ! ''
cry Johnny Chuck .
Peter do not need to be tell twice .
He saw the danger of Hooty the Owl , and he start down the Lone Little Path on to the Green Meadows so fast that in a few minute all Johnny Chuck and Sammy Jay could see of him be a little spot of white , which be the patch on the seat of Peter 's pant , bob through the grass on the Green Meadows .
Johnny Chuck would have go himself , but he be round and fat and roly-poly and can not run fast , while Peter Rabbit 's leg be long and meant for run .
In a few minute Johnny Chuck saw one of the Merry Little Breezes start for the big pine a fast a he could go .
Johnny give a great sigh of relief .
Farmer Brown 's boy keep on to the big pine .
When he get there he find no one there , for Hooty the Owl have heed the warning of the Merry Little Breeze and have fly into the deep , dark part of the Green Forest , where not even the sharp eye of Blacky the Crow be likely to find him .
And back on his doorstep Johnny Chuck chuckle to himself , for he be happy , be Johnny Chuck , happy because he possess the best thing in the world , which be contentment .
And this be all I be go to tell you about the fuss in the big pine .
IX JOHNNY CHUCK FINDS A USE FOR HIS BACK DOOR Johnny Chuck sit in his doorway look over the Green Meadows .
He felt very fine .
He have have a good breakfast in the sweet-clover patch .
He have have a good nap on his own doorstep .
By and by he saw the Merry Little Breezes of old Mother West Wind hurry in his direction .
They seem in a very great hurry .
They do n't stop to kiss the buttercup or tease the daisy .
Johnny prick up his small ear and watch them hurry up the hill .
`` Good morning , Johnny Chuck , '' pant the first Merry Little Breeze to reach him , `` have you hear the news ? ''
`` What news ? ''
ask Johnny Chuck .
`` The news about old Mother Chuck , '' reply the Merry Little Breezes .
Johnny shake his head .
`` No , '' say he .
`` What be it ? ''
The Merry Little Breezes grow very , very sober .
`` It be bad news , '' they reply .
`` What be it ?
Tell me quick ! ''
beg Johnny .
Just then Reddy Fox come hop and skip down the Lone Little Path .
`` Hi , Johnny Chuck , have you hear the news ? ''
`` No , '' say Johnny Chuck , `` do tell me quick ! ''
Reddy Fox grin maliciously , for Reddy like to torment others .
`` It 's about old Mrs. Chuck , '' say Reddy .
`` I know that already , '' reply Johnny , `` but , please , what be it ? ''
`` Farmer Brown 's boy have catch old Mrs. Chuck , and now I would n't wonder but what he will come up here and catch you , '' reply Reddy , turn a somersault .
Johnny Chuck grow pale .
He have not see Mother Chuck to speak to since he run away from home .
Now he be glad that he have run away , and yet sorry , oh , so sorry that anything have happen to Mrs. Chuck .
Two big tear come into his eye and run down his funny little black nose .
The Merry Little Breezes saw this , and one of them hurry over and whisper in Johnny Chuck 's ear .
`` Do n't cry , Johnny Chuck , '' whisper the Merry Little Breeze .
`` Old Mother Chuck get away , and Farmer Brown 's boy be still wonder how she do it . ''
Johnny 's heart give a great throb of relief .
`` I do n't believe that Farmer Brown 's boy will catch me , '' say Johnny Chuck , `` for my house have two back door . ''
Johnny Chuck awake very early the next morning .
He stretch and yawn and then just lay quietly enjoy himself for a few minute .
His bedchamber , way down underground , be snug and warm and very , very comfortable .
By and by , Johnny Chuck hear a noise up by his front door .
`` I wonder what be go on out there , '' say Johnny Chuck to himself , and jump up , he tiptoe softly up the long hall until he have almost reach his doorway .
Then he hear a voice which he have hear before , and it make little shiver run all over him .
It be the voice of Granny Fox .
`` So this be where that fat little Chuck have make his home , '' say Granny Fox .
`` Yes , '' reply another voice , `` this be where Johnny Chuck live , for I saw him here yesterday . ''
Johnny prick up his ear , for that be the voice of Reddy Fox .
`` Do you think he be in here now ? ''
inquired Granny Fox .
`` I be sure of it , '' reply Reddy , `` for I have be watch ever since jolly , round , red Mr. Sun throw his nightcap off this morning , and Johnny Chuck have not put his nose out yet . ''
`` Good , '' say Granny Fox , `` I think fat Chuck will taste good for breakfast . ''
Johnny felt the cold shiver run over him again a he hear Granny Fox and Reddy Fox smack their lip .
Then Granny Fox speak again : `` You lie down behind that bunch of grass over there , Reddy , and I will lie down behind the old apple-tree .
When he come out , you just jump into his doorway and I will catch him before he can say Jack Robinson . ''
Johnny wait and listen and listen , but all be as still a still could be .
Then Johnny Chuck tiptoe back along the hall to his bedroom and sit down to think .
He felt sure that Granny Fox and Reddy be wait for him , just a he have hear them plan .
`` However be I go to know when they leave ? ''
say Johnny Chuck to himself .
Then he remember the back door which he have take such care to make , and which Peter Rabbit have laugh at him for take the trouble to make .
He have hide one so cunningly in the long grass and have so carefully remove all sand from around it that he felt quite sure that no one have find it .
Very softly Johnny Chuck creep along the back passageway .
Very , very cautiously he stick his little black nose out the doorway and sniffed .
Yes , he could smell fox , but he know that they be not at his back door .
Little by little he creep out until he could peep through the grass .
There lay Reddy Fox behind a big clump of grass , his eye fix on Johnny Chuck 's front door , and there behind the apple-tree lay Granny Fox take her ease , but all ready to jump when Reddy should give the word .
Johnny Chuck almost giggle out loud a he saw how eagerly Reddy Fox be watch for him .
Then Johnny Chuck have an idea that make him giggle harder .
His black eye snap and he chuckle to himself .
Pretty soon along come Bumble the Bee , look for honey .
He come bustle and hum through the tall grass and settle on a dandelion right on the doorstep of Johnny Chuck 's back door .
`` Good morning , '' grumble Bumble the Bee .
Johnny put a hand on his lip and beckon Bumble to come inside .
Now Bumble the Bee be a gruff and rough fellow , but he be a good fellow , too , when you know him .
Johnny Chuck have many time tell him of place where the flower grow thick and sweet , so when Johnny beckon to him , Bumble come at once .
`` Will you do something for me , Bumble ? ''
whisper Johnny Chuck .
`` Of course , I will , '' reply Bumble , in his gruff voice .
`` What be it ? ''
Then Johnny Chuck tell Bumble the Bee how Granny and Reddy Fox be wait for him to come out for his breakfast and how they have plan to gobble him up for their own breakfast .
Bumble the Bee grow very indignant .
`` What do you want me to do , Johnny Chuck ? ''
he ask .
`` If I can help you , just tell me how . ''
Johnny whisper something to Bumble the Bee , and Bumble laugh right out loud .
Then he buzz up out of the doorway , and Johnny creep up to watch .
Straight over to where Reddy Fox be squat behind the clump of grass fly Bumble the Bee , so swiftly that Johnny could hardly see him .
Suddenly Reddy give a yelp and sprang into the air .
Johnny Chuck clap both hand over his mouth to keep from laugh out loud , for you see Bumble the Bee have stick his sharp little lance into one of the ear of Reddy Fox .
Granny Fox look up and scowl .
`` Keep still , '' she whisper .
Just then Reddy yelp loud than before , for Bumble have sting him in the other ear .
`` What 's the matter ? ''
snap Granny Fox .
`` I do n't know , '' cry Reddy Fox , hang on to both ear .
`` You be -- '' begin Granny Fox , but Johnny Chuck never know what she be go to say Reddy Fox be , for you see just then Bumble the Bee thrust his sharp little lance into one of her ear , and before she could turn around he have do the same thing to the other ear .
Granny Fox do n't wait for any more .
She start off as fast a she could go , with Reddy Fox after her , and every few step they rub their ear and shake their head a if they think they could shake out the pain .
X BILLY MINK GOES DINNERLESS Down the Laughing Brook come Billy Mink .
He be feel very good that morning , be Billy Mink , please with the world in general and with himself in particular .
When he reach the Smiling Pool he swim out to the Big Rock .
Little Joe Otter be already there , and not far away , lazily float , with his head and back out of water , be Jerry Muskrat .
`` Hello , Billy Mink , '' cry Little Joe Otter .
`` Hello yourself , '' reply Billy Mink , with a grin .
`` Where be you go ? ''
ask Little Joe Otter .
`` Nowhere in particular , '' reply Billy Mink .
`` Let 's go fish down to the Big River , '' say Little Joe Otter .
`` Let 's ! ''
cry Billy , dive from the high point on the Big Rock .
So off they start across the Green Meadows towards the Big River .
Half way there they meet Reddy Fox .
`` Hello , Reddy !
Come on with u to the Big River , fishing , '' call Billy Mink .
-LSB- Illustration : `` Come on with u to the Big River , fishing , '' call Billy Mink . -RSB-
Now Reddy Fox be no fisherman , though he like fish to eat well enough .
He remember the last time he go fish and how Billy Mink have laugh at him when he fell into the Smiling Pool .
He be just about to say `` no '' when he change his mind .
`` All right , I 'll go , '' say Reddy Fox .
So the three of them race merrily across the Green Meadows until they come to the Big River .
Now Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter be famous fisherman and can swim even faster than the fish themselves .
But Reddy Fox be a poor swimmer and must depend upon his wit .
When they reach the bank of the Big River they very carefully crawl down to a sandy beach .
There , just a little way out from shore , a school of little striped perch be at play .
Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter prepare to dive in and each grab a fish , but Reddy Fox know that he could not swim well enough for that .
`` Wait a minute , '' whisper Reddy .
`` Billy Mink , you go up the river a little way and swim out beyond where the fish be at play .
Little Joe Otter , you go down the river a little way and swim out to join Billy Mink .
Then both together rush in as fast a you can swim .
The fish will be so frightened they will rush in where the water be shallow .
Of course you will each catch one , anyway , and perhaps I may be so lucky a to catch one in the shallow water . ''
Billy Mink and little Joe Otter agree , and do just a Reddy Fox have tell them to .
When they be between the play fish and deep water they start in with a rush .
The little striped perch be young and foolish .
When they saw Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter they rush madly away from them without look to see where they be go to .
As Reddy Fox have foresee would be the case , a lot of them become strand where the water be too shallow for swimming , and there they jump and flap helplessly .
Reddy be wait for them and in a twinkle his little black paw have scoop half a dozen fish high and dry on the beach .
Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter be too busy watch the fish to see what Reddy be do .
He have catch six fish and these he hide under a log .
When Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter swam ashore , Reddy be the picture of disappointment , for he have nothing to show , while the others each have a plump little fish .
`` Never mind , '' say Little Joe Otter , `` I 'll give you the next one I catch . ''
But Billy Mink jeer at Reddy Fox .
`` Pooh !
you 're no fisherman , Reddy Fox !
If I could n't catch fish when they be chase right into my hand I 'd never go fishing . ''
Reddy Fox pretend to be indignant .
`` I tell you what , Billy Mink , '' say he , `` if I do n't catch more fish than you do to-day I 'll bring you the plump chicken in Farmer Brown 's dooryard , but if I do catch more fish than you do you will give me the big one you catch .
Do you agree ? ''
Now Billy Mink be very fond of plump chicken and here be a chance to get one without danger of meet Bowser the Hound , who guard Farmer Brown 's chicken .
So Billy Mink agree to give Reddy Fox the big fish he catch that day if Reddy could show more fish than he could at the end of the day .
All the time he chuckle to himself , for you know Billy Mink be a famous fisherman , and he know that Reddy Fox be a poor swimmer and do not like the water .
By and by they come to another sandy beach like the first one .
They could see another school of foolish young fish at play .
As before , Reddy Fox remain on shore while the others swim out and drive the fish in .
As before Reddy catch half a dozen , while Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter each catch one this time .
Reddy hid five and then pretend to be so tickle over catch one , the small of the lot , that Billy Mink do n't once suspect a trick .
Two or three time more Reddy Fox repeat this .
Then he discover a big pickerel sun himself beside an old log float in deep water .
Reddy could n't catch Mr. Pickerel , for the water be deep .
What should he do ?
Reddy sit down to think .
Finally he think of a plan .
Very cautiously he back away so a not to scare the big fish .
Then he call Billy Mink .
When Billy saw the big pickerel , his mouth water , too , and his little black eye sparkle .
Very quietly Billy slip into the water back of the old log .
There be not so much a a ripple to warn the big pickerel .
Drawing a long breath , Billy dive under the log , and come up under the big pickerel , seize it by the middle .
There be a tremendous thrashing and splashing , and then Billy Mink swim ashore and proudly lay the big fish on the bank .
`` Do n't you wish it be yours ? ''
ask Billy Mink .
`` It ought to be mine , for I saw it first , '' say Reddy Fox .
`` But you do n't catch it and I do , '' retort Billy Mink .
`` I 'm go to have it for my dinner .
My , but I do like fat pickerel ! ''
Billy smack his lip .
Reddy Fox say nothing , but try his best to look disappointed and deject .
All the time he be chuckle inwardly .
For the rest of the day the fishing be poor .
Just a Old Mother West Wind start for the Green Meadows to take her child , the Merry Little Breezes , to their home behind the Purple Hills , the three little fisherman start to count up their catch .
Then Reddy bring out all the fish that he have hide .
When they saw the pile of fish Reddy Fox have , Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter be so surprised that their eye pop out and their jaw drop .
Very foolish they look , very foolish indeed , for Reddy have four time as many a either of them .
Reddy walk over to the big pickerel and pick it up , carry it over to his pile .
`` What be you do with my fish ? ''
shout Billy Mink angrily .
`` It be n't yours , it 's mine ! ''
retort Reddy Fox .
Billy Mink fairly dance up and down he be so angry .
`` It 's not yours ! ''
he shriek .
`` It 's mine , for I catch it ! ''
`` And you agree that your big fish should be mine if I catch more fish than you do .
I 've catch four time a many , so the pickerel be mine , '' retort Reddy , wink at Little Joe Otter .
Then Billy Mink do a very foolish thing ; he lose his temper completely .
He call Reddy Fox bad name .
But he do not dare try to take the big pickerel away from Reddy , for Reddy be much big than he .
Finally he work himself into such a rage that he run off home leave his pile of fish behind .
Reddy Fox and Little Joe Otter take care not to touch Billy Mink 's fish , but Reddy divide his big pile with Little Joe Otter .
Then they , too , start for home , Reddy carry the big pickerel .
Late that night , when he have recover his temper , Billy Mink begin to grow hungry .
The more he think of his fish the hungrier he grow .
Finally he could stand it no longer and start for the Big River to see what have become of his fish .
He reach the strip of beach where he have so foolishly leave them just in time to see the last striped perch disappear down the long throat of Mr. Night Heron .
And this be how it happen that Billy Mink go dinnerless to bed .
But he have learn three thing , have Billy , and he never forget them -- that wit be often good than skill ; that it be not only mean but be very foolish to sneer at another ; and that to lose one 's temper be the most foolish thing in the world .
XI GRANDFATHER FROG 'S JOURNEY Grandfather Frog sit on his big green lily-pad in the Smiling Pool and -- Grandfather Frog be asleep !
There be no doubt about it , Grandfather Frog be really and truly asleep .
His hand be fold across his white and yellow waistcoat and his eye be close .
Three time the Merry Little Breezes blow a foolish green fly right past his nose ; -- Grandfather Frog do n't so much a blink .
Presently Billy Mink discover that Grandfather Frog be asleep .
Billy 's little black eye twinkle with mischief a he hurry over to the slippery slide in search of Little Joe Otter .
Then the two scamp hunt up Jerry Muskrat .
They find him very busy store away a supply of food in his new house .
At first Jerry refuse to listen to what they have to say , but the more they talk the more Jerry become interested .
`` We wo n't hurt Grandfather Frog , not the least little bit , '' protest Billy Mink .
`` It will be just the best joke and the great fun ever , and no harm do . ''
The more Jerry think over Billy Mink 's plan , the funny the joke seem .
Finally Jerry agree to join Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter .
Then the three put their head together and with a lot of giggle and chuckle they plan their joke on Grandfather Frog .
Now Jerry Muskrat can stay a very long time under water , and his teeth be long and sharp in order to cut the root on which he depend for much of his food .
So Jerry swim out to the big green lily-pad on which sit Grandfather Frog fast asleep .
Diving way to the bottom of the Smiling Pool , Jerry cut off the stem of the big green lily-pad close to it root way down in the mud .
While Jerry be at work do this , Billy Mink send the Merry Little Breezes hurry over the Green Meadows to call all the little meadow people to the Smiling Pool .
Then , when Jerry Muskrat come up for a breath of air , Billy Mink dive down and , get hold of the end of the lily-pad stem , he begin to swim , tow the big green lily-pad after him very slowly and gently so a not to waken Grandfather Frog .
When Billy have to come up for air , Little Joe Otter take his place .
Then Jerry Muskrat take his turn .
Across the Smiling Pool , past the Big Rock , they tow the big green lily-pad , while Grandfather Frog sleep peacefully , his hand fold over his white and yellow waistcoat .
Past the bulrush and Jerry Muskrat 's new house , past Little Joe Otter 's slippery slide sail Grandfather Frog , and still he sleep and dream of the day when the world be young .
Out of the Smiling Pool and into the Laughing Brook , where the brown water flow smoothly , the three little swimmer tow the big green lily-pad .
It float along of itself now , and all they have to do be to steer it clear of rock and old log .
Once it almost get away from them , on the edge of a tiny waterfall , but all three pull together tow it out of danger .
At last , in a dear little pool with a mossy green bank , they anchor the big green lily-pad .
Then Billy Mink hurry back to the Smiling Pool to tell the little meadow people where to find Grandfather Frog .
Little Joe Otter climb out on the mossy green bank and Jerry Muskrat join him there to rest and dry off .
One by one the little meadow people come hurry up .
Reddy Fox be the first .
Then come Johnny Chuck and Striped Chipmunk .
Of course Peter Rabbit be on hand .
You can always count Peter in , when there be anything go on among the little meadow people .
Danny Meadow Mouse and Happy Jack Squirrel arrive quite out of breath .
Sammy Jay and Blacky the Crow be not far behind .
Last of all come Jimmy Skunk , who never hurry .
Each in turn peep over the edge of the mossy green bank to see Grandfather Frog still sleep peacefully on his big green lily-pad in the dear little pool .
Then all hid where they could see him when he awake , but where he could not see them .
Presently Billy Mink reach out with a long straw and tickle Grandfather Frog on the end of his nose .
Grandfather Frog open his eye and yawn sleepily .
Right over his head he saw jolly , round , red Mr. Sun smile down on him just a he last saw him before fall asleep .
He yawn again and then look to see if Billy Mink be sit on the Big Rock .
Where be the Big Rock ?
Grandfather Frog sit up very suddenly and rub his eye .
There be n't any Big Rock !
Grandfather Frog pinch himself to make sure that he be awake .
Then he rub his eye again and look down at the big green lily-pad .
Yes , that be his , the very same lily-pad on which he sit every day .
Grandfather Frog be more perplexed than ever .
Slowly he look around .
Where be the slippery slide and Jerry Muskrat 's new house ?
Where be the bulrush and where -- where be the Smiling Pool ?
Grandfather Frog 's jaw drop a he look about him .
His own big green lily-pad be the only lily-pad in sight .
Had the world turn topsy-turvy while he sleep ?
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog .
`` This be very strange , very strange , indeed ! ''
Then he turn around three time and pinch himself again .
`` Very strange , very strange , indeed , '' mutter Grandfather Frog over and over again .
He scratch his head first with one hand and then with the other , and the more he scratch the stranger it all seem .
Just then he hear a giggle up on the mossy green bank .
Grandfather Frog whirl around .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
he exclaim .
`` Billy Mink , come out from behind that tall grass and tell me where I be and what this mean !
I might have know that you be at the bottom of it . ''
Then out jump all the little meadow people and the Merry Little Breezes to shout and laugh and dance and roll over and over on the mossy green bank .
Grandfather Frog look at one and then at another and gradually he begin to smile .
Pretty soon he be laugh as hard a any of them , a Billy Mink tell how they have tow him down to the dear little pool .
`` And now , Grandfather Frog , we 'll take you home again , '' conclude Billy Mink .
So , a before , Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Jerry Muskrat take turn tow the big green lily-pad , while in the middle of it sit Grandfather Frog , catch foolish green fly which the Merry Little Breezes blow over to him .
Reddy Fox , Johnny Chuck , Peter Rabbit , Danny Meadow Mouse , Striped Chipmunk , Happy Jack Squirrel and Jimmy Skunk race and caper along the bank and shout encouragement to the three little swimmer , while over-head flew Sammy Jay and Blacky the Crow .
And , never once lose his balance , Grandfather Frog sit on the big green lily-pad , enjoy his strange ride and smack his lip over the foolish green fly .
And so they come once more to the Smiling Pool , past the slippery slide , past the bulrush and Jerry Muskrat 's new house and the Big Rock , until Grandfather Frog and his queer craft be once more anchored safe and sound in the old familiar place .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog .
`` I think I 'd like to go again . ''
XII WHY BLACKY THE CROW WEARS MOURNING Grandfather Frog sit on his big green lily-pad in the Smiling Pool .
Grandfather Frog felt very good that morning , very good indeed , because -- why , because his white and yellow waistcoat be full of foolish green fly .
It be doubtful , very , very doubtful if Grandfather Frog could have swallow another foolish green fly to save his life .
So he sit with his hand fold across his white and yellow waistcoat , and into his eye , his great goggly eye , there creep a far , far , far away look .
Grandfather Frog be dream of the day when the world be young and the frog rule the world .
Pretty soon the Merry Little Breezes of Old Mother West Wind come over to the Smiling Pool to rock Mrs. Redwing 's baby to sleep in their cradle in the bulrush .
But when they saw Grandfather Frog they forget all about Mrs. Redwing and her baby .
`` Good morning , Grandfather Frog ! ''
they shout .
Grandfather Frog awake from his dream with a funny little jump .
`` Goodness , how you startle me ! ''
say Grandfather Frog , smooth down his white and yellow waistcoat .
The Merry Little Breezes giggle .
`` We do n't mean to , truly we do n't , '' say the merry one of all .
`` We just want to know how you do this fine morning , and -- and -- '' `` Chug-a-rum , '' say Grandfather Frog , `` you want me to tell you a story . ''
The Merry Little Breezes giggle again .
`` How do you ever guess it ? ''
they cry .
`` It must be because you be so very , very wise .
Will you tell u a story , Grandfather Frog ?
Will you please ? ''
Grandfather Frog look up and wink one big , goggly eye at jolly , round , red Mr. Sun , who be smile down from the blue sky .
Then he sit still so long that the Merry Little Breezes begin to fear that Grandfather Frog be out of sort and that there would be no story that morning .
They fidget about among the bulrush and dance back and forth across the lily-pads .
They have even begin to think again of Mrs. Redwing 's baby .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog suddenly .
`` What shall I tell you about ? ''
Just then a black shadow sweep across the Smiling Pool .
`` Caw , caw , caw , caw ! ''
shout Blacky the Crow noisily , a he fly over toward Farmer Brown 's cornfield .
`` Tell u why Blacky the Crow always wear a coat of black , a if he be in mourning , '' shout the Merry Little Breezes .
Grandfather Frog watch Blacky disappear behind the Lone Pine .
Then , when the Merry Little Breezes have settle down , each in the golden heart of a white water-lily , he begin : `` Once upon a time , when the world be young , old Mr. Crow , the grandfather a thousand time remove of Blacky , whom you all know , live in the Green Forest on the edge of the Green Meadows , just a Blacky do now , and with him live his brother and sister , his uncle and aunt , his cousin and all his poor relation .
`` Now Mr. Crow be very smart .
Indeed , he be the smart of all the bird .
There be n't anything that old Mr. Crow could n't do or do n't know .
At least he think there be n't .
All the little meadow people and forest folk begin to think so , too , and one after another they get in the habit of come to him for advice , until pretty soon they be bring all their affair to Mr. Crow for settlement .
`` Now for a while Mr. Crow show great wisdom , and this so pleased Old Mother Nature that she give him a suit of pure , dazzle white , so that all see him might look up to him a a shin example of wisdom and virtue .
Of course all his brother and sister , his uncle and aunt , his cousin and all his poor relation at once put on white , that all might know that they be of Mr. Crow 's family .
And of course every one show them the great attention out of respect to old Mr. Crow , so that presently they begin to hold their head very high and to think that because they be relate to old Mr. Crow they be a little good than any of the other little meadow people and forest folk .
When they meet old Mr. Rabbit they would pretend not to see him , because he wear a white patch on the seat of his trouser .
When old Mr. Woodchuck say ` good morning , ' they would pretend not to hear , for you know Mr. Woodchuck wear a suit of dingy yellow and live in a hole in the ground .
Old Mr. Toad be ugly to look upon .
Besides , he work for his living in a garden .
So when they happen to meet him on the road they always turn their back .
`` For a long time old Mr. Crow himself continue to be a very fine gentleman and to hold the respect of all his neighbor .
He be polite to every one , and to all who come to him he freely give of his advice as wisely a he know how .
Of course it be n't long before he know all about his neighbor and their private affair .
Now it be n't safe to know too much about your neighbor and what they be do .
It be dangerous knowledge , very dangerous knowledge indeed , '' say Grandfather Frog solemnly .
`` To be sure it would have be safe enough , '' he continue , `` if Mr. Crow have keep it to himself .
But after a while Mr. Crow become vain .
Yes , Sir , that be just what happen to old Mr. Crow -- he become vain .
He like to feel that all the little meadow people and forest folk look up to him with respect , and whenever he saw one of them come he would brush his white coat , swell himself up and look very important .
After a while he begin to brag among his relative of how much he know about his neighbor .
Of course they be very much interested , very much interested indeed , and this flatter Mr. Crow so that almost before he know it he be tell some of the private affair which have be bring to him for his advice .
Oh , dear me , Mr. Crow begin to gossip .
`` Now , gossip be one of the bad habit in all the world , one of the very bad .
No good ever come of it .
It just make trouble , trouble , trouble .
It be so now .
Mr. Crow 's relative repeat the story that they hear .
But they take great care that no one should know where they come from .
My , my , my , how trouble do spread on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest !
No one suspect old Mr. Crow , so he be more in demand than ever to straighten matter out .
His neighbor come to him so much that they begin to be ashamed to ask his advice for nothing , so they bring him present so that no more need Mr. Crow hunt for thing to eat .
Instead , he live on the fat of the land without work , and grow fat and lazy .
`` As I have tell you , Mr. Crow be smart .
Yes , indeed , he certainly be smart .
It do not take him long to see that the more trouble there be among his neighbor the more they would need his advice , and the more they need his advice the more present he would receive .
He grow very crafty .
He would tell tale just to make trouble , and sometimes , when he saw a chance , he would give advice that he know would make more trouble .
The fact be , old Mr. Crow become a mischief-maker , the very bad kind of a mischief-maker .
And all the time he appear to be the fine gentleman that he use to be .
He wear his fine white coat as proudly a ever .
`` Matters grow bad and bad .
Never have there be so much trouble on the Green Meadows or so many quarrel in the Green Forest .
Old Mr. Mink never meet old Mr . Otter without pick a fight .
Old Mrs . Skunk would n't speak to old Mrs. Coon .
Old Mr. Chipmunk turn his back on his cousin , old Mr. Red Squirrel , whenever their path cross .
Even my grandfather a thousand time remove , old Mr. Frog , refuse to see his near relative , old Mr. Toad .
And all the time old Mr. Crow wear his beautiful suit of white and grow rich and fat , chuckle to himself over his ill-gotten wealth .
`` Then one day come Old Mother Nature to visit the Green Meadows .
It do n't take her long to find that something be wrong , very wrong indeed .
Old Mr. Crow and all his relative hasten to pay their respect and to tell her how much they appreciate their beautiful white suit .
Old Mr. Crow make a full report of all the trouble that have be bring to him , but he take great care not to let her know that he have have any part in make trouble .
He look very innocent , oh , very , very innocent , but not once do he look her straight in the face .
`` Now the eye of Old Mother Nature be wonderfully sharp and they seem to bore right through old Mr. Crow .
You ca n't fool Old Mother Nature .
No , Sir , you ca n't fool Old Mother Nature , and it 's of no use to try .
She listen to all that Mr. Crow have to say .
Then she send Mr. North Wind to blow his great trumpet and call together all the little people of the Green Meadows and all the little folk of the Green Forest .
`` When they have all come together she tell them all that have happen .
She tell just how Mr. Crow have start the story in order to make trouble so that they would seek his advice and bring him present to pay for it .
When the neighbor of old Mr. Crow hear this they be very angry , and they demand of Old Mother Nature that Mr. Crow be punish . ''
` Look ! '
say Old Mother Nature , point at old Mr. Crow .
` He have be punish already . '
`` Every one turn to look at Mr. Crow .
At first they hardly know him .
Instead of his suit of spotless white his clothes be black , as black a the black night .
So be the clothes of his uncle and aunt , his brother and sister , his cousin and all his poor relation .
`` And ever since that long-ago day , when the world be young , the Crows have be mischief-maker and have wear black , that all who look may know that they bring nothing but trouble , '' conclude Grandfather Frog .
`` Thank you !
Thank you , Grandfather Frog , '' shout the Merry Little Breezes , jump up to go rock the Redwing baby .
`` Caw , caw , caw , caw ! ''
shout Blacky the Crow , fly over their head with a mouthful of corn he have steal from Farmer Brown 's cornfield .
XIII STRIPED CHIPMUNK FOOLS PETER RABBIT Peter Rabbit sit at the top of the Crooked Little Path where it start down the hill .
He be sit there when jolly , round , red Mr. Sun throw his nightcap off and begin his daily climb up into the blue , blue sky .
He saw Old Mother West Wind hurry down from the Purple Hills and turn her Merry Little Breezes out to play on the Green Meadows .
Peter yawn .
The fact be , Peter have be out nearly all night , and now he do n't know just what to do with himself .
Presently he saw Striped Chipmunk whisk up on top of an old log .
As usual the pocket in Striped Chipmunk 's cheek be stuff so full that his head look to be twice as big a it really be , and as usual he seem to be very busy , very busy indeed .
He stop just long enough to wink one of his saucy black eye and shout : `` Good morning , Peter Rabbit ! ''
Then he disappear as suddenly a he have come .
A few minute later he be back on the old log , but this time his cheek be empty .
`` Fine day , Peter Rabbit , '' say Striped Chipmunk , and whisk out of sight .
Peter Rabbit yawn again .
Then he close his eye for just a minute .
When he open them there be Striped Chipmunk on the old log just a before , and the pocket in both cheek be so full that it seem a if they would burst .
`` Nice morning to work , Peter Rabbit , '' say Striped Chipmunk , in spite of his full cheek .
Then he be go .
Once more Peter Rabbit close his eye , but hardly be they shut when Striped Chipmunk shout : `` Oh , you Peter Rabbit , be out all night ? ''
Peter snap his eye open just in time to see the funny little tail of Striped Chipmunk vanish over the side of the old log .
Peter scratch one of his long ear and yawn again , for Peter be grow more and more sleepy .
It be a long yawn , but Peter cut it off right in the middle , for there be Striped Chipmunk back on the old log , and both pocket in his cheek be stuff full .
Now Peter Rabbit be as curious a he be lazy , and you know he be very , very lazy .
The fact be , Peter Rabbit 's curiosity be his great fault , and it get him into a great deal of trouble .
It be because of this and the bad , bad habit of meddle in the affair of other people into which it have lead him that Peter Rabbit have such long ear .
For a while Peter watch busy Striped Chipmunk .
Then he begin to wonder what Striped Chipmunk could be do .
The more he wonder the more he felt that he really must know .
The next time Striped Chipmunk appear on the old log , Peter shout to him .
`` Hi , Striped Chipmunk , what be you so busy about ?
Why do n't you play a little ? ''
Striped Chipmunk stop a minute .
`` I 'm build a new house , '' say he .
`` Where ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` That 's telling , '' reply Striped Chipmunk , and whisk out of sight .
Now Peter Rabbit know where Reddy Fox and Jimmy Skunk and Bobby Coon and Happy Jack Squirrel and Johnny Chuck and Danny Meadow Mouse live .
He know all the little paths lead to their home .
But he do not know where Striped Chipmunk live .
He never have know .
He think of this a he watch Striped Chipmunk hurry back and forth .
The more he think of it the more curious he grow .
He really must know .
Pretty soon along come Jimmy Skunk , look for some beetle .
`` Hello , Jimmy Skunk , '' say Peter Rabbit .
`` Hello , Peter Rabbit , '' say Jimmy Skunk .
`` Do you know where Striped Chipmunk live ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` No , I do n't know where Striped Chipmunk live , and I do n't care ; it 's none of my business , '' reply Jimmy Skunk .
`` Have you see any beetle this morning ? ''
Peter Rabbit have n't see any beetle , so Jimmy Skunk go on down the Crooked Little Path , still look for his breakfast .
By and by along come Johnny Chuck .
`` Hello , Johnny Chuck ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` Hello , yourself ! ''
say Johnny Chuck .
`` Do you know where Striped Chipmunk live ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` No , I do n't , for it 's none of my business , '' say Johnny Chuck , and start on down the Crooked Little Path to the Green Meadows .
Then along come Bobby Coon .
`` Hello , Bobby Coon ! ''
say Peter Rabbit .
`` Hello ! ''
replied Bobby Coon shortly , for he too have be out all night and be very sleepy .
`` Do you know where Striped Chipmunk live ? ''
ask Peter Rabbit .
`` Do n't know and do n't want to ; it 's none of my business , '' say Bobby Coon even more shortly than before , and start on for his hollow chestnut tree to sleep the long , bright day away .
Peter Rabbit could stand it no longer .
Curiosity have drive away all desire to sleep .
He simply have to know where Striped Chipmunk live .
`` I 'll just follow Striped Chipmunk and see for myself where he live , '' say Peter to himself .
So Peter Rabbit hid behind a tuft of grass close by the old log and sat very , very still .
It be a very good place to hide , a very good place .
Probably if Peter Rabbit have not be so brim over with curiosity he would have succeed in escape the sharp eye of Striped Chipmunk .
But people full of curiosity be forever prick up their ear to hear thing which do not in the least concern them .
It be so with Peter Rabbit .
He be so afraid that he would miss something that both his long ear be stand up straight , and they come above the grass behind which Peter Rabbit be hide .
Of course Striped Chipmunk saw them the very instant he jump up on the old log with both pocket in his cheek stuff full .
He do n't say a word , but his sharp little eye twinkle a he jump off the end of the old log and scurry along under the bush , for he guess what Peter Rabbit be hide for , and though he do not once turn his head he know that Peter be follow him .
You see Peter run with big jump , lipperty-lipperty-lip , and people who jump must make a noise .
So , though he try very hard not to make a sound , Peter be in such a hurry to keep Striped Chipmunk in sight that he really make a great deal of noise .
The more noise Peter make , the more Striped Chipmunk chuckle to himself .
Presently Striped Chipmunk stop .
Then he sit up very straight and look this way and look that way , just a if try to make sure that no one be watch him .
Then he empty two pocketful of shin yellow gravel on to a nice new mound which he be build .
Once more he sit up and look this way and look that way .
Then he scuttle back towards the old log .
As he run Striped Chipmunk chuckle and chuckle to himself , for all the time he have see Peter Rabbit lie flat down behind a little bush and know that Peter Rabbit be think to himself how smart he have be to find Striped Chipmunk 's home when no one else know where it be .
No sooner be Striped Chipmunk out of sight than up jumped Peter Rabbit .
He smile to himself a he hurry over to the shin mound of yellow gravel .
You see Peter 's curiosity be so great that not once do he think how mean he be to spy on Striped Chipmunk .
`` Now , '' think Peter , `` I know where Striped Chipmunk live .
Jimmy Skunk do n't know .
Johnny Chuck do n't know .
Bobby Coon do n't know .
But I know .
Striped Chipmunk may fool all the others , but he ca n't fool me . ''
By this time Peter Rabbit have reach the shin mound of yellow gravel .
At once he begin to hunt for the doorway to Striped Chipmunk 's home .
But there be n't any doorway .
No , Sir , there be n't any doorway !
Look a he would , Peter Rabbit could not find the least sign of a doorway .
He walk ` round and ` round the mound and look here and look there , but not the least sign of a door be to be see .
There be nothing but the shin mound of yellow gravel , the green grass , the green bush and the blue , blue sky , with jolly , round , red Mr. Sun look down and laugh at him .
Peter Rabbit sit down on Striped Chipmunk 's shin mound of yellow gravel and scratch his left ear with his left hindfoot .
Then he scratch his right ear with his right hindfoot .
It be very perplexing .
Indeed , it be so perplexing that Peter quite forget that Striped Chipmunk would soon be come back .
Suddenly right behind Peter 's back Striped Chipmunk speak .
`` How do you like my sand pile , Peter Rabbit ?
Do n't you think it be a pretty nice sand pile ? ''
ask Striped Chipmunk politely .
And all the time he be chuckle away to himself .
Peter be so surprised that he very nearly fell backward off the shin mound of yellow gravel .
For a minute he do n't know what to say .
Then he find his tongue .
-LSB- Illustration : Peter be so surprised that he nearly fell backward . -RSB-
`` Oh , '' say Peter Rabbit , apparently in the great surprise , `` be this your sand pile , Striped Chipmunk ?
It 's a very nice sand pile indeed .
Is this where you live ? ''
Striped Chipmunk shake his head .
`` No , oh , my , no ! ''
say he .
`` I would n't think of live in such an exposed place !
My goodness , no indeed !
Everybody know where this be .
I 'm build a new home , you know , and of course I do n't want the gravel to clutter up my dooryard .
So I 've bring it all here .
Makes a nice sand pile , do n't it ?
You be very welcome to sit on my sand pile whenever you feel like it , Peter Rabbit .
It 's a good place to take a sun bath ; I hope you 'll come often . ''
All the time Striped Chipmunk be say this his sharp little eye twinkle with mischief and he chuckle softly to himself .
Peter Rabbit be more curious than ever .
`` Where be your new home , Striped Chipmunk ? ''
he ask .
`` Not far from here ; come call on me , '' say Striped Chipmunk .
Then with a jerk of his funny little tail he be go .
It seem a if the earth must have swallow him up .
Striped Chipmunk can move very quickly , and he have whisk out of sight in the bush before Peter Rabbit could turn his head to watch him .
Peter look behind every bush and under every stone , but nowhere could he find Striped Chipmunk or a sign of Striped Chipmunk 's home , except the shin mound of yellow gravel .
At last Peter push his inquisitive nose right into the doorway of Bumble the Bee .
Now Bumble the Bee happen to be at home , and be very short of temper , he thrust a sharp little needle into the inquisitive nose of Peter Rabbit .
`` Oh !
oh !
oh ! ''
shriek Peter , clap both hand to his nose , and start off home as fast a he could go .
And though he do n't know it and do n't know it to this day , he go right across the doorstep of Striped Chipmunk 's home .
So Peter still wonder and wonder where Striped Chipmunk live , and no one can tell him , not even the Merry Little Breezes .
You see there be not even a sign of a path lead to his doorway , for Striped Chipmunk never go or come twice the same way .
His doorway be very small , just large enough for him to squeeze through , and it be so hidden in the grass that often the Merry Little Breezes skip right over it without see it .
Every grain of sand and gravel from the fine long hall and snug chamber Striped Chipmunk have build underground he have carefully carry in the pocket in his cheek to the shin mound of yellow gravel find by Peter Rabbit .
Not so much a a grain be drop on his doorstep to let his secret out .
So in and out among the little meadow people skip Striped Chipmunk all the long day , and not one have find out where he live .
But no one really care except Peter Rabbit , who be still curious .
XIV JERRY MUSKRAT 'S NEW HOUSE Jerry Muskrat would n't play .
Billy Mink have try to get him to .
Little Joe Otter have try to get him to .
The Merry Little Breezes have try to get him to .
It be of no use , no use at all .
Jerry Muskrat would n't play .
`` Come on , Jerry , come on play with u , '' they beg all together .
But Jerry shake his head .
`` Ca n't , '' say he .
`` Why not ?
Wo n't your mother let you ? ''
demand Billy Mink , make a long dive into the Smiling Pool .
He be up again in time to hear Jerry reply : `` Yes , my mother will let me .
It be n't that .
It 's because we be go to have a long winter and a cold winter and I must prepare for it . ''
Every one laugh , every one except Grandfather Frog , who sit on his big green lily-pad watching for foolish green fly .
`` Pooh ! ''
exclaim Little Joe Otter .
`` A lot you know about it , Jerry Muskrat !
Ho , ho , ho !
A lot you know about it !
Are you clerk of the weather ?
It be only fall now -- what can you know about what the winter will be ?
Oh come , Jerry Muskrat , do n't pretend to be so wise .
I can swim twice across the Smiling Pool while you be swim across once -- come on ! ''
Jerry Muskrat shake his head .
`` Have n't time , '' say he .
`` I tell you we be go to have a long winter and a hard winter , and I 've get to prepare for it .
When it come you 'll remember what I have tell you . ''
Little Joe Otter make a wry face and slide down his slippery slide , splash into the Smiling Pool , throw water all over Jerry Muskrat , who be sit on the end of a log close by .
Jerry shake the water from his coat , which be water-proof , you know .
Everybody laugh , that be , everybody but Grandfather Frog .
He do not even smile .
`` Chug-a-rum ! ''
say Grandfather Frog , who be very wise .
`` Jerry Muskrat know .
If Jerry say that we be go to have a long cold winter you may be sure that he know what he be talk about . ''
Billy Mink turn a back somersault into the Smiling Pool so close to the big green lily-pad on which Grandfather Frog sit that the wave almost throw Grandfather Frog into the water .
`` Pooh , '' say Billy Mink , `` how can Jerry Muskrat know anything more about it than we do ? ''
Grandfather Frog look at Billy Mink severely .
He do not like Billy Mink , who have be know to gobble up some of Grandfather Frog 's child when he think that no one be look .
`` Old Mother Nature be here and tell him , '' say Grandfather Frog gruffly .
`` Oh ! ''
exclaim Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter together .
`` That 's different , '' and they look at Jerry Muskrat with great respect .
`` How be you go to prepare for the long cold winter , Jerry Muskrat ? ''
ask one of the Merry Little Breezes .
`` I 'm go to build a house , a big , warm house , '' reply Jerry Muskrat , `` and I 'm go to begin right now . ''
-LSB- Illustration : `` I 'm go , to build a house , '' reply Jerry Muskrat . -RSB-
Splash !
Jerry have disappear into the Smiling Pool .
Presently , over on the far side where the water be shallow , it begin to bubble and boil a if a great fuss be go on underneath the surface .
Jerry Muskrat have begin work .
The water grow muddy , very muddy indeed , so muddy that Little Joe Otter and Billy Mink climb out on the Big Rock in disgust .
When finally Jerry Muskrat swim out to rest on the end of a log they shout to him angrily .
`` Hi , Jerry Muskrat , you 're spoil our swimming water !
What be you do anyway ? ''
`` I 'm dig for the foundation for my new house , and it be n't your water any more than it 's mine , '' reply Jerry Muskrat , draw a long breath before he disappear under water again .
The water grow muddy and muddy , until even Grandfather Frog begin to look annoyed .
Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter start off up the Laughing Brook , where the water be clear .
The Merry Little Breezes dance away across the Green Meadows to play with Johnny Chuck , and Grandfather Frog settle himself comfortably on his big green lily-pad to dream of the day when the world be young and the frog rule the world .
But Jerry Muskrat work steadily , dig and pile sod in a circle for the foundation of his house .
In the center he dig out a chamber from which he plan a long tunnel to his secret burrow far away in the bank , and another to the deep part of the Smiling Pool , where even in the coldest weather the water would not freeze to the bottom a it would do in the shallow place .
All day long while Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and the Merry Little Breezes and Johnny Chuck and Peter Rabbit and Danny Meadow Mouse and all the other little meadow people be play or lazily take sun nap , Jerry Muskrat work steadily .
Jolly , round , red Mr. Sun , look down from the blue , blue sky , smile to see how industrious the little fellow be .
That evening , when Old Mother West Wind hurry across the Green Meadows on her way to her home behind the Purple Hills , she find Jerry Muskrat sit on the end of a log eat his supper of fresh-water clam .
Showing just above the water on the edge of the Smiling Pool be the foundation of Jerry Muskrat 's new house .
The next morning Jerry be up and at work even before Old Mother West Wind , who be a very early riser , come down from the Purple Hills .
Of course every one be interested to see how the new house be come along and to offer advice .
`` Are you go to build it all of mud ? ''
ask one of the Merry Little Breezes .
`` No , '' say Jerry Muskrat , `` I 'm go to use green alder twig and willow shoot and bulrush stalk .
It 's go to be two story high , with a room down deep under water and another room up above with a beautiful bed of grass and soft moss . ''
`` That will be splendid ! ''
cry the Merry Little Breezes .
Then one of them have an idea .
He whisper to the other Little Breezes .
They all giggle and clap their hand .
Then they hurry off to find Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter .
They even hunt up Johnny Chuck and Peter Rabbit and Danny Meadow Mouse .
Jerry Muskrat be so busy that he pay no attention to any one or anything else .
He be attend strictly to the business of build a house that would keep him warm and comfortable when the long cold winter should freeze up tight the Smiling Pool .
Pretty soon he be ready for some green twig to use in the wall of the new house .
He swim across the Smiling Pool to the Laughing Brook , where the alder grow , to cut the green twig which he need .
What do you think he find when he get there ?
Why , the nice little pile of green twig , all cut ready to use , and Johnny Chuck cut more .
`` Hello , Jerry Muskrat , '' say Johnny Chuck .
`` I 've cut all these green twig for your new house .
I hope you can use them . ''
Jerry be so surprised that he hardly know what to say .
He thank Johnny Chuck , and with the bundle of green twig swim back to his new house .
When he have use the last one he swim across to the bulrush on the edge of the Smiling Pool .
`` Good morning , Jerry Muskrat , '' say some one almost hide by a big pile of bulrush , all nicely cut .
`` I want to help build the new house . ''
It be Danny Meadow Mouse .
Jerry Muskrat be more surprised than ever .
`` Oh , thank you , Danny Meadow Mouse , thank you ! ''
he say , and push the pile of bulrush before him he swim back to his new house .
When he have use the rush , Jerry want some young willow shoot , so he start for the place where the willow grow .
Before he reach them he hear some one shouting : `` Hi , Jerry Muskrat !
See the pile of willow shoot I 've cut for your new house . ''
It be Peter Rabbit , who be never know to work .
Jerry Muskrat be more surprised than ever and so pleased that all he could say be , `` Thank you , thank you , Peter Rabbit ! ''
Back to the new house he swim with the pile of young willow shoot .
When he have place them to suit him he sit up on the wall of his house to rest .
He look across the Smiling Pool .
Then he rub his eye and look again .
Could it be -- yes , it certainly be a bundle of green alder twig float straight across the Smiling Pool towards the new house !
When they get close to him Jerry spy a sharp little black nose push them along , and back of the little black nose twinkle two little black eye .
`` What be you do with those alder twig , Billy Mink ? ''
cry Jerry .
`` Bringing them for your new house , '' shout Billy Mink , pop out from behind the bundle of alder twig .
And that be the beginning of the busy day that the Smiling Pool have ever know .
Billy Mink bring more alder twig and willow shoot and bulrush as fast a Johnny Chuck and Peter Rabbit and Danny Meadow Mouse could cut them .
Little Joe Otter bring sod and mud to hold them in place .
Thick and high grow the wall of the new house .
In the upper part Jerry build the nice little room , and line it with grass and soft moss , so that he could sleep warm and comfortable through the long cold winter .
Over all he build a strong , thick roof beautifully round .
An hour before it be time for Old Mother West Wind to come for the Merry Little Breezes , Jerry Muskrat 's new house be finish .
Then such a frolic a there be in and around the Smiling Pool !
Little Joe Otter make a new slippery slide down one side of the roof .
Billy Mink say that the new house be good to dive off of than the Big Rock .
Then the two of them , with Jerry Muskrat , cut up all sort of monkey-shines in the water , while Johnny Chuck , Peter Rabbit , Danny Meadow Mouse and the Merry Little Breezes dance on the shore and shout themselves hoarse .
When at last jolly , round , red Mr. Sun go to bed behind the Purple Hills , and the black shadow creep ever so softly out across the Smiling Pool , Jerry Muskrat sit on the roof of his house eat his supper of fresh-water clam .
He be very tired , be Jerry Muskrat , very tired indeed , but he be very happy , for now he have no fear of the long cold winter .
Best of all his heart be full of love -- love for his little playmate of the Smiling Pool and the Green Meadows .
XV PETER RABBIT 'S BIG COUSIN Jumper the Hare have come down out of the Great Woods to the Green Meadows .
He be first cousin to Peter Rabbit , you know , and he look just like Peter , only he be twice as big .
His leg be twice a long and he can jump twice a far .
All the little meadow people be very polite to Jumper the Hare , all but Reddy Fox , who be never polite to any one unless he have a favor to ask .
Peter Rabbit be very proud of his big cousin , very proud indeed .
He show Jumper the Hare all the secret path in the Green Forest and across the Green Meadows .
He take him to the Smiling Pool and the Laughing Brook , and everywhere Jumper the Hare be meet with the great politeness .
But Jumper the Hare be timid , oh , very timid indeed .
Every few jump he sit up very straight to look this way and look that way , and to listen with his long ear .
He jump nervously at the least little noise .
Yes , Sir , Jumper the Hare certainly be very timid .
`` He 's a coward ! ''
sneer Reddy Fox .
And Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter and Jimmy Skunk , even Johnny Chuck , see Jumper the Hare duck and dodge at the shadow of Blacky the Crow , agree with Reddy Fox .
Still , they be polite to him for the sake of Peter Rabbit and because Jumper really be such a big , handsome fellow .
But behind his back they laugh at him .
Even little Danny Meadow Mouse laugh .
Now it happen that Jumper the Hare have live all his life in the Great Woods , where Mr. Panther and Tufty the Lynx and fierce Mr. Fisher be always hunt him , but where the shadow be deep and where there be plenty of place to hide .
Indeed , his whole life have be a game of hide and seek , and always he have be the one sought .
So on the Green Meadows , where hide place be few and far between , Jumper the Hare be nervous .
But the little meadow people , not know this , think him a coward , and while they be polite to him they have little to do with him , for no one really like a coward .
Peter Rabbit , however , could see no fault in his big cousin .
He show him where Farmer Brown 's tender young carrot grow , and the short way to the cabbage patch .
He make him acquaint with all his own secret hiding place in the old brier patch .
Then one bright sunny morning something happen .
Johnny Chuck saw it .
Jimmy Skunk saw it .
Happy Jack Squirrel saw it .
Sammy Jay saw it .
And they tell all the others .
Very early that morning Reddy Fox have start out to hunt for his breakfast .
He be tiptoe softly along the edge of the Green Forest look for wood mouse when whom should he see but Peter Rabbit .
Peter be get his breakfast in the sweet-clover bed , just beyond the old brier patch .
Reddy Fox squat down behind a bush to watch .
Peter Rabbit look plump and fat .
Reddy Fox lick his chop .
`` Peter Rabbit would make a good breakfast than wood mouse , a very much good breakfast , '' say Reddy Fox to himself .
Beside , he owe Peter Rabbit a grudge .
He have not forget how Peter have try to save his little brother from Reddy by bring up Bowser the Hound .
Reddy Fox lick his chop again .
He look this way and he look that way , but he could see no one watching .
Old Mother West Wind have go about her business .
The Merry Little Breezes be over at the Smiling Pool to pay their respect to Grandfather Frog .
Even jolly , round , red Mr. Sun be behind a cloud .
From his hide place Reddy could not see Johnny Chuck or Jimmy Skunk or Happy Jack Squirrel or Sammy Jay .
`` No one will know what become of Peter Rabbit , '' think Reddy Fox .
Very cautiously Reddy Fox creep out from behind the bush into the tall meadow grass .
Flat on his stomach he crawl inch by inch .
Every few minute he stop to listen and to peep over at the sweet-clover bed .
There sat Peter Rabbit , eat , eat , eat the tender young clover a if he have n't a care in the world but to fill his little round stomach .
Nearer and nearer crawl Reddy Fox .
Now he be almost near enough to spring .
`` Thump , thump , thump ! ''
The sound come from the brier patch .
`` Thump , thump ! ''
This be Peter Rabbit hit the ground with one of his hind foot .
He have stop eat and be sit up very straight .
`` Thump , thump , thump ! ''
come the signal from the brier patch .
`` Thump , thump ! ''
respond Peter Rabbit , and start to run .
With a snarl Reddy Fox sprang after him .
Then the thing happen .
Reddy Fox catch a glimpse of something go over him and at the same time he receive a blow that roll him over and over in the grass .
In an instant he be on his foot and have whirl about , his eye yellow with anger .
There right in front of him sit Jumper the Hare .
Reddy Fox could hardly believe his own eye !
Could it be that Jumper the Hare , the coward , have dare to strike him such a blow ?
Reddy forget all about Peter Rabbit .
With a snarl he rush at Jumper the Hare .
Then it happen again .
As light a a feather Jumper leap over him , and a he pass , those big hind leg , at which Reddy Fox have laugh , come back with a kick that knock all the breath out of Reddy Fox .
Reddy Fox be furious .
Twice more he spring , and twice more he be send sprawling , with the breath knock out of his body .
That be enough .
Tucking his tail between his leg , Reddy Fox sneak away towards the Green Forest .
As he run he hear Peter Rabbit thump in the old brier patch .
`` I 'm safe , '' signal Peter Rabbit .
`` Thump , thump , thump , thump !
The coast be clear , '' reply Jumper the Hare .
Reddy Fox look back from the edge of the Green Forest and gnash his teeth .
Peter Rabbit and Jumper the Hare be rub nose and contentedly eat tender young clover leave .
`` Now who 's the coward ? ''
jeered Sammy Jay from the top of the Lone Pine .
Reddy Fox say nothing , but slink out of sight .
Late that afternoon he sit on the hill at the top of the Crooked Little Path , and look down on the Green Meadows .
Over near the Smiling Pool be gather all the little meadow people have the jolly time in the world .
While he watch they join hand in a big circle and begin to dance , Johnny Chuck , Jimmy Skunk , Bobby Coon , Little Joe Otter , Billy Mink , Happy Jack Squirrel , Striped Chipmunk , Danny Meadow Mouse , Peter Rabbit , Spotty the Turtle , even Grandfather Frog and old Mr. Toad .
And in the middle , sit very straight , be Jumper the Hare .
And since that day Peter Rabbit have be prouder than ever of his big cousin , Jumper the Hare , for now no one call him a coward .

CHAPTER I PETER RABBIT LOSES HIS APPETITE Good appetite , you 'll always find , Depends upon your state of mind .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit have lose his appetite .
Now when Peter Rabbit lose his appetite , something be very wrong indeed with him .
Peter have boast that he can eat any time and all the time .
In fact , the two thing that Peter think most about be his stomach and satisfy his curiosity , and nearly all of the scrape that Peter have get into have be because of those two thing .
So when Peter lose his appetite or his curiosity , there be surely something the matter with him .
Ever since Old Man Coyote have come to live on the Green Meadows , Peter have be afraid to go very far from the dear Old Briar-patch where he make his home , and where he always feel safe .
Now there be n't any reason why he should go far from the dear Old Briar-patch .
There be plenty to eat in it and all around it , for sweet clover grow almost up to the very edge of it , and you know Peter be very fond of sweet clover .
So there be plenty for Peter to eat without run any risk of danger .
With nothing to do but eat and sleep , Peter should have grow fat and content .
But he do n't .
Now that be just the way with a lot of people .
The more they have and the less they have to worry about , the more discontented they become , and at last they be positively unhappy .
There be little Danny Meadow Mouse , live out on the Green Meadows ; he be happy all the livelong day , and yet he have no safe castle like the dear Old Briar-patch where he could always be safe .
Every minute of every day Danny have to keep his eye wide open and his wit work their very quick , for any minute he be likely to be in danger .
Old Man Coyote or Reddy Fox or Granny Fox or Digger the Badger or Mr. Blacksnake be likely to come creep through the grass any time , and they be always hungry for a fat Meadow Mouse .
And a if that be n't worry enough , Danny have to watch the sky , too , for Old Whitetail the Marsh Hawk , or his cousin Redtail , or Blacky the Crow , each of whom would be glad of a Meadow Mouse dinner .
Yet in spite of all this , Danny be happy and never once lose his appetite .
But Peter Rabbit , with nothing to worry him so long a he stay in the Old Briar-patch , could n't eat and grow more and more unhappy .
`` I do n't know what 's the matter with me .
I really do n't know what 's the matter with me , '' say Peter , a he turn up his nose at a patch of sweet , tender young clover .
`` I think I 'll go and cut some new path through the Old Briar-patch . ''
Now , though he do n't know it , that be the very best thing he could do .
It give him something to think about .
For two or three day he be very busy cut new path , and his appetite come back .
But when he have make all the path he want , and there be nothing else to do , he lose his appetite again .
He just sit still all day long and mop and think and think and think .
The trouble with Peter Rabbit 's thinking be that it be all about himself and how unhappy he be .
Of course , the more he think about this , the more unhappy he grow .
`` If I only have some one to talk to , I 'd feel well , '' say he to himself .
That remind him of Johnny Chuck and what good time they use to have together when Johnny live on the Green Meadows .
Then he think of how happy Johnny seem with his little family in his new home in the Old Orchard , in spite of all the worry his family make him .
And right then Peter find out what be the matter with him .
`` I believe I 'm just lonesome , '' say Peter .
`` Yes , Sir , that 's what 's the matter with me .
`` It be n't good to be alone , I 've often hear my mother say .
It make one selfish , grouchy , cross , And quite unhappy all the day .
One need to think of other folk , And not of just one 's self alone , To find the true happiness , And joy and real content to own .
`` Now that I 've find out what be the trouble with me , the question be , what be I go to do about it ? ''
CHAPTER II PETER RABBIT PLANS A JOURNEY It 's a long jump that make no landing .
Peter Rabbit .
`` The trouble with me be that I 'm lonesome , '' repeat Peter Rabbit a he sit in the dear Old Briar-patch .
`` Yes , Sir , that 's the only thing that 's wrong with me .
I 'm just tire of myself , and that 's why I 've lose my appetite .
And now I know what 's the matter , what be I go to do about it ?
If I be sure , absolutely sure , that Old Man Coyote mean what he say about our be friend , I 'd start out this very minute to call on all my old friend .
My , my , my , it seem an age since I visit the Smiling Pool and saw Grandfather Frog and Jerry Muskrat and Billy Mink and Little Joe Otter !
Mr. Coyote sound a if he really mean to leave me alone , but , but -- well , perhaps he do mean it when he saw me sit here safe among the bramble , but if I should meet him out in the open , he might change his mind and -- oh , dear , his teeth be terrible long and sharp ! ''
Peter sit a little long , think and thinking .
Then a bright idea pop into his head .
He kick up his heel .
`` I 'll do it , '' say he .
`` I 'll make a journey !
That 's what I 'll do !
I 'll make a journey and see the Great World .
`` By stay here and sit still I 'm sure I 'll simply grow quite ill .
A change of scene be what I need To be from all my trouble freed . ''
Of course if Peter have really stop to think the matter over thoroughly he would have know that run away from one kind of trouble be almost sure to lead to other trouble .
But Peter be one of those who do his think afterward .
Peter be what be call impulsive .
That be , he do thing and then think about them later , and often wish he have n't do them .
So now the minute the idea of make a journey pop into his head , he make up his mind that he would do it , and that be all there be to it .
You see , Peter never look ahead .
If he could get rid of the trouble that bother him now , which , you know , be nothing but lonesomeness , he would n't worry about the trouble he might get into later .
Now the minute Peter make up his mind to make a journey , he begin to feel well .
His lose appetite return , and the first thing he do be to eat a good meal of sweet clover .
`` Let me see , '' say he , a he fill his big stomach , `` I believe I 'll visit the Old Pasture .
It 's a long way off and I 've never be there , but I 've hear Sammy Jay say that it 's a very wonderful place , and I do n't believe it be any more dangerous than the Green Meadows and the Green Forest , now that Old Man Coyote and Reddy and Granny Fox be all living here .
I 'll start tonight when I be sure that Old Man Coyote be nowhere around , and I wo n't tell a soul where I be go . ''
So Peter settle himself and try to sleep the long day away , but his mind be so full of the long journey he be go to make that he could n't sleep much , and when he do have a nap , he dream of wonderful sight and adventure out in the Great World .
At last he saw jolly , round , red Mr. Sun drop down to his bed behind the Purple Hills .
Old Mother West Wind come hurry back from her day 's work and gather her child , the Merry Little Breezes , into her big bag , and then she , too , start for her home behind the Purple Hills .
A little star come out and wink at Peter , and then way over on the edge of the Green Forest he hear Old Man Coyote laugh .
Peter grin .
That be what he have be wait for , since it mean that Old Man Coyote be so far away that there be nothing to fear from him .
Peter hop out from the dear , safe Old Briar-patch , look this way and that way , and then , with his heart in his mouth , start towards the Old Pasture as fast a he could go , lipperty -- lipperty -- lip .
CHAPTER III HOOTY THE OWL CHANGES HIS HUNTING GROUNDS A full stomach make a pleasant Day ; An empty stomach turn the whole world gray .
Peter Rabbit .
Hooty the owl sit on the tip-top of a tall dead tree in the Green Forest while the Black Shadows creep swiftly among the tree .
He be talk to himself .
It would n't have do for him to have speak aloud what he be say to himself , for then the little people in feather and fur on whom he like to make his dinner would have hear him and know just where he be .
So he say it to himself , and sit so still that he look for all the world like a part of the tree on which he be sit .
What he be say be this : `` Towhit , towhoo !
Towhit , towhoo !
Will some one tell me what to do ?
My child have an appetite That keep me hunt all the night , And though their stomach I may stuff They never seem to have enough .
Towhit , towhoo !
Towhit , towhoo !
Will some one tell me what to do ? ''
When it be dark enough he give his fierce hunt call -- `` Whooo-hoo - hoo , whoo-hoo ! ''
Now that be a terrible sound in the dark wood , very terrible indeed to the little forest people , because it sound so fierce and hungry .
It make them jump and shiver , and that be just what Hooty want them to do , for in do it one of them be likely to make just the least scratching with his claw , or to rustle a leaf .
If he do , Hooty , whose ear be very , very wonderful , be almost sure to hear , and with his great yellow eye see him , and then -- Hooty have his dinner .
The very night when Peter Rabbit start on his journey to the Old Pasture , Hooty the Owl have make up his mind that something have get to be do to get more food for those hungry baby of his up in the big hemlock-tree in the dark corner of the Green Forest .
Hunting be very poor , very poor indeed , and Hooty be at his wit ' end to know what he should do .
He have hoot and hoot in vain in the Green Forest , and he have sail back and forth over the Green Meadows like a great black shadow without see so much a a single Mouse .
`` It 's all because of Old Man Coyote and Granny and Reddy Fox , '' say Hooty angrily .
`` They 've spoil the hunting .
Yes , Sir , that 's just what they have do !
If I expect to fee those hungry baby of mine , I must find new hunt ground .
I believe I 'll go up to the Old Pasture .
Perhaps I 'll have good luck up there . ''
So Hooty the Owl spread his broad wing and start for the Old Pasture just a little while after Peter Rabbit have start for the same place .
Of course he do n't know that Peter be on his way there , and of course Peter do n't know that Hooty even think of the Old Pasture .
If he have , perhaps he would have think twice before start .
Anyway , he would have keep a sharp watch on the sky .
But a it be his thought be all of Old Man Coyote and Granny Fox , and that be where Peter make a very grave mistake , a very grave mistake indeed , a he be soon to find out .
CHAPTEE IV THE SHADOW WITH SHARP CLAWS Now what 's the use , pray tell me this , When all be say and do ; A thousand thing and one to learn And then forget the one ?
For when that one alone you need , And nothing else will do , What good be all the thousand then ?
I do not see ; do you ?
Peter Rabbit .
Forgetting lead to more trouble than almost anything under the sun .
Peter Rabbit know this .
Of course he know it .
Peter have have many a narrow escape just from forget something .
He know just as well a you know that he might just as well not learn a thing a to learn it and then forget it .
But Peter be such a happy-go-lucky little fellow that he be very apt to forget , and forget lead him into all kind of difficulty , just a it do most folk .
Now Peter have learn when he be a very little fellow that when he go out at night , he must watch out quite a sharply for Hooty the Owl a for either Granny or Reddy Fox , and usually he do .
But the night he start to make a journey to the Old Pasture , his mind be so full of Old Man Coyote and Granny and Reddy Fox that he wholly forget Hooty the Owl .
So , a he scamper across the Green Meadows , lipperty -- lipperty -- lip , as fast a he could go , with his long ear and his big eye and his wobbly nose all watch out for danger on the ground , not once do he think that there might be danger from the sky above him .
It be a moonlight night , and Peter be sharp enough to keep in the shadow whenever he could .
He would scamper as fast a he know how from one shadow to another and then sit down in the black part of each shadow to get his breath , and to look and listen and so make sure that no one be follow him .
The nearer he get to the Old Pasture , the safer he felt from Old Man Coyote and Granny and Reddy Fox .
When he scamper across the patch of moonshine his heart do n't come up in his mouth the way it have at first .
He grow bolder and bolder .
Once or twice he stop for a mouthful of sweet clover .
He be tire , for he have come a long way , but he be almost to the Old Pasture now , and it look very dark and safe , for it be cover with bush and bramble .
`` Plenty of hide place there , '' think Peter .
`` It really look as safe a the dear Old Briar-patch .
No one will ever think to look for me way off here . ''
Just then he spy a patch of sweet clover out in the moonlight .
His mouth begin to water .
`` I 'll just fill my stomach before I go into the Old Pasture , for there may not be any clover there , '' say Peter .
`` You 'd well be careful , Peter Rabbit , '' say a wee warn voice inside him .
`` Pooh ! ''
say Peter .
`` There 's nothing to be afraid of way up here ! ''
A shadow drift across the sweet clover patch .
Peter saw it .
`` That must be make by a cloud cross the moon , '' say Peter , and he be so sure of it that he do n't even look up to see , but boldly hop out to fill his stomach .
Just a he reach the patch of clover , the shadow drift over it again .
Then all in a flash a terrible thought enter Peter 's head .
He do n't stop to look up .
He suddenly spring sideways , and even a he do so , sharp claw tear his coat and hurt him dreadfully .
He twist and dodge and jump and turn this way and that way , and all the time the shadow follow him .
Once again sharp claw tear his coat and make him squeal with pain .
