At last , when his breath be almost go , he reach the edge of the Old Pasture and dive under a friendly old bramble-bush .
`` Oh , '' sob Peter , `` I forget all about Hooty the Owl !
Besides , I do n't suppose he ever come way up here . ''
CHAPTER V IN THE OLD PASTURE Brambles never scratch those who understand and be considerate of them .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit sit under a friendly bramble-bush on the edge of the Old Pasture and pant for breath , while his heart go pit-a-pat , pit-a - pat , a if it would thump it way right through his side .
Peter have have a terrible fright .
There be long tear in his coat , and he smart and ache dreadfully where the cruel claw of Hooty the Owl have tear him .
And there he be in a strange place , not know which way to turn , for you know he never have visit the Old Pasture before .
But Peter have have so many narrow escape in his life that he have learn not to worry over danger that be past .
Peter be what wise men call a phi-los-o-pher .
That be a big word , but it meaning be very simple .
A philosopher be one who believe that it be foolish to think about thing that have happen , except to learn some lesson from them , and that the best thing to do be to make the most of the present .
Peter have learn his lesson .
He be sure of that .
`` I never , never will forget again to watch out for Hooty the Owl , '' say he to himself , a he nurse his wound , `` and so perhaps it be a good thing that he so nearly catch me this time .
If he have n't , I might have forget all about him some time when he could catch me .
I certainly would n't have watch out for him way up here , for I do n't think he ever come up to the Old Pasture .
But now I know he do , Mr. Hooty 'll have to be smart than he 's ever be before to catch me nap again .
My , how I do smart and ache !
I know now just how Danny Meadow Mouse felt that time Hooty catch him and drop him into the Old Briar-patch .
Ouch !
Well , a my mother use to say : ` Yesterday have go away ; Make the most of just to-day . '
Here I be up in the Old Pasture , and the question be , what shall I do next ? ''
Peter felt a queer little thrill a he peep out from under the friendly bramble-bush .
Very strange and wonderful it seem .
Of course he could n't see very far , because the Old Pasture be all overgrown with bush and briar , and they make the very black of black shadow in the moonlight .
Peter wonder what danger might be await him there , but somehow he do n't feel much afraid .
No , Sir , he do n't feel much afraid .
You see those briar look good to him , for briar be always friendly to Peter and unfriendly to those who would do harm to Peter .
So when he saw them , he felt almost at home .
Peter draw a long breath .
Then he cry `` Ouch ! ''
You see , he have forget for a minute how sore he be .
He be eager to explore this new wonderland , for Sammy Jay have tell him wonderful tale about it , and he know that here old Granny Fox and Reddy Fox have find safety when Farmer Brown 's boy have hunt for them so hard on the Green Meadows and in the Green Forest .
He felt sure that there must be the most splendid hiding - place , and it seem a if he certainly must start right out to see them , for you know Peter be very , very curious .
But the first move he make bring another `` Ouch '' from him , and he make up a wry face .
`` I guess the best thing for me to do be to stay right where I be , '' say he , `` for here I be safe under this friendly old bramble . ''
So with a sigh Peter settle down to make himself as comfortable a he could , and once , a far , far away on the Green Meadows he hear the voice of Old Man Coyote , Peter even smile .
`` I have n't anything to fear from him , anyway , for he 'll never think of come way up here , '' say he .
CHAPTER VI PETER RABBIT IS STILL LONESOME A sympathetic word or two A wond ` rous help be , when you 're blue .
So pity him who sit alone His ache and trouble to bemoan .
Peter Rabbit .
All the rest of that night Peter sit under a friendly old bramble-bush on the edge of the Old Pasture and nurse the sore place make by the claw of Hooty the Owl .
At last jolly , round , red Mr. Sun begin to climb up in the blue , blue sky , just a he do every day .
Peter look up at him , and he felt sure that Mr. Sun wink at him .
Somehow it make him feel well .
The fact be , Peter be begin to feel just a wee , wee bit homesick .
It be bad enough to be in a strange place alone , but to be sore and to smart and ache a Peter do make that lonesome feel a whole lot hard to bear .
It be dreadful not to have any one to speak to , but to look around and not see a single thing you have ever see before , -- my , my , my , it certainly do give you a strange , sink feel way down inside !
Before that long night be over Peter felt a if his heart have go way down to his very toe .
Yes , Sir , that 's the way he felt .
Every time he move at all he cry `` Ouch ! ''
He just know that he be grow more stiff and sore every minute .
Then he begin to wonder what he should do for something to eat , for he be in a strange place , you remember .
And that make him think of all his private little path through the dear Old Briar-patch , the little path he have make all himself , and which no one use but himself , except Danny Meadow Mouse when he come for a visit .
`` Perhaps I shall never , never see them again , '' moan Peter , and two big tear fill his eye and be just ready to drop .
At that moment he look up and saw jolly , round , red Mr. Sun wink .
Peter try to wink back , and that make the two tear fall .
But there be no more tear to follow .
You see that wink have make all the difference in the world , Peter 's heart have jump right back where it belong .
Mr. Sun be one of his old friend and you know When trouble come , a friendly face Makes bright the very dark place .
And so , just a he make bright all the Old Pasture , Mr. Sun also make bright the dark little corner in Peter 's heart just because he be an old friend .
To be sure Peter be still lonesome , but it be a different kind of lonesomeness .
He have n't anybody to talk to , which be always a dreadful thing to Peter , but he have only to look up to catch a friendly wink , and somehow that not only make him feel well inside but it seem to make his ache and smart well too .
CHAPTER VII PETER FINDS TRACKS Every day be different from every other day , And always there be something new to see along the way .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit have sit still just as long a he could .
He be stiff and lame and sore from the wound make by Hooty the Owl , but his curiosity would n't let him sit still a minute longer .
He just HAD to explore the Old Pasture .
So with many a wry face and many an `` Ouch '' he limp out from the shelter of the friendly old bramble-bush and start out to see what the Old Pasture be like .
Now Hooty the Owl have teach Peter wisdom .
With his torn clothes and his ache and smart he could n't very well forget to be careful .
First he make sure that there be no danger near , and this time he take pain to look all around in the sky as well a on the ground .
Then he limp out to the very patch of sweet clover where Hooty have so nearly catch him the night before .
`` A good breakfast , '' say Peter , `` will make a new Rabbit of me . ''
You know Peter think a great deal of his stomach .
So he begin to eat as fast a he could , stop every other mouthful to look and listen .
`` I know it 's a bad habit to eat fast , '' say he , `` but it 's a whole lot bad to have an empty stomach . ''
So he eat and eat and eat as fast a he could make his little jaw go , which be very fast indeed .
When Peter 's stomach be stuff full he give a great sigh of relief and limp back to the friendly old bramble-bush to rest .
But he could n't sit still long , for he just have to find out all about the Old Pasture .
So pretty soon he start out to explore .
Such a wonderful place a it seem to Peter !
There be clump of bush with little open space between , just the nice kind of playground .
Then there be funny spreading , prickly juniper-trees , which make the very safe place to crawl out of harm 's way and to hide .
Everywhere be path make by cow .
Very wonderful they seem to Peter , who have never see any like them before .
He like to follow them because they lead to all kind of queer place .
Sometimes he would come to place where tall tree make him think of the Green Forest , only there be never more than a few tree together .
Once he find an old tumble-down stone wall all cover with vine , and he shout right out with delight .
`` It 's a regular castle ! ''
cry Peter , and he know that there he would be safe from every one but Shadow the Weasel .
But he never be wholly safe from Shadow the Weasel anywhere , so he do n't let that thought worry him .
By and by he come to a wet place call a swamp .
The ground be soft , and there be little pool of water .
Great ferns grow here just a they do along the bank of the Laughing Brook , only more of them .
There be pretty birch-trees and wild cherry-trees .
It be still and dark and oh , so peaceful !
Peter like that place and sit down under a big fern to rest .
He do n't hear a sound except the beautiful silvery voice of Veery the Thrush .
Listening to it , Peter fell asleep , for he be very tired .
By and by Peter awoke .
For a minute he could n't think where he be .
Then he remember .
But for a long time he sit perfectly still , think of his adventure and wonder if he would be miss down on the Green Meadows .
Then all of a sudden Peter saw something that make him sit up so suddenly that he cry `` Ouch ! ''
for he have forget all about how stiff and sore he be .
What do you think Peter saw ?
Tracks !
Yes , Sir , he saw track , Rabbit track in the soft mud , and Peter know that he have n't make them !
CHAPTER VIII THE STRANGE TRACKS IN THE OLD PASTURE Who have attentive ear and eye Will learn a lot if he but try .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit star and star at the track in the soft mud of the swamp in the Old Pasture .
He would look first at the track , then at his own foot , and finally back at the track again .
He scratch his long right ear with his long right hind foot .
Then he scratch his long left ear with his long left hind foot , all the time star his hardest at those strange track .
They certainly be the track of a Rabbit , and it be equally certain that they be not his own .
`` They be too big for mine , and they be too small for Jumper the Hare 's .
Besides , Jumper be in the Green Forest and not way off up here , '' say Peter to himself .
`` I wonder -- well , I wonder if he will try to drive me away . ''
You see Peter know that if he have find a strange Rabbit in his dear Old Briar-patch he certainly would have try his best to drive him out , for he felt that the Old Briar-patch belong to him .
Now he wonder if the maker of these track would feel the same way about the Old Pasture .
Peter look troubled a he think it over .
Then his face clear .

The white patch on the seat of his trouser be stain and dirty from sit down in the mud .
There be burr tangle in his waistcoat .
He be thin and altogether a miserable look Rabbit .
`` It must be that Miss Fuzzytail just pity me .
She certainly ca n't admire me , '' mutter Peter , a he pull out the burr .
For the next hour Peter be very busy .
He wash and he brush and he comb .
When , at last , he have do all that he could , he take another look in his looking-glass , and what he saw be a very different look Rabbit .
`` Though I be homely , lank and lean , I can at least be neat and clean , '' say he , a he start back for the sunning-bank .
CHAPTER XVII PETER MEETS MISS FUZZYTAIL That this be true there 's no denying -- There 's nothing in the world like try .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit be feel good .
Certainly he be look good .
You see , just as soon a Old Mother Nature saw that Peter be try to look as well a he could , and be keep himself a neat and tidy a he know how , she be ready to help , a she always be .
She do her best with the rent in his coat , make by the claw of Hooty the Owl and the teeth of Old Jed Thumper , and so it be n't long before Peter 's coat look nearly as good a new .
Then , too , Peter be get enough to eat these day .
Days and day have pass since he have see Old Jed Thumper , and this have give him time to eat and sleep .
Peter wonder what have become of Old Jed Thumper .
`` Perhaps something have happen to him , '' think Peter .
`` I -- I almost hope something have . ''
Then , be ashamed of such a wish , he add , `` Something not very dreadful , but which will keep him from hunt me for a while and try to drive me out of the Old Pasture . ''
Now all this time Peter have be try to find little Miss Fuzzytail .
He be already in love with her , although all he have see of her be her two soft , gentle eye , shyly peep at him from behind a big fern .
He have wander here and saunter there , look for her , but although he find her footprint very often , she always manage to keep out of his sight , You see , she know the Old Pasture so much good than he do , and all the little path in it , that she have very little trouble in keep out of his way .
Then , too , she be very busy , for it be she who be keep her cross father , Old Jed Thumper , away from Peter , because she be so sorry for Peter .
But Peter do n't know this .
If he have , I be afraid that he would have be more in love than ever .
The harder she be to find , the more Peter want to find her .
He spend a great deal of time each day brush his coat and make himself look as fine a he could , and while he be do it , he keep wish over and over again that something would happen so that he could show little Miss Fuzzytail what a smart , brave fellow he really be .
But one day follow another , and Peter seem no nearer than ever to meet little Miss Fuzzytail .
He be think of this one morning and be really grow very down-hearted , a he sit under a friendly bramble-bush , when suddenly there be a sharp little scream of fright from behind a little juniper-tree .
Somehow Peter know whose voice that be , although he never have hear it before .
He spring around the little juniper-tree , and what he saw fill him with such rage that he do n't once stop to think of himself .
There be little Miss Fuzzytail in the clutch of Black Pussy , Farmer Brown 's cat , who often steal away from home to hunt in the Old Pasture .
Like a flash Peter sprang over Black Pussy , and a he do so he kick with all his might .
The cat have n't see him come , and the kick knock her right into the prickly juniper-tree .
Of course she lose her grip on little Miss Fuzzytail , who have n't be hurt so much a frightened .
By the time the cat get out of the juniper-tree , Peter and Miss Fuzzytail be sit side by side safe in the middle of a bull-briar patch .
`` Oh ?
how brave you be ! ''
sob little Miss Fuzzytail .
And this be the way that Peter Rabbit at last get his heart 's desire .
CHAPTER XVIII TOMMY TIT PROVES A FRIEND INDEED Nothing in all the world be so precious a a true friend .
Peter Rabbit .
After Peter Rabbit have save little Miss Fuzzytail from Black Pussy , the cat who belong way down at Farmer Brown 's house and have no business hunt in the Old Pasture , he go with her a near to her home a she would let him .

Miss Fuzzytail laugh at that , for she felt quite able to take care of herself .

So Peter be force to go back , but he take with him a half promise that she would meet him the next night up near his sunning-bank in the far corner of the Old Pasture .
After that there be many pleasant day for Peter Rabbit .
Sometimes little Miss Fuzzytail would meet him , and sometimes she would shyly hide from , him , but somehow , somewhere , he manage to see her every day , and so all the time in Peter 's heart be a little song : `` The sky be blue ; the leaf be green ; The golden sunbeam peep between ; My heart be joyful a can be , And all the world look bright to me . ''
And then one day Old Jed Thumper find out all about how his daughter , little Miss Fuzzytail , and Peter Rabbit have become such good friend .
Old Jed Thumper go into a terrible rage .
He chew and chew with nothing in his mouth , that be , nothing but his temper , the way an angry Rabbit will .
He vow and declare that if he never eat another mouthful he would drive Peter Rabbit from the Old Pasture .
My , my , my , those be bad day for Peter Rabbit !
Yes , Sir , those certainly be bad day !
Old Jed Thumper have find out how little Miss Fuzzytail have be fool him by make him think Peter be in part of the Old Pasture in quite the opposite direction from where he really be .
Worse still , he find Peter 's favorite sunning-bank in the far corner of the Old Pasture and would hide near it and try to catch Peter every time Peter try to get a few minute ' rest there .
He do something bad than that .
One day he saw fierce Mr. Goshawk hunt .
He let Mr. Goshawk almost catch him .
and then duck under a bramble-bush .
Then he show himself again and once more escaped in the same way .
So he lead fierce Mr. Goshawk to a point where Mr. Goshawk could look down and see Peter Rabbit stretch out on his sunning-bank , try to get a little rest .
Right ; away Mr. Goshawk forget all about Old Jed Thumper and sail up in the sky from where he could swoop down on Peter , while Old Jed Thumper , chuckle to himself wickedly , hid where he could watch what would happen .
That certainly would have be the last of Peter Rabbit if it have n't be for Tommy Tit the Chickadee .
Tommy saw Mr. Goshawk and just in time warn Peter , and so Mr. Goshawk get only his claws full of soft earth for his pain , while Old Jed Thumper once more chewed on nothing in rage and disappointment .
Dear me , dear me , those certainly be dreadful day for Peter Rabbit and little Miss Fuzzytail .
You see , all the time little Miss Fuzzytail be terribly worry for fear Peter would be catch .

CHAPTER XIX OLD MAN COYOTE PAYS A DEBT Some little seed of goodness You 'll find in every heart , To sprout and keep on grow When once they get a start .
Peter Rabbit .
Matters go from bad to worse with Peter Rabbit and little Miss Fuzzytail .
Peter would have make up his mind to go back to his old home in the dear Old Briar-patch on the Green Meadows , but he felt that he just could n't leave little Miss Fuzzytail , and little Miss Fuzzytail could n't make up her mind to go with Peter , because she felt that she just could n't leave the Old Pasture , which always have be her home .
So Peter spend his day and night ready to jump and run from Jed Thumper , the gray old Rabbit who think he own the Old Pasture , and who have declare that he would drive Peter out .
Now Peter , a you know , have an old friend in the Old Pasture , Tommy Tit the Chickadee .

There he find everybody wonder what have become of Peter Rabbit , for you remember Peter have steal away from the dear Old Briar-patch in the night and have tell no one where he be go .

Tommy tell him where Peter be and of the dreadful time Peter be have , Old Man Coyote ask a lot of question about the Old Pasture and thank Tommy very politely a Tommy fly over to the Smiling Pool to call on Grandfather Frog and Jerry Muskrat .

Pretty soon he come to a bramble-bush , and under it he could see Old Jed Thumper .
For just a minute he chuckle , a noiseless chuckle , to himself .
Then he open his mouth and out come that terrible sound which have so frighten all the little people on the Green Meadows when Old Man Coyote have first come there to live .
`` Ha , ha , ha !
Ho , ho , ho !
Hee , hee , hee !
Ha , ho , hee , ho ! ''
Old Jed Thumper never have hear anything like that before .
It frighten him so that before he think what he be do he have jump out from under the bramble-bush .
Of course this be just what Old Man Coyote want .
In a flash he be after him , and then begin such a race a the Old Pasture never have see before .
Round and round , this way and that way , along the cow path race Old Jed Thumper with Old Man Coyote at his heel , until at last , out of breath , so tired that it seem to him he could n't run another step , frighten almost out of his sens , Old Jed Thumper reach his bull-briar castle and be safe .
Then Old Man Coyote laugh his terrible laugh once more and trot over to the tumble-down stone-wall in which his keen nose tell him Peter Rabbit be hide .
`` One good turn deserve another , and I always pay my debt , Peter Rabbit '' say he .
`` You do me a good turn some time ago down on the Green Meadows , when you tell me how Granny and Reddy Fox be plan to make trouble for me by lead Bowser the Hound to the place where I take my daily nap , and now we be even .
I do n't think that old gray Rabbit will dare to poke so much a his nose out of his bull-briar castle for a week .
Now I be go back to the Green Meadows , Good night , Peter Rabbit , and do n't forget that I always pay my debt . ''
`` Good night , and thank you , Mr. Coyote , '' say Peter , and then , when Old Man Coyote have go , he add to himself in a shame-faced way : `` I do n't believe him when he say that he guess we would be friend . ''

Peter Rabbit .

CHAPTER XXI PETER AND LITTLE MISS FUZZYTAIL LEAVE THE OLD PASTURE A danger past be a danger past , So why not just forget it ?
Watch out instead for the one ahead Until you 've safely meet it , Peter Rabbit .
As soon a little Miss Fuzzytail have agree to go with him to make her home in the dear Old Briar-patch down on the Green Meadows , Peter Rabbit fairly boil over with impatience to start , He have have so much trouble in the Old Pasture that he be afraid if they wait too long little Miss Fuzzytail might change her mind , and if she should do that -- well , Peter do n't know what he would do .
But Peter , who always have be so happy-go-lucky , with no one to think about but himself , now felt for the first time re-sponsi-bil-ity .
That 's a big word , but it be a word that everybody have to learn the meaning of sometime .
Johnny Chuck learn it when he make a home for Polly Chuck in Farmer Brown 's orchard , and try to keep it a secret , so that no harm would come to Polly .
It mean take care of other people or other people 's thing , and feel that you must take even great care than you would of yourself or your own thing , So , while Peter himself would have be willing to take chance , and might even have make the journey down to the dear Old Briar-patch in broad daylight , he felt that that would n't do at all for little Miss Fuzzytail ; that he must avoid every possible chance of danger for her .
So Peter wait for a dark night , not too dark , you know , but a night when there be no moon to make great patch of light , but only the kindly little Stars look down and twinkle in the friendly way they have .
At last there be just such a night .
All the afternoon little Miss Fuzzytail go about in the Old Pasture say good-by to her friend and visit each one of her favorite little path and hiding-places , and I suspect that in each one she drop a tear or two , for you see she felt sure that she never would see them again , although Peter have promise that he would bring her back to the Old Pasture for a visit whenever she want to come .
At last it be time to start .
Peter lead the way .
Very big and brave and strong and important he felt , and very timid and frighten felt little Miss Fuzzytail , hop after him close at his heel .
You see , she felt that she be go out into the Great World , of which she know nothing at all .
`` Oh , Peter , '' she whisper , `` suppose we should meet Reddy Fox !
I would n't know where to run or hide . ''

I have fool Reddy so many time that I 'm not afraid of him . ''
Never in all his life have Peter be so watchful and careful .
That be because he felt his re-sponsi-bil-ity .
Every few jump he would stop to sit up and look and listen .
Then little Miss Fuzzytail would nestle up close to him , and Peter 's heart would swell with happiness , and he would feel , oh , so proud and important .
Once they hear the sharp bark of Reddy Fox , but it be a long way off , and Peter smile , for he know that Reddy be hunt on the edge of the Green Forest .
Once a dim shadow sweep across the meadow grass ahead of them .
Peter drop flat in the grass and keep perfectly still , and little Miss Fuzzytail do just a he do , a she have promise she would .
`` Wha -- what be it ? ''
she whisper .
`` I think it be Hooty the Owl , '' Peter whisper back , `` but he do n't see u . ''
After what seem like a long , long time they hear Hooty 's fierce hunting call , but it come from way back of them on the edge of the Old Pasture .
Peter hop to his foot .
`` Come on , '' say he .
`` There 's nothing to fear from him now . ''
So slowly and watchfully Peter lead the way down across the Green Meadows while the little Stars look down and twinkle in the most friendly way , and just a jolly , round , red Mr. Sun start to kick off his bedclothes behind the Purple Hills they reach the dear Old Briar - patch .
`` Here we be ! ''
cry Peter .
`` Oh , I 'm so glad ! ''

CHAPTER XXII SAMMY JAY BECOMES CURIOUS Learn all you can about others , but keep your own affair to yourself .
Peter Rabbit .
Of course it be Sammy Jay who first find out that Peter Rabbit be back in the dear Old Briar-patch .
Sammy take it into his head to fly over there the very morning of Peter 's home-coming .
Indeed , little Miss Fuzzytail have n't have time to half see the clear Old Briar-patch which , you know , be to be her new home , when Peter saw Sammy Jay come .

They want to keep by themselves for a little while and just be happy with each other .

Of course Sammy Jay saw him right away , and of course Sammy be very much surprise .
`` Hello , Peter Rabbit !
Where 'd you come from ? ''
he shout , a he settle himself comfortably in a little poplar-tree grow on the edge of the Old Briar-patch .

Sammy chuckle , for he dearly love to tease Peter and make him angry .
Then the imp of mischief , who seem always to live just under that smart cap of Sammy 's , prompt him to ask : `` Did you come home alone ? ''
Now Peter could n't say `` yes '' for that would be an untruth , and whatever fault Peter may have , he be at least truthful .

Peter Rabbit 's married ! ''

Peter Rabbit .

What do you suppose he mean ?

`` What do that funny little Meadow Mouse have to say ? ''

Peter tell her and then add , `` But I do n't believe we have anything to fear from Old Man Coyote .

`` But I do n't know that he be mine ! ''
reply little Mrs. Peter , and the way she say it make Peter look at her anxiously .
`` I believe Danny Meadow Mouse be right , '' she continue , `` Oh , Peter , you will watch out , wo n't you ? ''
And Peter promise her that he would .
CHAPTER XXV PETER RABBIT 'S HEEDLESSNESS Heedlessness be just the twin of thoughtlessness , you know , And where you find them both at once , there trouble 's sure to grow .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit do n't mean to be heedless .
No , indeed !
Oh , my , no !
Peter think so much of Mrs. Peter , he mean to be so thoughtful that she never would have a thing to worry about .
But Peter be heedless .
He always be heedless .
This be the bad of a bad habit -- you can try to let go of it , but it wo n't let go of you .
So it be with Peter .
He have be heedless so long that now he actually do n't know when he be heedless .
When there be nobody but himself to think about , and no one to worry about him , his heedlessness do n't so much matter .
If anything have happen to him then , there would have be no one to suffer .
But now all this be change .
You see , there be little Mrs. Peter .
At first Peter have be perfectly content to stay with her in the dear Old Briar - patch .

Little Mrs. Peter have be delight with everything , and not once have she complain of be homesick for the Old Pasture .
But after a little while Peter begin to get uneasy .
You see in the day before Old Man Coyote have come to live on the Green Meadows , Peter have come and go about a he please .
Of course he have have to watch out for Granny and Reddy Fox , but he have have to watch out for them ever since he be a baby , so he do n't fear them very much in spite of their smartness .
He felt quite as smart a they and perhaps a little bit smarter .
Anyway , they never have catch him , and he do n't believe they ever would .
So he have come and go a he please , and poke his nose into everybody 's business , and gossip with everybody .
Of course it be quite natural that Peter should want to call on all his old friend and visit the Green Forest , the Old Orchard , the Laughing Brook , and the Smiling Pool .
Probably Mrs. Peter would n't have worry very much if it have n't be for the warning leave by Danny Meadow Mouse .
Danny have say that Old Man Coyote be more to be fear than all the Hawk family and all the Fox family together , because he be smarter and slyer than any of them .
At first Peter have look very serious , but after Danny have go back to his own home Peter have laugh at Danny for be so afraid , and he begin to go far and farther away from the safe Old Briar-patch .

`` So we be until I have pay my debt to you .

`` But do n't forget that I always pay my debt , Peter Rabbit . ''
CHAPTER XXVI PETER RABBIT LISTENS TO MRS. PETER Safety first be a wise rule for those who would live long .
Peter Rabbit .
Peter Rabbit be glad enough to get back to the dear Old Briar-patch after his narrow escape from Old Man Coyote by dodge into Jimmy Skunk 's old house halfway up the hill .

Peter Rabbit .

CHAPTER XXVIII NEWS FROM THE OLD BRIAR-PATCH To use your eye be very wise And much to be commend ; But never see what can not be For such a you intend .
Peter Rabbit .
Jenny Wren be a busybody .

She be so small and spry that it be hard work to keep track of her , and she pop out at the most unexpected time and place .

CHAPTER XXIX JIMMY SKUNK VISITS PETER RABBIT It 's hard to keep a secret which you fairly ache to tell ; So not to know such secret be often quite as well .
Peter Rabbit .

CHAPTER XXX REDDY FOX LEARNS THE SECRET Nothing that you ever do , Nothing good or nothing bad , But have effect on other folk -- Gives them pain or make them glad .
Peter Rabbit .

CHAPTER XXXI BLACKY THE CROW HAS SHARP EYES Mischief always wait to greet Idle hand and idle foot .
Peter Rabbit .
That be what a lot of people say about Blacky the Crow .

Thus the good Blacky do be n't see , while the bad be , and so he have grow to have a reputation blacker than the coat he wear .
But this do n't worry Blacky the Crow .
No , Sir , it do n't worry him a bit .

CHAPTER XXXII PETER RABBIT 'S NURSERY With home , the home you call your own , It really do n't matter where , There be no place , in all the world , That ever will or can compare .
Peter Rabbit .

Right away the Old Briar - patch become the most interesting place on the Green Meadows to all the little people who live there and in the near-by Green Forest .
